----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math
from pathlib import Path
from time import time

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND = DATA / "candles"
DEBUG_DIR = DATA / "debug" / "bridge"
DEBUG_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Garde-fous (modifiables par env)
ENTRY_FROM_HOLD = int(os.environ.get("ENTRY_FROM_HOLD", "0"))
MIN_STRENGTH    = float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH", "7"))
PB_TH           = float(os.environ.get("PB_TH", "0.65"))
PS_TH           = float(os.environ.get("PS_TH", "0.65"))
ATR_PER         = int(os.environ.get("ATR_PER", "14"))
ATR_MIN_PCT     = float(os.environ.get("ATR_MIN_PCT", "0.10"))   # % mini en 1m
EMA_VETO        = int(os.environ.get("EMA_VETO", "0"))           # 0=off
COOLDOWN_S      = int(os.environ.get("COOLDOWN_S", "120"))
RISK_PCT        = float(os.environ.get("RISK_PCT", "0.01"))
LEVERAGE        = float(os.environ.get("LEVERAGE", "5"))
SLxATR          = float(os.environ.get("SLxATR", "1.0"))
TpxATR          = float(os.environ.get("TpxATR", "1.5"))
FORCE_ENTRY     = int(os.environ.get("FORCE_ENTRY", "0"))

SIG = DATA / "signals.json"
POS = DATA / "paper" / "positions.json"
BAL = DATA / "paper" / "balance.json"

def jload(p: Path, dflt):
    try:
        return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception:
        return dflt

def dump_json(p: Path, obj):
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_closed_1m(sym: str):
    """Retourne close de la dernière bougie 1m **clôturée**.
    Règle simple: on prend l'avant-dernière ligne."""
    f = CAND / "1m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        if len(rows) >= 2:
            return float(rows[-2][4])  # close
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None

def atr_1m_pct(sym: str, n=ATR_PER):
    f = CAND / "1m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        rows = rows[-(n+1):]
        if len(rows) < n+1: 
            return None
        trs = []
        prev_close = float(rows[0][4])
        for r in rows[1:]:
            h,l,c = float(r[1]), float(r[2]), float(r[4])
            tr = max(h-l, abs(h-prev_close), abs(l-prev_close))
            trs.append(tr); prev_close = c
        atr = sum(trs)/len(trs)
        last_close = float(rows[-1][4])
        return 100.0*atr/last_close
    except Exception:
        return None

def ema(series, span):
    k = 2/(span+1)
    e = series[0]
    for x in series[1:]:
        e = x*k + e*(1-k)
    return e

def ema_veto(side: str, sym: str):
    if not EMA_VETO: 
        return False
    f = CAND / "5m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        closes = [float(r[4]) for r in rows][-50:]
        if len(closes) < 22: 
            return False
        e9  = ema(closes, 9)
        e21 = ema(closes, 21)
        return (side=="buy"  and e9<e21) or (side=="sell" and e9>e21)
    except Exception:
        return False

def cooldown_block(sym: str):
    """Anti double entrée: refuse si position 'open' existe récente."""
    pos = jload(POS, [])
    now = time()
    for p in pos:
        if p.get("symbol")==sym and str(p.get("status","")).lower().startswith("open"):
            # si la position a été ouverte il y a moins de COOLDOWN_S on bloque
            ts = p.get("ts_open") or 0
            try:
                if now - float(ts) < COOLDOWN_S: 
                    return True
            except Exception:
                return True
    return False

def decide(sig: dict):
    sym  = sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin")
    ctx  = (sig.get("ctx") or sig.get("context") or "").lower()
    act  = (sig.get("action") or "").lower()
    side = (sig.get("side") or "").lower()

    # mapping context -> side si besoin
    if side not in ("buy","sell"):
        if ctx=="buy" or ctx=="bullish": side="buy"
        elif ctx=="sell" or ctx=="bearish": side="sell"
        else: side="none"

    strength = float(sig.get("strength") or sig.get("str") or 0)
    pb = float(sig.get("pb", 0)); ps = float(sig.get("ps", 0))

    # filtre A/B pour convertir hold->enter
    will_enter = act in ("enter_long","enter_short")
    if not will_enter and ENTRY_FROM_HOLD:
        if act in ("hold_long","hold_short"):
            will_enter = True
            side = "buy" if "long" in act else "sell"

    # gardes-fous
    reason = []
    if not will_enter and not FORCE_ENTRY:
        return "gate_action_none", None

    if not FORCE_ENTRY:
        if strength < MIN_STRENGTH or (pb < PB_TH and ps < PS_TH):
            return "gate_strength_pb_ps", None

        atrp = atr_1m_pct(sym)
        if atrp is None or atrp < ATR_MIN_PCT:
            return "gate_atr_too_small", None

        if ema_veto(side, sym):
            return "gate_ema_veto", None

        if cooldown_block(sym):
            return "gate_cooldown", None

    # prix d'entrée
    px = last_closed_1m(sym)
    if px is None:
        if FORCE_ENTRY:
            return "skip_no_price_force", {"sym":sym, "side":side, "action":"hold_"+("long" if side=="buy" else "short"),
                                           "price": None, "sl": None, "tp": None, "size": 0, "margin": 0}
        return "gate_no_px_or_atr", None

    # ATR pour SL/TP (recalc au besoin)
    atrp = atr_1m_pct(sym) or 0.0
    atr_abs = px * (atrp/100.0)
    sl = px - SLxATR*atr_abs if side=="buy" else px + SLxATR*atr_abs
    tp = px + TpxATR*atr_abs if side=="buy" else px - TpxATR*atr_abs

    # sizing risque fixe
    bal = float(jload(BAL, {"cash":200}).get("cash", 200))
    risk_amt = max(0.0, bal*RISK_PCT)
    stop_dist = abs(px - sl)
    qty = 0.0 if stop_dist<=0 else risk_amt/stop_dist
    # marge
    notionnel = qty*px
    margin = notionnel/LEVERAGE if LEVERAGE>0 else notionnel

    # arrondis simples
    def rnd(x, step): 
        try: 
            return math.floor(x/step)*step
        except Exception:
            return x
    qty = rnd(qty, 1e-3)
    px  = round(px, 6); sl = round(sl, 6); tp = round(tp, 6)
    margin = round(margin, 2)

    out = {"sym": sym, "side": side, "action": "enter_"+("long" if side=="buy" else "short"),
           "price": px, "sl": sl, "tp": tp, "size": qty, "margin": margin}

    # log par coin
    log = {
        "ctx": ctx, "str": strength, "pb": pb, "ps": ps, "atr%": atrp,
        "side": side, "px": px, "sl": sl, "tp": tp, "qty": qty, "margin": margin
    }
    (DEBUG_DIR/f"{sym}.log").write_text(json.dumps(log, indent=2))
    return "ENTRY", out

def main():
    sigs = jload(SIG, [])
    items = []
    gates = {"ENTRY":0, "gate_strength_pb_ps":0, "gate_atr_too_small":0,
             "gate_ema_veto":0, "gate_cooldown":0, "gate_no_px_or_atr":0,
             "gate_action_none":0, "skip_no_price_force":0}
    for s in sigs:
        decision, out = decide(s)
        gates[decision] = gates.get(decision,0)+1
        if out: 
            items.append(out)
        else:
            # garder le signal original si pas d'entrée, mais renseigner champs par défaut
            s.setdefault("price", None); s.setdefault("sl", None)
            s.setdefault("tp", None);    s.setdefault("size", 0)
            s.setdefault("margin", 0)
            items.append({"sym": s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin"),
                          "side": s.get("side") or "none",
                          "action": s.get("action") or "none",
                          "price": s.get("price"), "sl": s.get("sl"),
                          "tp": s.get("tp"), "size": s.get("size"), "margin": s.get("margin")})

    dump_json(SIG, items)

    # petite synthèse stdout
    print(f"[bridge] wrote {SIG} items={len(items)}",
          *[f"{k}={v}" for k,v in gates.items() if v], sep=" ")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import os, json, time, math, traceback
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
CAND.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"1m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"3m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"5m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

TOP = json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())
A   = json.loads((DATA/"analyse_A_out.json").read_text()) if (DATA/"analyse_A_out.json").exists() else {}

# --- Sélection: seulement ctx != "none" ---
symbols = [s for s in (TOP.get("symbols") or []) if (A.get(s,{}).get("ctx") or "none") != "none"]

# --- Exchange ccxt ---
import ccxt
EXCHANGE = os.getenv("EXCHANGE", TOP.get("exchange") or "xt").lower()
def build_ex():
    klass = getattr(ccxt, EXCHANGE)
    return klass({"enableRateLimit": True, "timeout": 20000})

ex = build_ex()

# --- Utilitaires OHLCV ---
def fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, limit=600):
    # returns list[[ts,open,high,low,close,vol], ...], ts ms
    try:
        return ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym.replace("_","/"), timeframe=tf, limit=limit) or []
    except Exception:
        return []

def save_json(p, arr):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr))

def last_complete(arr, tf_sec):
    if not arr: return []
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    return arr[:-1] if now - arr[-1][0] < tf_sec*1000 else arr

def resample_3m_from_1m(arr1):
    out=[]
    bucket=None
    for k in arr1:
        ts,o,h,l,c,v = k
        # début de bucket 3m aligné
        b = ts - (ts % (3*60*1000))
        if (bucket is None) or (b!=bucket[0]):
            # push précédent
            if bucket is not None: out.append(bucket)
            bucket = [b,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            bucket[2] = max(bucket[2], h)
            bucket[3] = min(bucket[3], l)
            bucket[4] = c
            bucket[5] += v
    if bucket is not None: out.append(bucket)
    return out

# --- Worker par symbole ---
RATE_MS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_RATE_MS", "220"))
def work(sym):
    t0=time.time()
    try:
        m1 = fetch_ohlcv(sym, "1m", 900)
        m5 = fetch_ohlcv(sym, "5m", 600)
        m1 = last_complete(m1, 60)
        m5 = last_complete(m5, 300)
        m3 = resample_3m_from_1m(m1)
        save_json(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json", m1)
        save_json(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json", m5)
        save_json(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json", m3)
        ok = (len(m1)>0 and len(m3)>0 and len(m5)>0)
        dt = int((time.time()-t0)*1000)
        return (sym, ok, dt, len(m1), len(m3), len(m5))
    except Exception as e:
        return (sym, False, -1, 0, 0, 0)
    finally:
        # petit rate-limit inter-threads
        time.sleep(RATE_MS/1000.0)

WORKERS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_WORKERS", "8"))
results=[]
with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS) as pool:
    futs=[pool.submit(work, s) for s in symbols]
    for f in as_completed(futs):
        results.append(f.result())

# Log court sur stdout
for sym,ok,dt,n1,n3,n5 in sorted(results):
    print(f"{sym:12s} ok={int(ok)}  {dt:4d}ms  1m={n1:4d} 3m={n3:4d} 5m={n5:4d}")
print(f"done ctx-syms={len(symbols)}")

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
export DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
export TRIGGER_B=ctx
export A_CMD='python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py {sym}'
export B_CMD='python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin_debug.py {sym}'
while :; do
  now_min=$(date -u +%M); m=$((10#$now_min))
  due5=$(( m % 5 == 0 )); due15=$(( m % 15 == 0 )); due30=$(( m % 30 == 0 ))
  echo "=== tick $(date -u +%FT%TZ) m=$m (5:$due5 15:$due15 30:$due30) ==="
  # fetch A seulement quand TF due
  if (( due5 || due15 || due30 )); then
    python3 /opt/scalp/tools/fetch_A_then_B.py

    # pas d’update A, mais laisse B tourner via ctx existant
    python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_top_bridge.py || true
  fi
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/signals_bridge_enforce.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, time, asyncio, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# --------- Params ---------
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"
TOP_N = int(os.getenv("TOP_N","30"))
SHORTLIST_K = int(os.getenv("SHORTLIST_K","80"))
MIN_QV = float(os.getenv("MIN_QV","1000000"))
MAX_SP = float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS","60"))   # 0.60%
USE_DEPTH = os.getenv("USE_DEPTH","0")=="1"
MIN_DEPTH = float(os.getenv("MIN_DEPTH_USD","200000"))
BAND_BPS = int(os.getenv("DEPTH_BAND_BPS","50"))  # ±0.5%

# pondérations
W_VOL24 = 0.30
W_TURN  = 0.30
W_VOLA  = 0.20
W_DEPTH = 0.15
W_SP    = -0.05

# exécution
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("TOP_WORKERS","8"))
RATE_LIMIT_MS = int(os.getenv("TOP_RATE_LIMIT_MS","220"))
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"

def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
def clamp(x,a,b): return a if x<a else b if x>b else x
def winsor(vals, p=0.01):
    if not vals: return vals
    s=sorted(vals); n=len(s)
    lo=s[max(0,int(n*p)-1)]; hi=s[min(n-1,int(n*(1-p)))]
    return [min(max(v,lo),hi) for v in vals]
def rnorm(d):
    if not d: return {}
    it=sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1]); n=max(1,len(it)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(it)}
def ema(vals, p):
    if not vals: return 0.0
    a=2/(p+1); e=float(vals[0])
    for v in vals[1:]: e=a*float(v)+(1-a)*e
    return float(e)

# ---------- async throttle ----------
_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(max(1, 1000//RATE_LIMIT_MS))
async def throttled(loop, fn, *a, **k):
    async with _sem:
        t0=time.time()
        try: res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: fn(*a, **k))
        except Exception: res=None
        dt=time.time()-t0
        sl=max(0.0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - dt)
        if sl: await asyncio.sleep(sl)
        return res

def load_seed():
    try:
        j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
        out=[x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
        return out if out else ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]
    except:
        return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # ---- 1) bulk tickers
    tickers={}
    try: tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): continue
        if b in BAD_BASES: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        # volume quote avec fallback "info"
        qv = t.get("quoteVolume")
        if not qv:
            info=t.get("info",{}); qv = info.get("quoteVolume") or info.get("quoteVolume24h") or 0.0
        qv=float(qv or 0.0)
        bid,ask=t.get("bid"),t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: continue
        mid=0.5*(bid+ask)
        sp=clamp(10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid, 0.0, 200.0)
        if qv<MIN_QV or sp>MAX_SP: continue
        pool.append({"sym":s,"flat":s.replace('/','').replace(':',''),"qv":qv,"sp":sp})

    # tri volume puis shortlist K
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x["qv"], reverse=True)
    short = pool[:max(TOP_N, SHORTLIST_K)]

    # ---- 2) métriques pour shortlist
    async def gather_metrics():
        loop=asyncio.get_running_loop()
        # OHLCV 1h pour 7j
        async def one(sym):
            o1h = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1h", 24*7+1, FUT)
            turn=0.0; rets=[]
            if isinstance(o1h,list) and len(o1h)>10:
                prev=o1h[0][4]
                for _,_,_,_,c,v in o1h[1:]:
                    turn += float(v)*float(c)
                    if prev>0 and c>0: rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
                    prev=c
            turn_ema = ema([turn/(24*7)], 1) if turn>0 else 0.0  # lissé light
            vola = float(stats.pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0
            # Depth optionnel
            d_q=0.0
            if USE_DEPTH:
                ob = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_order_book, sym, 100, FUT)
                if ob and ob.get("bids") and ob.get("asks"):
                    bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
                    lo,hi = mid*(1-BAND_BPS/10000.0), mid*(1+BAND_BPS/10000.0)
                    for p,a in ob["bids"]:
                        if p<lo: break
                        d_q += p*a
                    for p,a in ob["asks"]:
                        if p>hi: break
                        d_q += p*a
            return turn_ema, vola, d_q
        tasks=[one(e["sym"]) for e in short]
        res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        for e,(turn,vola,depth) in zip(short,res):
            if isinstance(turn, Exception): turn=0.0; vola=0.0; depth=0.0
            e["turn"]=float(turn); e["vola"]=float(vola); e["depth"]=float(depth)
    asyncio.run(gather_metrics())

    # gate depth si activé
    if USE_DEPTH:
        short=[e for e in short if e["depth"]>=MIN_DEPTH]

    # ---- 3) scoring robuste
    # log-scale + winsor
    vmap={e["sym"]: math.log1p(v) for e,v in zip(short, winsor([x["qv"] for x in short],0.01))}
    tmap={e["sym"]: math.log1p(v) for e,v in zip(short, winsor([x["turn"] for x in short],0.01))}
    volmap={e["sym"]: x["vola"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}
    dmap={e["sym"]: x["depth"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}
    smap={e["sym"]: x["sp"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}

    Rv, Rt, Rvol, Rd, Rs = map(rnorm, (vmap,tmap,volmap,dmap,smap))

    score={}
    for e in short:
        s=e["sym"]
        score[s] = (
            W_VOL24*Rv.get(s,0.0) + W_TURN*Rt.get(s,0.0) + W_VOLA*Rvol.get(s,0.0)
            + W_DEPTH*Rd.get(s,0.0) + W_SP*Rs.get(s,0.0)
        )
        e["score"]=round(float(score[s]),6)

    short.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)

    # compose sortie avec noyau fixe en tête puis complétion
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    # Ajoute stats si seed dans shortlist
    idx={e["flat"]: e for e in short}
    for s in seeds:
        e=idx.get(s, None)
        if e:
            details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": e["score"],
                            "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "turnover7d_ema": e["turn"],
                            "volatility7d": e["vola"], "depth_quote_band": e["depth"],
                            "spread_bps": e["sp"]})
        else:
            details.append({"symbol": s, "score": 1.0})

    for e in short:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set: continue
        out.append(e["flat"]); seed_set.add(e["flat"])
        details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": e["score"],
                        "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "turnover7d_ema": e["turn"],
                        "volatility7d": e["vola"], "depth_quote_band": e["depth"],
                        "spread_bps": e["sp"]})
        if len(out)>=TOP_N: break

    meta={"generated_at": now_iso(), "source":"futures-tickers-shortlist+ranked-light", "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE}
    (TOP).write_text(json.dumps({**meta,"symbols": out[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    (RANK).write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at": meta["generated_at"], "n": len(out[:TOP_N]), "items": details[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))

    print(f"[top-light] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} short={len(short)} "
          f"use_depth={int(USE_DEPTH)} top={len(out[:TOP_N])}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); OUT = DATA/"candles"

def main():
    tfs=[]; syms=[]; i=1
    while i < len(sys.argv):
        if sys.argv[i]=="--tfs": i+=1; tfs=sys.argv[i].split(",")
        elif sys.argv[i]=="--symbols": i+=1; syms=sys.argv[i].split(",")
        i+=1
    tfs=[x.strip() for x in tfs if x.strip()]
    syms=[to_flat(x) for x in syms if x.strip()]
    ok=err=0
    for s in syms:
        for tf in tfs:
            p=OUT/tf/f"{s}.json"; p.parent.mkdir(parents=True,exist_ok=True)
            if not p.exists(): p.write_text("[]")
            arr=json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
            if arr: print(f"[ok]  {s:<12} tf={tf:<4} bars={len(arr):>3}"); ok+=1
            else:   print(f"[x]   {s:<12} tf=None err=missing"); err+=1
    print(f"[fetch] done  tfs={','.join(tfs)}  syms={len(syms)}  ok={ok}  err={err}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
SIGF = DATA/"signals.json"
POSF = DATA/"paper/positions.json"
BALF = DATA/"paper/balance.json"
AOUT = DATA/"analysis_a"
CAND = DATA/"candles"

FRESH_S = int(os.environ.get("FRESH_S", "300"))          # fraicheur max OHLCV
MIN_STRENGTH = float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH", "1"))# seuil de force
N = int(os.environ.get("N", "20"))                       # nb de signaux à inspecter
LOG = DATA/"logs"/"paper_debug.log"

def jload(p, default):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return default

def age_ok(p:Path) -> bool:
    try: return (time.time() - p.stat().st_mtime) <= FRESH_S
    except: return False

def ctx_of(sym):
    j = jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json", {})
    return str(j.get("context","none")).lower()

def is_open(sym):
    pos = jload(POSF, [])
    for p in pos:
        if str(p.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running") and (p.get("symbol") == sym or p.get("sym")==sym):
            return True
    return False

def budget():
    b = jload(BALF, {})
    for k in ("balance","equity","cash","budget"):
        if k in b: 
            try: return float(b[k])
            except: pass
    return float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))

def evaluate(sig):
    sym  = sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin") or "?"
    side = (sig.get("side") or sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    action = (sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    strength = float(sig.get("strength") or 0)
    margin = float(sig.get("margin") or sig.get("margin_usd") or sig.get("size_usd") or 0)
    # règles
    if side == "none":         return "side_none"
    if action in ("hold_long","hold_short","idle","wait"): 
        return f"action_{action}"
    if is_open(sym):           return "already_open"
    if budget() < margin:      return f"insufficient_budget({margin:.2f}>{budget():.2f})"
    if strength < MIN_STRENGTH:return f"weak_strength({strength:.2f}<{MIN_STRENGTH:.2f})"
    # fraicheur OHLCV
    fresh = all([
        age_ok(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"),
        age_ok(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json") or (CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        age_ok(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json"),
    ])
    if not fresh:              return "stale_ohlcv"
    # contexte A informatif
    ctx = ctx_of(sym)
    if ctx == "none":          return "ctx_none"
    return "entry_ok_if_router_accepts"  # rien de bloquant côté debug

def hhmm(ts):
    if isinstance(ts,(int,float)):
        ts = int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        try: return datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M")
        except: return "--:--"
    return "--:--"

def main():
    LOG.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    sigs = jload(SIGF, [])
    if isinstance(sigs, dict):
        sigs = sigs.get("items") or sigs.get("signals") or []
    tail = sigs[-N:]
    lines=[]
    lines.append(f"== paper_debug @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ')} ==")
    lines.append(f"balance={budget():.2f}  positions_open={jload(POSF,[])}")
    for s in tail:
        sym = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin") or "?"
        side = s.get("side") or s.get("action") or "-"
        m = float(s.get("margin") or s.get("margin_usd") or s.get("size_usd") or 0)
        st = evaluate(s)
        lines.append(f"{hhmm(s.get('ts') or s.get('time') or s.get('timestamp'))}  {sym:<10} {side:<6} margin={m:>7.2f}  -> {st}")
    out = "\n".join(lines)+"\n"
    print(out, end="")
    with open(LOG, "a") as f: f.write(out)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
try:
    from colorama import init as _cinit, Fore, Style
    _cinit(); G=Fore.GREEN; Y=Fore.YELLOW; R=Fore.RED; C=Fore.CYAN; M=Fore.MAGENTA; B=Fore.BLUE; X=Style.RESET_ALL
except Exception:
    class _N: pass
    G=Y=R=C=M=B=X=_N()

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND= DATA/"candles"; AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"; PAPR=DATA/"paper"; SIGF=DATA/"signals.json"; TOPF=DATA/"top.json"
REFRESH=int(os.environ.get("REFRESH","10"))
BUDGET = float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))

def jload(p, default=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return default

def nowz(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc)

def strip_usdt(s): return s.replace("USDT","")

def fmt_i10(v):  # valeur *10 tronquée à 1 chiffre
    try:
        n = int(float(v)*10)
        return f"{n:>2d}"
    except: return " -"

def tick(p):
    try: age= int(time.time() - Path(p).stat().st_mtime)
    except: return f"{R}❌{X}"
    return f"{G}✅{X}" if age<=180 else f"{Y}⏳{X}"

def load_top():
    t=jload(TOPF,{})
    syms=t.get("symbols") or []
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str)]

def read_A(sym):
    j=jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json",{})
    S=float(j.get("S") or j.get("score") or 0)
    pb=float(j.get("pb") or 0); pH=float(j.get("pH") or 0); ps=float(j.get("ps") or 0)
    ctx=(j.get("context") or "none").lower()
    return S,pb,pH,ps,ctx

def a_rows():
    syms=load_top()
    score=[]
    for s in syms:
        S,pb,pH,ps,ctx=read_A(s)
        score.append((S,s,ctx))
    score.sort()
    best2=[score[-1][1], score[-2][1]] if len(score)>=2 else [s for _,s,_ in score][-2:]
    worst2=[score[0][1], score[1][1]] if len(score)>=2 else [s for _,s,_ in score][:2]
    rows=[]
    keep=[]
    for must in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if must in syms: keep.append(must)
    for s in best2+worst2:
        if s not in keep: keep.append(s)
    for s in keep:
        S,pb,pH,ps,ctx=read_A(s)
        rows.append((s,S,pb,pH,ps,ctx))
    return rows, score

def last_signals(n=5):
    js=jload(SIGF,[])
    if isinstance(js,dict): js=js.get("items") or js.get("signals") or []
    return list(js)[-n:]

def pos_open():
    p=jload(PAPR/"positions.json",[])
    return [x for x in p if str(x.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running")]

def pnl_history():
    return jload(PAPR/"history.json",[])

def header():
    opened=pos_open()
    float_pnl=sum(float(p.get("pnl") or p.get("pnl_usd") or 0) for p in opened)
    realized=sum(float(h.get("pnl") or h.get("pnl_usd") or 0) for h in pnl_history())
    line1=f"{C}== SCALP DASHBOARD v2 =={X}  @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}Z"
    line2=f"Paper Budget: {BUDGET:.2f} USDT   Realized: {M}{realized:.2f}{X}   Floating: {C}{float_pnl:.2f}{X}"
    proc=f"Données:{tick(CAND/'5m')}  Analyse A:{tick(AOUT)}  Signaux:{tick(SIGF)}  Paper:{tick(PAPR/'positions.json')}"
    return "\n".join((line1,line2,proc))

def table_A():
    rows, score = a_rows()
    # bloc buy/sell/hold top 5
    byctx={"buy":[],"sell":[],"hold":[]}
    for S,sym,ctx in sorted(((S,s,c) for S,s,c in score), reverse=True):
        if ctx in byctx and len(byctx[ctx])<5: byctx[ctx].append(strip_usdt(sym))
    # compte par contexte
    from collections import Counter
    cnt=Counter(c for _,_,c in score)
    # rendu
    out=[]
    out.append(f"{B}ANALYSE A{X}  (valeurs x10 tronquées)")
    out.append(f"{'COIN':<10} {'S':>2} {'pb':>2} {'pH':>2} {'ps':>2}  {'CTX':<6}")
    for s,S,pb,pH,ps,ctx in rows:
        out.append(f"{strip_usdt(s):<10} {fmt_i10(S):>2} {fmt_i10(pb):>2} {fmt_i10(pH):>2} {fmt_i10(ps):>2}  {ctx:<6}")
    out.append("")
    out.append(f"Buy:  {', '.join(byctx['buy']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Sell: {', '.join(byctx['sell']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Hold: {', '.join(byctx['hold']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Ave  buy={cnt.get('buy',0)}  hold={cnt.get('hold',0)}  sell={cnt.get('sell',0)}  none={cnt.get('none',0)}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_signals():
    items=last_signals(5); openmap={ (p.get('symbol') or p.get('sym')):'IN' for p in pos_open() }
    out=[f"{B}DERNIERS SIGNAUX{X} (5)", f"{'hh:mm':<6} {'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'status':<7} {'margin$':>8}"]
    for s in items:
        ts=s.get("ts") or s.get("time") or s.get("timestamp") or 0
        if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        hhmm=datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M") if ts else "--:--"
        coin=s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin") or "-"
        side=s.get("side") or s.get("action") or "-"
        st = openmap.get(coin,"WAIT")
        margin = s.get("margin") or s.get("margin_usd") or s.get("size_usd") or 0
        out.append(f"{hhmm:<6} {strip_usdt(coin):<8} {side:<6} {st:<7} {float(margin):>8.2f}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_positions():
    pp=pos_open()
    out=[f"{B}POSITIONS OUVERTES{X}", f"{'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'qty':>7} {'entry':>9} {'last':>9} {'PnL$':>8}"]
    if not pp: out.append("(aucune)"); return "\n".join(out)
    for p in pp:
        coin=strip_usdt(p.get("symbol") or p.get("sym") or "-")
        side=p.get("side") or "-"
        qty =p.get("qty") or p.get("quantity") or 0
        entry=p.get("entry") or p.get("entry_price") or 0
        last =p.get("last") or p.get("mark_price") or p.get("price") or 0
        pnl  =p.get("pnl") or p.get("pnl_usd") or 0
        out.append(f"{coin:<8} {side:<6} {float(qty):>7.3g} {float(entry):>9.2f} {float(last):>9.2f} {float(pnl):>8.2f}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_history():
    hh=pnl_history()[-10:]
    out=[f"{B}HISTORIQUE PnL{X} (10)", f"{'hh:mm':<6} {'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'pnl$':>8}"]
    total=0.0
    for h in hh:
        ts=h.get("ts") or h.get("time") or h.get("timestamp") or 0
        if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        hhmm=datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M") if ts else "--:--"
        coin=strip_usdt(h.get("symbol") or h.get("sym") or "-")
        side=h.get("side") or "-"
        pnl=float(h.get("pnl") or h.get("pnl_usd") or 0); total+=pnl
        out.append(f"{hhmm:<6} {coin:<8} {side:<6} {pnl:>8.2f}")
    out.append(f"{M}TOTAL:{X} {total:.2f} USD")
    return "\n".join(out)

def clear(): print("\033[2J\033[H", end="")

def main():
    while True:
        clear()
        print(header()); print()
        print(table_A()); print()
        print(table_signals()); print()
        print(table_positions()); print()
        print(table_history()); print()
        print(f"(maj auto {REFRESH}s)  Ctrl-C pour quitter")
        time.sleep(REFRESH)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Construit candles 3m à partir des 1m (groupes de 3 bougies complètes)
import json, sys, math, time
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C = DATA/"candles"

def load_1m(sym):
    p = C/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return []
    arr = json.loads(p.read_text())
    # retire la bougie 1m incomplète
    now = int(time.time())
    if arr and now - arr[-1][0]//1000 < 60:
        arr = arr[:-1]
    return arr

def build_3m_from_1m(m1):
    out=[]; n=len(m1)//3*3
    for i in range(0, n, 3):
        g = m1[i:i+3]
        ts = g[0][0]  # premier ts du bloc
        o  = g[0][1]
        h  = max(x[2] for x in g)
        l  = min(x[3] for x in g)
        c  = g[-1][4]
        v  = sum(x[5] for x in g)
        out.append([ts, o, h, l, c, v])
    return out

def save_3m(sym, arr):
    p = C/"3m"/f"{sym}.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr))

def main():
    syms = [to_flat(s) for s in sys.argv[1:]]
    if not syms:
        # par défaut: top.json
        top = json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())
        syms = [to_flat(s) for s in top.get("symbols",[])]
    ok=err=0
    for s in syms:
        m1 = load_1m(s)
        if len(m1) < 3: print(f"[x] {s}: 1m insuffisant"); err+=1; continue
        m3 = build_3m_from_1m(m1)
        save_3m(s, m3)
        print(f"[ok] {s}: 3m={len(m3)}")
        ok+=1
    print(f"[build3m] ok={ok} err={err} syms={len(syms)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TOP=/opt/scalp/data/top.json
RANK=/opt/scalp/data/top_ranked.json
jq -e '.symbols|type=="array" and length>=5' "$TOP" >/dev/null

# fraîcheur < 3h

gen=$(date -u -d "$(jq -r .generated_at "$TOP")" +%s)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from ctx_logic_b import PosState, decide_signal
from indicators_tf import indicators_from_ohlcv

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND=DATA/"candles"
AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"          # fichiers par coin de A
BSTATE=DATA/"analysis_b_state"  # états par coin
BSTATE.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
BOUT=DATA/"signals_coin"        # signaux par coin
BOUT.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def jload(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def load_last_ohlcv(sym, tf):
    f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    j=jload(f,{}) or {}
    rows=j.get("data") or []
    if not rows: raise RuntimeError(f"missing candles: {f}")
    return rows[-200:]

def atrp5_from_ohlcv(sym):
    rows=load_last_ohlcv(sym, "5m")
    feats=indicators_from_ohlcv(rows)
    return float(feats.get("atr_pct", 0.0))

def load_a(sym):
    f = AOUT/f"{sym}.json"
    j = jload(f,{})
    if not j: raise RuntimeError(f"missing A output: {f}")
    return j

def load_state(sym):
    f=BSTATE/f"{sym}.json"
    j=jload(f,{})
    if not j: return PosState()
    try: return PosState(**{k:j.get(k) for k in ("pos","cooldown","last_ctx")})
    except: return PosState()

def save_state(sym, st: PosState):
    (BSTATE/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(st.__dict__, indent=2))

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: run_analysis_b_coin.py SYMBOL", file=sys.stderr); return 2
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    try:
        a = load_a(sym)
        atr5 = atrp5_from_ohlcv(sym)
        feats = dict(atrp5=atr5)
        st = load_state(sym)
        res = decide_signal(a, feats, st)
        save_state(sym, res["new_state"])
        out = dict(symbol=sym, side=res["side"], action=res["action"],
                   strength=int(res["strength"]), reason=res["reason"])
        (BOUT/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
        print(json.dumps(out))
        return 0
    except Exception as e:
        (BOUT/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(
            dict(symbol=sym, side="none", action="error", strength=0, reason=str(e)), indent=2))
        return 1

if __name__=="__main__":
    import sys as _; _.exit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, re, shutil
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP =DATA/"top.json"
RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"
OUT =DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LOG =Path("/opt/scalp/logs/top_rebuild.log")

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def ok(x): return "✅" if x else "❌"
def ts():  return datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ")

def per_tf_from_reason(reason:str):
    d={}
    if not isinstance(reason,str): return d
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        m=re.search(rf"['\"]{tf}['\"]\s*:\s*(-?\d+\.?\d*)", reason)
        if m: d[tf]=float(m.group(1))
    return d

def i10(x): 
    try: return int(round(float(x)))
    except: return 0

def row(sym, rec):
    sym=sym.replace("USDT","")
    s_int = i10(10*(rec.get("S") or 0))
    pb_i  = i10(rec.get("pb_i", 10*(rec.get("pb") or 0)))
    ph_i  = i10(rec.get("pH_i", 10*(rec.get("pH") or 0)))
    ps_i  = i10(rec.get("ps_i", 10*(rec.get("ps") or 0)))
    ctx   = (rec.get("context") or "")[:4]
    ptf   = per_tf_from_reason(rec.get("reason",""))
    s5  = ptf.get("5m");  s15 = ptf.get("15m");  s30 = ptf.get("30m")
    s5  = f"{s5: .3f}" if s5  is not None else "   —  "
    s15 = f"{s15: .3f}" if s15 is not None else "   —  "
    s30 = f"{s30: .3f}" if s30 is not None else "   —  "
    return f"{sym:6s} {s_int:2d}  {pb_i:2d} {ph_i:2d} {ps_i:2d}  {ctx:4s}  {s5:>6} {s15:>6} {s30:>6}"

def pick_best_worst(allrec, exclude:set, k=2):
    items=[(k_,v) for k_,v in (allrec or {}).items() if isinstance(v,dict) and v.get("S") is not None and k_ not in exclude]
    best = sorted(items, key=lambda x: x[1]["S"], reverse=True)[:k]
    worst= sorted(items, key=lambda x: x[1]["S"])[:k]
    return best, worst

def main():
    print(f"== SCALP DASHBOARD @ {ts()} ==\n")
    # Top
    top=jload(TOP,{})
    syms=top.get("symbols") or []; src=top.get("source","?"); tss=top.get("generated_at","?")
    print("Top30")
    print(f"{ok(bool(syms))} ts={tss}  src={src}  N={len(syms)}")
    print(f"{ok(True)} OHLCV 5/15/30 ({len(syms)}/{len(syms)})")
    if len(syms)>=10:
        print("6->10:", ", ".join(s.replace("USDT","") for s in syms[5:10]))
    print()
    # Analyses
    out=jload(OUT,{}) or {}
    print("Analyses  (BTC, ETH, 2 best, 2 worst)")
    print("sym    s   pb pH ps  ctx   5m     15m    30m")
    for sym in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        print(row(sym, out.get(sym, {})))
    best, worst = pick_best_worst(out, {"BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"}, 2)
    for sym,rec in best+worst:
        print(row(sym, rec))
    print("\nInputs & logs")
    for p in [TOP, RANK, DATA/'signals.json', DATA/'positions.json', LOG]:
        print(f"{ok(Path(p).exists())} {p}")
    print("\nRésultat global:", ok(True))

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import re, shutil

ROOT = Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
candidates = [p for p in ROOT.rglob("*.py") if "analysis_a" in p.name or p.name in ("run_analysis_a_coin.py","run_analysis_a_top_bridge.py")]

# remplace tous les motifs last.json vers TF/SYM.json
REGEXES = [
    re.compile(r'candles/\s*\{\s*sym\s*\}\s*/\s*\{\s*tf\s*\}\s*/\s*last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'candles/\w+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'candles/[^\'"]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'(/candles/)[^/]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
]

def patch_text(s):
    changed=False
    for rx in REGEXES:
        if rx.search(s):
            s = rx.sub('candles/{tf}/{sym}.json', s)
            changed=True
    # quelques Path(...)/sym/tf/"last.json"
    s2 = re.sub(r'(?i)Path\([^)]*\)\s*/\s*sym\s*/\s*tf\s*/\s*"last\.json"', 'Path(DATA)/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"', s)
    if s2!=s: changed=True; s=s2
    return s, changed

for p in candidates:
    txt = p.read_text(errors="ignore")
    new, ch = patch_text(txt)
    if ch:
        shutil.copy2(p, p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak"))
        p.write_text(new)
        print("[patched]", p)
print("[done]")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Normalise les symboles provenant du top (retire suffixes bizarres, map USD->USDT, enlève '/')
def to_flat(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip().upper().replace("/", ":").replace("::", ":")
    s = s.replace(":USDT", "USDT").replace("USDTUSDT", "USDT")
    s = s.replace("USDUSDT", "USDT").replace("BUSDUSDT", "USDT")
    if s.endswith(":USD"):   s = s[:-4] + "USDT"
    if s.endswith("USD"):    s = s[:-3] + "USDT"
    if s.endswith(":USDT"):  s = s.replace(":USDT","USDT")
    s = s.replace(":", "")
    return s

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import sys
    for a in sys.argv[1:]:
        print(to_flat(a))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, os, sys, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
import ccxt

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
OUT  = DATA/"candles"  # stockage isolé, non intrusif

# Env tunables
TF_LIST = os.getenv("TF_LIST","5m,15m,30m,1h").split(",")
LIMIT   = int(os.getenv("LIMIT","600"))           # ~600 bougies / tf
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_WORKERS","12"))    # parallélisme IO
RATE_MS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_RATE_MS","200"))   # throttle ccxt
EX      = os.getenv("EXCHANGE","bitget")
QUOTE   = os.getenv("QUOTE","USDT")
FUTPAR  = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def load_symbols():
    j = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    syms = [s for s in j.get("symbols") or []]
    # map flat -> ccxt symbol (BTCUSDT -> BTC/USDT:USDT si présent)
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    imap={}
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE:
            imap[m["symbol"].replace("/","").replace(":","")] = m["symbol"]
    ccxt_syms = []
    for flat in syms:
        s = imap.get(flat)
        if s: ccxt_syms.append((flat,s))
    return ccxt_syms

class Throttle:
    def __init__(self, rate_ms): self.rate=rate_ms/1000; self._t=0.0
    async def wait(self):
        dt = time.time()-self._t
        if dt < self.rate: await asyncio.sleep(self.rate-dt)
        self._t = time.time()

async def fetch_symbol(loop, ex, flat, sym, tf, limit, throttle):
    await throttle.wait()
    try:
        ohlcv = await loop.run_in_executor(None, lambda: ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, None, limit, FUTPAR))
        if not isinstance(ohlcv, list): return 0
        d = OUT/flat/tf; d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        (d/"last.json").write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at":now_iso(),"symbol":sym,"tf":tf,"data":ohlcv[-limit:]}, indent=0))
        return len(ohlcv)
    except Exception:
        return 0

async def run():
    pairs = load_symbols()
    if not pairs: 
        print("[ohlcv-top] no mapped symbols")
        return
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    throttle = Throttle(RATE_MS)
    async def one(flat, sym):
        out=0
        async with sem:
            for tf in TF_LIST:
                out += await fetch_symbol(loop, ex, flat, sym, tf, LIMIT, throttle)
        return flat, out
    tasks=[one(f,s) for f,s in pairs]
    res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
    ok = sum(1 for r in res if isinstance(r, tuple) and r[1]>0)
    print(f"[ohlcv-top] symbols={len(pairs)} ok={ok} tf={','.join(TF_LIST)} workers={WORKERS}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=/opt/scalp/data; C=$DATA/candles; TRASH=$C/.trash_$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)
mkdir -p "$TRASH"/{5m,15m,30m}
mapfile -t TOP < <(jq -r '.symbols[]' "$DATA/top.json")
declare -A OK=(); for s in "${TOP[@]}"; do OK["${s//\//}"]=1; done
for tf in 5m 15m 30m; do
  shopt -s nullglob; for f in "$C/$tf"/*.json; do
    base=${f##*/}; base=${base%.json}
    [[ ${OK[$base]+x} ]] || mv -f "$f" "$TRASH/$tf/" || true
  done
done
echo "[gc] déplacé dans $TRASH"

MTime: 2025-09-26 10:38:06.747495441 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, os
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("ANALYSIS_WORKERS","8"))

# scripts existants
A_COIN = "/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py"
B_COIN = "/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py"  # s'il n'existe pas, on ignore

def load_symbols():
    j=json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    return [s for s in j.get("symbols") or []]

async def run_coin(cmd):
    proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(*cmd, stdout=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL)
    await proc.wait()
    return proc.returncode

async def main():
    syms = load_symbols()
    if not syms:
        print("[analysis-pool] no symbols"); return
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    async def one(sym):
        async with sem:
            rc1 = await run_coin(("python3", A_COIN, sym))
            rc2 = 0
            if Path(B_COIN).exists():
                rc2 = await run_coin(("python3", B_COIN, sym))
            return sym, max(rc1, rc2)
    tasks=[one(s) for s in syms]
    res=await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
    fails=[r[0] for r in res if isinstance(r,tuple) and r[1]!=0]
    print(f"[analysis-pool] total={len(syms)} fails={len(fails)} workers={WORKERS}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

Size: 2238
MTime: 2025-09-27 05:17:38.636022444 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
from pathlib import Path
import json, os, time
from _lib_price import last_close_1m

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PAPER = DATA/"paper"
PAPER.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
SIG = DATA/"signals.json"
POS = PAPER/"positions.json"
BAL = PAPER/"balance.json"

def jload(p:Path, dflt):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return dflt

def jsave(p:Path, obj):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

# paramètres
RISK_PCT = float(os.getenv("RISK_PCT", "0.02"))
LEV      = float(os.getenv("LEVERAGE", "5"))

def already_open(pos, sym):
    for p in pos:
        st = str(p.get("status","")).lower()
        if p.get("symbol")==sym and st.startswith("open"):
            return True
    return False

def main():
    sigs = jload(SIG, [])
    pos  = jload(POS, [])
    bal  = jload(BAL, {"cash":200.0})

    opened = 0
    for s in sigs:
        act  = s.get("action")
        if act not in ("enter_long","enter_short"): 
            continue
        sym  = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym")
        side = "long" if "long" in act else "short"
        if not sym or already_open(pos, sym): 
            continue

        # prix d'entrée
        price = s.get("price") or last_close_1m(sym)
        if not price or price <= 0:
            # pas de prix => skip
            s.setdefault("veto", "no_price")
            continue

        # sizing simple risque fixe
        cash = float(bal.get("cash", 0))
        risk_cash = cash * RISK_PCT
        notionnel = risk_cash * LEV
        qty = round(notionnel / price, 6)

        # marge consommée
        margin = notionnel / LEV

        entry = price
        now   = int(time.time())

        pos.append({
            "symbol": sym,
            "side": side,
            "status": f"open_{side}",
            "qty": qty,
            "entry": entry,
            "last": entry,
            "pnl$": 0.0,
            "opened_ts": now,
            "margin": round(margin, 2),
        })
        bal["cash"] = round(cash - margin, 2)
        opened += 1

    jsave(POS, pos)
    jsave(BAL, bal)
    print(f"[paper-open] opened={opened} cash={bal['cash']}")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
D=/opt/scalp/data/candles
mkdir -p "$D/1m" "$D/5m" "$D/15m" "$D/30m"

#  A. coin/TF/last.json  ->  TF/coin.json
find "$D" -mindepth 3 -maxdepth 3 -type f -name 'last.json' | while read -r f; do
  coin="$(basename "$(dirname "$(dirname "$f")")")"
  tf="$(basename "$(dirname "$f")")"
  mkdir -p "$D/$tf"
  ln -sfn "$f" "$D/$tf/${coin}.json"
done

#  B. TF/coin.json  ->  coin/TF/last.json
#     (si le consumer inverse existe)
find "$D" -mindepth 2 -maxdepth 2 -type f -name '*.json' | while read -r f; do
  tf="$(basename "$(dirname "$f")")"
  coin="$(basename "$f" .json)"
  mkdir -p "$D/${coin}/${tf}"
  [ -e "$D/${coin}/${tf}/last.json" ] || ln -sfn "$f" "$D/${coin}/${tf}/last.json"
done

#  C. (option) si fichier manquant, marquer pour refetch
missing=0
for tf in 1m 5m 15m 30m; do
  for coin in $(jq -r '.symbols[]' /opt/scalp/data/top.json 2>/dev/null || echo); do
    [ -f "$D/$tf/${coin}.json" ] || { echo "[MISSING] $tf/$coin"; missing=1; }
  done
done

if [ "$missing" = 1 ]; then
  echo "[fix] some candles missing -> ask fetcher to force."
fi

import re
def normalize(sym:str)->str:
    s=sym.replace("/","").replace(":","")
    s=re.sub(r"_U?MCBL$","",s); s=re.sub(r"PERP$","USDT",s)
    s=re.sub(r"(USDT){2}$","USDT",s)   # FIX
    return s

Size: 2708
MTime: 2025-09-26 15:58:42.958402941 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, argparse, tempfile
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"

DEF_MAX = {"1m":1800, "3m":1200, "5m":600, "15m":600, "30m":600}

def atomic_write(path:Path, obj):
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile("w", delete=False, dir=path.parent) as f:
        json.dump(obj, f)
        tmp = Path(f.name)
    tmp.replace(path)

def load_top():
    try:
        return set(json.loads(TOPF.read_text()).get("symbols",[]))
    except Exception:
        return set()

def valid_row(r):
    return isinstance(r,list) and len(r)>=6 and all(isinstance(x,(int,float)) for x in r[:6])

def trim_file(f:Path, maxbars:int)->tuple[int,int,str]:
    try:
        j = json.loads(f.read_text())
        data = j.get("data", [])
        if not isinstance(data, list) or not all(valid_row(r) for r in data):
            return (0,0,"bad")
        # tri par timestamp, dédoublonnage
        data.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
        dedup = []
        last_ts = None
        for r in data:
            if r[0] != last_ts:
                dedup.append(r)
                last_ts = r[0]
        kept = dedup[-maxbars:] if len(dedup)>maxbars else dedup
        if kept != data:
            atomic_write(f, {"data": kept})
        return (len(dedup), len(kept), "ok")
    except Exception:
        return (0,0,"err")

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--max", default=",".join(f"{k}={v}" for k,v in DEF_MAX.items()),
                    help="ex: 1m=1800,3m=1200,5m=600,15m=600,30m=600")
    ap.add_argument("--prune-not-in-top", action="store_true")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    maxmap = DEF_MAX.copy()
    for kv in args.max.split(","):
        if "=" in kv:
            k,v = kv.split("="); maxmap[k.strip()] = int(v)

    top = load_top() if args.prune_not_in_top else None

    total_before=total_after=bad=removed=0
    for tf in maxmap.keys():
        d = CAND/tf
        if not d.exists(): continue
        for f in d.glob("*.json"):
            if top is not None:
                sym = f.stem
                if sym not in top:
                    f.unlink(missing_ok=True)
                    removed += 1
                    continue
            before, after, status = trim_file(f, maxmap[tf])
            if status in ("bad","err"):
                f.unlink(missing_ok=True); bad += 1
            total_before += before
            total_after  += after

    print(f"[trim] bars before={total_before} after={total_after} files_bad_deleted={bad} files_pruned_not_in_top={removed}")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Size: 1269
MTime: 2025-09-27 05:34:00.513205618 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import re

USDT = "USDT"

# patterns rapides pour gagner du temps
_rx_bad_chars = re.compile(r'[^A-Z0-9]')
_rx_usdt_tail  = re.compile(r'(USDT)+$')           # un ou plusieurs USDT à la fin
_rx_any_usdt   = re.compile(r'USDT')               # présence de USDT quelque part

def sanitize(sym: str) -> str:
    """
    Normalise un symbole en MAJ, supprime les caractères bizarres,
    élimine les suffixes USDT répétés (USDTUSDT, USDT…USDT), et
    s'assure qu'il finit par *exactement* un USDT.
    """
    if not sym:
        return sym

    s = sym.upper().strip()

    # remplace séparateurs suspects par rien (ex: 'FIL-USDT', 'FLOKI/USDT', 'FL O K IUSDT')
    s = _rx_bad_chars.sub('', s)

    # si on trouve USDT quelque part: on coupe tout ce qui suit le premier USDT
    m = _rx_any_usdt.search(s)
    if m:
        base = s[:m.start()]         # ce qu'il y a avant le 1er USDT
        # nettoie le base (au cas où il reste un USDT fragmenté)
        base = _rx_bad_chars.sub('', base)
        s = base + USDT
    else:
        # pas de USDT du tout -> on l'ajoute (nos quotes sont fixées à USDT)
        s = s + USDT

    # compresse tout suffixe USDT répété (sécurité)
    s = _rx_usdt_tail.sub(USDT, s)

    return s

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, sys
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); TOP=DATA/"top.json"; C=DATA/"candles"
TFS=("5m","15m","30m")

def has(flat, tf):
    f=C/flat/tf/"last.json"
    if not f.exists(): return False
    try:
        j=json.loads(f.read_text()); return bool(j.get("data"))
    except: return False

def main():
    top=json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    syms=[s for s in top.get("symbols") or []][:30]
    missing={}
    for s in syms:
        miss=[tf for tf in TFS if not has(s, tf)]
        if miss: missing[s]=miss
    ok=len(missing)==0
    print(f"[ohlcv-check] ok={ok} missing={len(missing)}")
    for k,v in list(missing.items())[:20]:
        print(f" - {k}: {','.join(v)}")
    sys.exit(0 if ok else 1)
if __name__=="__main__": main()

DATA=/opt/scalp/data

AOUT=$DATA/analyse_A_out.json

  | sed 's/,/, /g; s/^/6->10: /; s/$//' || true

totA=$(jq 'to_entries|length' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
# Pour B: on compte les fichiers 1m/3m/5m présents pour les symbols d'A ctx!=none
totB=$(jq -r 'to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx!="none"))|length' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
okB=$(jq -r '
  to_entries
  | map(select(.value.ctx!="none")|.key)
  | map(["/opt/scalp/data/candles/1m/"+., "/opt/scalp/data/candles/3m/"+., "/opt/scalp/data/candles/5m/"+.] )
  | map( [.[0]+".json",.[1]+".json",.[2]+".json"] | map((input_filename? // "") ) )
' 2>/dev/null || true)
# résumé simple par fichiers réellement présents
b1=$(jq -r '
  to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx!="none")|.key)
  | map( (("/opt/scalp/data/candles/1m/"+.)+".json") ) 
  | map( ( ( (input/0)? ) ) )
' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null || true)

# Affichage compact et robuste
ok3=$(bash -lc '
  c=0
  while read -r s; do
    test -s "/opt/scalp/data/candles/1m/$s.json" \
      && test -s "/opt/scalp/data/candles/3m/$s.json" \
      && test -s "/opt/scalp/data/candles/5m/$s.json" && c=$((c+1))
  done < <(jq -r "to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx!=\"none\")|.key)|.[]" '"$AOUT"')
  echo $c
')
printf "Inputs A (5/15/30): %s/%s    Inputs B (1/3/5): %s/%s\n" "${okA:-0}" "${totA:-0}" "${ok3:-0}" "${totB:-0}"

echo
echo "Analyses A   (S  pb pH ps  ctx)"
pick=$(
  jq -r '
    def sc: .value.S // 0;
    def row: {sym:.key, S:(.value.S//0), pb:(.value.pb//0), ph:(.value.ph//0), ps:(.value.ps//0), ctx:(.value.ctx//"none")};
    . as $A
    | [ "BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT" ]
    | map(select(IN($A|keys[]; .))) as $fixed
    | ($A|to_entries|sort_by(-(.value.S//0))|map(.key)) as $sorted
    | $fixed + ($sorted - $fixed)[0:2] + (($sorted|reverse) - $fixed)[0:2]
    | unique
    | .[]
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null
)
for s in $pick; do
  jq -r --arg k "$s" '
    .[$k] // {}
    | [$k, (.S//0), (.pb//0), (.ph//0), (.ps//0), (.ctx//"none")]
    | @tsv
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null | awk -F'\t' '{
      sym=$1; gsub(/USDT$/,"",sym); gsub(/USD$/,"",sym);
      printf "%-5s S=%-0.3f  pb=%-0.3f pH=%-0.3f ps=%-0.3f  %s\n", sym,$2,$3,$4,$5,$6
  }'
done

# --- Lignes BUY/HOLD/SELL ---
echo
for side in BUY HOLD SELL; do
  low=$(echo "$side" | tr A-Z a-z)
  line=$(jq -r --arg s "$low" '
     to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx==$s)|.key)|map(sub("USDT$";"")|sub("USD$";""))|join(", ")
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null)
  [ -z "$line" ] && line="aucun"
  printf "%s: %s\n" "$side" "$line"
done

# --- Signaux récents ---
echo
echo "Signaux récents"

  [.[-8:][]] // []
  | reverse
  | .[]
  | "\(.ts) \(.side) \(.symbol) entry=\(.entry) sl=\(.sl) tp=\(.tp) lev=\(.leverage//0) why=\(.why//"")"
' "$SOUT" 2>/dev/null || echo "aucun"
[ -s "$SOUT" ] || echo "aucun"

echo
echo "Historique récents"
if [ -s /opt/scalp/logs/signals.log ]; then
  tail -n 12 /opt/scalp/logs/signals.log

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, re
from pathlib import Path
from sym_normalize import normalize

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TFs  = ["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]

def rename_inside(dirp: Path):
    if not dirp.exists(): return
    for p in dirp.iterdir():
        if not p.is_file(): continue
        base = p.stem
        norm = normalize(base)
        if norm != base:
            p2 = p.with_name(norm + p.suffix)
            if not p2.exists():
                p.rename(p2)

def fix_top_json():
    f = DATA/"top.json"
    if not f.exists(): return
    t = json.loads(f.read_text())
    syms = t.get("symbols") or []
    fixed = []
    for s in syms:
        n = normalize(s)
        if n not in fixed:
            fixed.append(n)
    t["symbols"] = fixed
    f.write_text(json.dumps(t, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def main():
    # candles by TF
    for tf in TFs:
        rename_inside(CAND/tf)
    # historique compact éventuel
    for tf in TFs:
        d = CAND/f"{tf}_raw"
        if d.exists(): rename_inside(d)
    fix_top_json()
    print("OK: filenames & top.json normalisés.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import pathlib, re, shutil

ROOT = pathlib.Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
targets = [p for p in ROOT.rglob("*.py") if "analysis_a" in p.name]

pattern_old = re.compile(r'candles/[^/]+/[0-9]+m/last\.json')
pattern_tpl = re.compile(r'candles/\{sym\}/\{tf\}/last\.json')

def patch_file(p):
    txt = p.read_text()
    orig = txt
    txt = pattern_old.sub("candles/{tf}/{sym}.json", txt)
    txt = pattern_tpl.sub("candles/{tf}/{sym}.json", txt)
    if txt != orig:
        shutil.copy2(p, p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak"))
        p.write_text(txt)
        print("[patched]", p)

for f in targets:
    patch_file(f)

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

TOOLS=/opt/scalp/tools
ARCH="$TOOLS._archive_$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)"
mkdir -p "$ARCH"

# Whitelist minimale à garder
keep=(
  "expand_top_ranked_light.py"  # Top futures, shortlist, depth optionnel
  "expand_top_fast_plus.py"     # Variante tickers-only + depth (fallback)
  "force_top5.sh"               # Noyau fixe d'urgence
  "show_top.py"                 # Affichage Top
  "snap_top.sh"                 # Snapshot top.*
  "diff_top.py"                 # Diff entre snapshots
)

# Crée fichiers vides si manquants pour éviter faux positifs
for f in "${keep[@]}"; do
  [ -e "$TOOLS/$f" ] || : > "$TOOLS/$f"
done

echo "[clean] Archiver tout sauf: ${keep[*]}"
shopt -s nullglob
moved=0
for f in "$TOOLS"/*; do
  base="$(basename "$f")"
  skip=0
  for k in "${keep[@]}"; do
    [[ "$base" == "$k" ]] && { skip=1; break; }
  done
  # Ne pas toucher au script courant
  [[ "$base" == "clean_tools.sh" ]] && skip=1
  if [[ $skip -eq 0 ]]; then
    mv -f "$f" "$ARCH/"
    ((moved++)) || true
  fi
done
shopt -u nullglob

echo "[clean] $moved éléments déplacés vers: $ARCH"
echo "[clean] Contenu conservé:"
printf ' - %s\n' "${keep[@]}" "clean_tools.sh"

from pathlib import Path
import json, time

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"

def last_close_1m(sym:str)->float:
    """close de la dernière bougie 1m CLÔTURÉE pour sym."""
    p = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return 0.0
    try:
        rows = json.loads(p.read_text())
        if not rows: return 0.0
        now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
        # période 1m
        per = 60_000
        last_ts = int(rows[-1][0])
        # si la dernière n'est pas close, on prend l'avant-dernière
        r = rows[-2] if last_ts + per > now_ms and len(rows) >= 2 else rows[-1]
        return float(r[4])  # close
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, time, shutil
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP   = DATA/"top.json"
AOUT1 = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
AOUT2 = DATA/"analysis_a_out.json"   # fallback
SIG   = DATA/"signals.json"
POS   = DATA/"positions.json"
HIST  = DATA/"history.json"
PBAL  = DATA/"paper_balance.json"    # {"balance": 200.0}

# ----- io -----
def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def human_k(x):
    try:
        x=float(x)
        if x>=1e9: return f"{x/1e9:.1f}B"
        if x>=1e6: return f"{x/1e6:.1f}M"
        if x>=1e3: return f"{x/1e3:.1f}k"
        return f"{x:.0f}"
    except: return "—"

def bold(s): return f"\x1b[1m{s}\x1b[0m"

# ----- header -----
def show_top_and_balance():
    t=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    ts=t.get("generated_at","—")
    src=t.get("source","—")
    syms=t.get("symbols") or []
    tail = [s.replace("USDT","") for s in syms[5:10]]
    bal = (jload(PBAL, {"balance":200.0}) or {}).get("balance", 200.0)
    print(bold(f"== SCALP DASHBOARD @ {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ', time.gmtime())} =="))
    print(f"Top30  ts={ts}  src={src}  N={len(syms)}   Paper: ${bal:.2f}")
    if tail: print("6→10:", ", ".join(tail))

# ----- Analyses A: 1 ligne -----
def pick_best_worst(a, k=2):
    items=[(sym,v) for sym,v in (a or {}).items() if isinstance(v,dict)]
    items.sort(key=lambda x: float(x[1].get("S",0.0)), reverse=True)
    return items[:k], items[-k:]

def show_analyses_a():
    a = jload(AOUT1, None)
    if a is None: a = jload(AOUT2, {})
    if not a:
        print("Analyses A: —"); return
    want=[]
    for s in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if s in a: want.append((s,a[s]))
    best,worst = pick_best_worst(a,2)
    seen=set(x[0] for x in want)
    for t in best+worst:
        if t[0] not in seen:
            want.append(t); seen.add(t[0])
        if len(want)>=6: break
    print(bold("Analyses A  (S  pb pH ps  ctx)"))
    for sym,rec in want:
        name=sym.replace("USDT","")
        S   = float(rec.get("S",0.0))
        pbi = int(rec.get("pb_i",0)); pHi=int(rec.get("pH_i",0)); psi=int(rec.get("ps_i",0))
        ctx = rec.get("context","none")
        print(f"{name:5s}  S={S:0.4f}  pb={pbi:2d} pH={pHi:2d} ps={psi:2d}  {ctx:4s}")

# ----- Signaux regroupés -----
def derive_lev(n, m):
    try:
        n=float(n); m=float(m); return int(round(n/m)) if m>0 else 0
    except: return 0

def show_signals():
    data = jload(SIG, []) or []
    print(bold("\nSignaux récents"))
    if not data:
        print("  aucun"); return
    print("ts            sym side lev qty        notion  entry      tp         sl         why")
    for r in data[-10:][::-1]:
        ts   = (r.get("ts","") or "")[:16]
        sym  = (r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")[:8]
        side = r.get("side","")
        lev  = derive_lev(r.get("notional",0), r.get("margin",0))
        qty  = float(r.get("qty",0.0))
        n    = human_k(r.get("notional",0.0))
        en   = r.get("entry","")
        tp   = r.get("tp","")
        sl   = r.get("sl","")
        why  = (r.get("why","") or "")[:28]
        print(f"{ts:16s} {sym:8s} {side:4s} {lev:3d} {qty:10.6f} {n:7s} {str(en):10s} {str(tp):10s} {str(sl):10s} {why}")

# ----- Positions / Historique -----
def show_positions():
    p = jload(POS, {}) or {}
    items = [p] if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("symbol") else (p if isinstance(p,list) else [])
    print(bold("\nPositions"))
    if not items:
        print("  aucune"); return
    print("sym   side  qty        entry      pnl     sl         tp")
    for r in items[:10]:
        sym=(r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")
        print(f"{sym:6s} {r.get('side',''):4s} {r.get('qty',0.0):10.6f} {str(r.get('entry','')):10s} {str(r.get('pnl','')):7s} {str(r.get('sl','')):10s} {str(r.get('tp','')):10s}")

def show_history():
    h = jload(HIST, [])
    print(bold("\nHistorique récents"))
    if not h:
        print("  aucun"); return
    for r in h[-10:][::-1]:
        ts = (r.get("ts","") or "")[:16]
        sym= (r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")

        p  = r.get("price","")
        q  = r.get("qty","")
        print(f"{ts:16s} {sym:8s} {act:10s} p={p} q={q}")

def main():
    _ = shutil.get_terminal_size((100,40))  # reserve sizing if needed
    show_top_and_balance()
    show_analyses_a()
    show_signals()
    show_positions()
    show_history()

    main()

import json, os, sys, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = Path(DATA) / "candles"
TOPF = Path(DATA) / "top.json"

# mapping TF -> durée en ms
TF_MS = {
    "1m": 60_000,
    "3m": 180_000,
    "5m": 300_000,
    "15m": 900_000,
    "30m": 1_800_000,
}

def main():
    if not TOPF.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] top.json introuvable: {TOPF}")
        sys.exit(1)

    top = json.loads(TOPF.read_text())
    symbols = top.get("symbols") or []
    if not symbols:
        print("[ERR] Aucun symbole dans top.json")
        sys.exit(1)

    ex_name = top.get("exchange", "binance").lower()
    if ex_name not in ccxt.exchanges:
        print(f"[WARN] Exchange {ex_name} non supporté, fallback binance")
        ex_name = "binance"

    ex = getattr(ccxt, ex_name)()
    ex.load_markets()

    for sym in symbols:
        for tf, ms in TF_MS.items():
            try:
                ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, limit=600)
                outdir = CAND / tf
                outdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                outf = outdir / f"{sym}.json"
                json.dump({"data": ohlcv}, open(outf, "w"))
                print(f"[OK] {sym} {tf} -> {outf}")
                time.sleep(ex.rateLimit/1000)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[ERR] {sym} {tf}: {e}", file=sys.stderr)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Entrée: dict tf -> OHLCV [[ts,o,h,l,c,v],...]
# Sortie: features par tf et agrégés
from analysis_a_lib import ema, rsi, stdev, atr, logret, lastn, safe

def tf_features(rows):
    ts=[r[0] for r in rows]; o=[float(r[1]) for r in rows]
    h=[float(r[2]) for r in rows]; l=[float(r[3]) for r in rows]
    c=[float(r[4]) for r in rows]; v=[float(r[5]) for r in rows]
    # returns, vola
    lr=logret(c)
    vola=stdev([x or 0.0 for x in lr], period=48)  # ~2j en 5m
    # trend: ema fast/slow
    efast=ema(c, 2/(12+1))
    eslow=ema(c, 2/(48+1))
    trend=[(f/s-1.0) if s else 0.0 for f,s in zip(efast, eslow)]
    # rsi
    r = rsi(c, period=14)
    # atr %
    a = atr(h,l,c,period=14)
    atrp=[(x/c[i]) if (x and c[i]) else None for i,x in enumerate(a)]
    return dict(ts=ts, o=o,h=h,l=l,c=c,v=v, lr=lr, vola=vola, trend=trend, rsi=r, atrp=atrp)

def aggregate(fs5, fs15, fs30):
    # momentum récent = somme des 3 derniers ret sur chaque tf
    def mom_last(fs):
        lr=fs["lr"]; vals=[x for x in lr if x is not None][-3:]
        return sum(vals) if vals else 0.0
    mom = mom_last(fs5)+mom_last(fs15)+mom_last(fs30)
    # volatilité récente = moyenne des 24 dernières vola sur chaque tf
    def vola_last(fs):
        vv=[x for x in fs["vola"] if x is not None][-24:]
        return sum(vv)/len(vv) if vv else 0.0
    vola = sum([vola_last(fs5), vola_last(fs15), vola_last(fs30)])/3.0
    # pression acheteuse/vendeuse par RSI centrée
    def pressure(fs):
        r=[x for x in fs["rsi"] if x is not None][-12:]
        if not r: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return (st.mean(r)-50.0)/50.0  # [-1..+1]
    p5,p15,p30 = pressure(fs5), pressure(fs15), pressure(fs30)
    press = 0.5*p5 + 0.3*p15 + 0.2*p30
    # surchauffe via ATR%
    def heat(fs):
        a=[x for x in fs["atrp"] if x is not None][-12:]
        if not a: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return st.mean(a)
    heatp = sum([heat(fs5),heat(fs15),heat(fs30)])/3.0
    # trend multi-échelles
    def trend_last(fs):
        t=[x for x in fs["trend"] if x is not None][-6:]
        if not t: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return st.mean(t)
    tr = 0.5*trend_last(fs5)+0.3*trend_last(fs15)+0.2*trend_last(fs30)
    return dict(mom=mom, vola=vola, press=press, heat=heatp, trend=tr)

def compute_features(data):
    f5 = tf_features(data["5m"])
    f15 = tf_features(data["15m"])
    f30 = tf_features(data["30m"])
    agg = aggregate(f5,f15,f30)
    return {"5m":f5, "15m":f15, "30m":f30, "agg":agg}

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat
from ctx_logic import compute_ctx, CtxState

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA / "candles"
TOP  = DATA / "top.json"
OUT  = DATA / "analyse_A_out.json"

def jload(p, d=None):
    p = Path(p)
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except: return d

def load_tf(sym, tf): return jload(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", [])

def last_complete(arr, tf_s):
    if not arr: return []
    now = int(time.time())
    ts_last = int(arr[-1][0])//1000
    return arr[:-1] if (now - ts_last) < tf_s else arr

def mk_inputs(arr):
    if len(arr) < 60:
        return dict(ema12=0,ema26=0,atr14=1,macd_hist=0,macd_sigma100=1,
                    rsi14=50,adx14=20,obv_delta20=0,obv_medabs200=1,atr_pct=0.2)
    closes=[x[4] for x in arr]
    def ema(vals,n):
        k=2/(n+1); e=None
        for v in vals: e=v if e is None else e+k*(v-e)
        return e
    return dict(ema12=ema(closes,12),ema26=ema(closes,26),
                atr14=1,macd_hist=0,macd_sigma100=1,
                rsi14=50,adx14=20,obv_delta20=0,obv_medabs200=1,atr_pct=0.2)

def main():
    top = jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms = [to_flat(s) for s in top.get("symbols",[])[:30]]
    out={}
    for s in syms:
        m5=last_complete(load_tf(s,"5m"),5*60)
        m15=last_complete(load_tf(s,"15m"),15*60)
        m30=last_complete(load_tf(s,"30m"),30*60)
        if not (m5 and m15 and m30):
            out[s]=dict(ctx="none",pb=1/3,ph=1/3,ps=1/3,S=0.0,Sw=0.0); continue
        res=compute_ctx({"5m":mk_inputs(m5),"15m":mk_inputs(m15),"30m":mk_inputs(m30)},CtxState())
        out[s]=dict(ctx=res["ctx_state"].ctx,pb=float(res["pb"]),ph=float(res["ph"]),ps=float(res["ps"]),
                    S=float(res["agg"].get("S_15m",res["Sw"])),Sw=float(res["Sw"]))
    OUT.write_text(json.dumps(out,ensure_ascii=False))
    print(f"[bridge] analysed={len(out)} out={OUT}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
DATA=Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SIGF=DATA/"signals.json"; POSF=DATA/"paper/positions.json"; BALF=DATA/"paper/balance.json"
CAND=DATA/"candles"; AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"; BLAST=DATA/"debug/b_last"
N=20; FRESH=300; MIN_STRENGTH=float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH","1"))
def jload(p, d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def hhmm(ts):
    if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
    try: return datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M")
    except: return "--:--"
def fresh(p:Path):
    try: return time.time()-p.stat().st_mtime <= FRESH
    except: return False
def budget():
    b=jload(BALF,{})
    for k in ("balance","equity","cash","budget"):
        if k in b:
            try: return float(b[k])
            except: pass
    return float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))
def is_open(sym):
    for p in jload(POSF,[]):
        if str(p.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running") and (p.get("symbol")==sym or p.get("sym")==sym):
            return True
    return False
def ctx(sym): return str(jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json",{}).get("context","none")).lower()
def ohlcv_ok(sym):
    return all([
        (CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        (CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        fresh(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"),
        fresh(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json"),
    ])
def explain(sig):
    sym=sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin") or "?"
    side=(sig.get("side") or sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    action=(sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    strength=float(sig.get("strength") or 0)
    margin=float(sig.get("margin") or sig.get("margin_usd") or sig.get("size_usd") or 0)
    bbal=budget()
    reasons=[]
    # infos brutes B
    b_last=jload(BLAST/f"{sym}.json",{})
    parsed=b_last.get("parsed",{})
    tp=parsed.get("tp"); sl=parsed.get("sl"); size=parsed.get("size") or 0; direction=parsed.get("direction") or side
    # règles
    if side=="none": reasons.append("side_none")
    if action in ("hold_long","hold_short","idle","wait"): reasons.append(f"action_{action}")
    if is_open(sym): reasons.append("already_open")
    if strength < MIN_STRENGTH: reasons.append(f"weak_strength<{MIN_STRENGTH}")
    if margin>0 and bbal < margin: reasons.append(f"insufficient_budget {bbal:.2f}<{margin:.2f}")
    if not ohlcv_ok(sym): reasons.append("stale_ohlcv")
    if ctx(sym)=="none": reasons.append("ctx_none")
    status = "WAIT" if reasons else "ACCEPTABLE"
    return {
        "t": hhmm(sig.get("ts") or sig.get("time") or sig.get("timestamp")),
        "sym": sym, "side": side, "action": action, "strength": strength,
        "margin": margin, "tp": tp, "sl": sl, "size": size, "dir": direction,
        "ctx": ctx(sym), "budget": bbal, "reasons": reasons or ["ok"]
    }, status
def main():
    sigs=jload(SIGF,[])
    if isinstance(sigs,dict): sigs=sigs.get("items") or sigs.get("signals") or []
    tail=sigs[-N:]
    print(f"== paper_debug_explain @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ')} ==")
    print(f"budget={budget():.2f}  open={len(jload(POSF,[]))}")
    for s in tail:
        res, st = explain(s)
        print(f"{res['t']} {res['sym']:<10} {res['side']:<5} str={res['strength']:<.1f} m={res['margin']:.2f} "
              f"tp={res['tp']} sl={res['sl']} sz={res['size']} dir={res['dir']} ctx={res['ctx']} -> {st} {','.join(res['reasons'])}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, subprocess, pathlib, time
DATA=pathlib.Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
ORIG="/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py"

def read_json_out(sym):
    p=subprocess.run(["python3", ORIG, sym], capture_output=True, text=True)
    out=(p.stdout or "").strip().splitlines()
    raw=out[-1] if out else "{}"
    try: j=json.loads(raw)
    except: j={"symbol":sym,"side":"none","action":"idle","strength":0,"reason":f"bad_json:{raw[:120]}"}
    j.setdefault("symbol", sym)
    # champs debug normalisés
    j.setdefault("direction", j.get("side","none"))
    j.setdefault("size", j.get("size") or j.get("qty") or j.get("amount") or 0)
    j.setdefault("margin", j.get("margin") or j.get("margin_usd") or j.get("size_usd") or 0)
    j.setdefault("tp", j.get("tp") or j.get("take_profit") or None)
    j.setdefault("sl", j.get("sl") or j.get("stop_loss") or None)
    j.setdefault("ts", int(time.time()))
    return j, p.stdout, p.stderr, p.returncode

def atomic_write(p, obj):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp=p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(p)

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2: sys.exit("usage: run_analysis_b_coin_debug.py SYMBOL")
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    j, out, err, rc = read_json_out(sym)
    # 1) trace debug
    dbg=DATA/"debug"/"b_last"/f"{sym}.json"
    atomic_write(dbg, {"stdout":out, "stderr":err, "rc":rc, "parsed":j})
    # 2) sortie coin pour l’agrégateur existant (ne rien casser)
    coin_out=DATA/"signals_coin"/f"{sym}.json"
    atomic_write(coin_out, j)
    # 3) echo pour logs
    print(json.dumps(j))
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import re, sys
from pathlib import Path
ROOT=Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
EXTS={".py",".sh",".bash",".zsh"}
SKIP=lambda p: any(s in p.name for s in (".bak",".backup","~")) or p.suffix not in EXTS
FILES=[p for p in ROOT.rglob("*") if p.is_file() and not SKIP(p)]

R=[
 # Python f-strings: f".../candles/{tf}/{sym}.json" -> f".../candles/{tf}/{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\s*\{\s*sym\s*\}\s*/\s*\{\s*tf\s*\}\s*/\s*last\.json'), r'candles/{tf}/{sym}.json'),
 # format %: "candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json" -> "candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/%\(sym\)s/%\(tf\)s/last\.json'), r'candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json'),
 # .format: "candles/{tf}/{sym}.json".format(...) -> "candles/{tf}/{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\{sym\}/\{tf\}/last\.json'), r'candles/{tf}/{sym}.json'),
 # pathlib vars explicites: f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json" -> f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'\bf\s*=\s*CAND\s*/\s*sym\s*/\s*tf\s*/\s*"?last\.json"?'), r'f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"'),
 # chaînes littérales coin/tf/last.json -> tf/coin.json
 (re.compile(r'candles/[A-Za-z0-9_]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'), r'candles/\1/{sym}.json'),
 # Bash: "$D/candles/${tf}/${sym}.json" -> "$D/candles/${tf}/${sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\$\{sym\}/\$\{tf\}/last\.json'), r'candles/${tf}/${sym}.json'),
 (re.compile(r'candles/\$sym/\$tf/last\.json'), r'candles/$tf/$sym.json'),
]

def patch_text(s):
    changed=False
    for rx, rep in R:
        ns = rx.sub(rep, s)
        if ns!=s:
            s=ns; changed=True
    return s, changed

def main():
    touched=0
    for p in FILES:
        txt=p.read_text(errors="ignore")
        new, ch = patch_text(txt)
        if ch:
            p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak").write_text(txt)
            p.write_text(new)
            print("[patched]", p)
            touched+=1
    print(f"[done] {touched} fichiers modifiés")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"

def norm(sym:str)->str:
    return sym.replace("/","").replace(":","").upper()

def main():
    top = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    exn = (top.get("exchange") or "bitget").lower()
    ex  = getattr(ccxt, exn)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()

    ok = {norm(m["symbol"]) for m in ex.markets.values() if (m.get("quote") or "").upper()=="USDT"}
    syms = [s.upper() for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])]
    bad  = [s for s in syms if norm(s) not in ok]

    print(f"[map] exchange={exn} total={len(syms)} mapped={len(syms)-len(bad)} bad={len(bad)}")
    if bad:
        print("[map] bad:", ",".join(bad))
        top["symbols"] = [s for s in syms if s not in bad]
        TOP.write_text(json.dumps(top, indent=2))
        if len(top["symbols"]) < 5:
            print("[map] trop peu de symboles valides"); sys.exit(2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
