# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
# Logic: S per TF -> softmax -> multi-TF aggregate -> 5m veto -> hysteresis+persist -> context

import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict

# ---------- Config ----------
W = dict(EMA=0.35, MACD=0.25, RSI=0.20, ADX=0.10, OBV=0.10)
TAU = {"30m": 0.35, "15m": 0.30, "5m": 0.25}
TF_W = {"30m": 0.50, "15m": 0.30, "5m": 0.20}
ATR_GATE = {"30m": 0.25, "15m": 0.18, "5m": 0.12}  # %

P_ENTER = 0.60
P_EXIT  = 0.45
RANGE_LOW, RANGE_HIGH = 0.40, 0.60
PERSIST_BARS = 2

# ---------- Helpers ----------
def clip(x, lo, hi): return hi if x>hi else lo if x<lo else x
def tanh(x): return math.tanh(x)

def softmax_triple(S, tau):
    e_pos = math.exp(S/tau); e_neg = math.exp(-S/tau); den = e_pos + 1.0 + e_neg
    return e_pos/den, 1.0/den, e_neg/den  # pb, ph, ps

# ---------- Score per TF ----------
def score_tf(inp: dict, tf: str):
    atr = max(inp.get("atr14", 0.0), 1e-12)
    s_ema  = tanh((inp.get("ema12",0.0)-inp.get("ema26",0.0))/(1.5*atr))
    sigma  = max(inp.get("macd_sigma100",1e-12), 1e-12)
    s_macd = tanh(inp.get("macd_hist",0.0)/sigma)
    s_rsi  = clip((inp.get("rsi14",50.0)-50.0)/50.0, -1.0, 1.0)
    s_adx  = clip((inp.get("adx14",20.0)-20.0)/20.0, -1.0, 1.0)
    medabs = max(inp.get("obv_medabs200",1e-12), 1e-12)
    s_obv  = tanh(inp.get("obv_delta20",0.0)/medabs)

    # ATR% gate (low vol -> damp EMA+MACD)
    atr_pct = float(inp.get("atr_pct", 0.0))  # %
    if atr_pct < ATR_GATE[tf]:
        s_ema *= 0.5; s_macd *= 0.5

    num = (W["EMA"]*s_ema + W["MACD"]*s_macd + W["RSI"]*s_rsi +
           W["ADX"]*s_adx + W["OBV"]*s_obv)
    S = clip(num/sum(W.values()), -1.0, 1.0)
    pb, ph, ps = softmax_triple(S, TAU[tf])
    return {"S": S, "pb": pb, "ph": ph, "ps": ps}

# ---------- Aggregation (expose per-TF for veto) ----------
def aggregate_probs(per_tf: dict):
    wsum = sum(TF_W.values())
    pb = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    ph = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    ps = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    Sw = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    tot = pb+ph+ps
    pb,ph,ps = (1/3,1/3,1/3) if tot<=0 else (pb/tot, ph/tot, ps/tot)
    out = {"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]
            out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]
            out[f"S_{tf}"] =per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out

# ---------- 5m veto ----------
def apply_veto_m5(agg: dict) -> dict:
    pb, ps = agg["pb"], agg["ps"]
    pb30, pb15 = agg.get("pb_30m",0.0), agg.get("pb_15m",0.0)
    ps30, ps15 = agg.get("ps_30m",0.0), agg.get("ps_15m",0.0)
    S5 = agg.get("S_5m", 0.0)

    bull_ok = (pb >= P_ENTER) and (pb30 >= 0.55) and (pb15 >= 0.55) and (S5 >= 0.0)
    bear_ok = (ps >= P_ENTER) and (ps30 >= 0.55) and (ps15 >= 0.55) and (S5 <= 0.0)

    if pb >= P_ENTER and not bull_ok:
        agg["pb"] = max(agg["pb"], P_EXIT - 1e-6)
    if ps >= P_ENTER and not bear_ok:
        agg["ps"] = max(agg["ps"], P_EXIT - 1e-6)

    tot = agg["pb"] + agg["ph"] + agg["ps"]
    if tot > 0:
        agg["pb"], agg["ph"], agg["ps"] = agg["pb"]/tot, agg["ph"]/tot, agg["ps"]/tot
    return agg

# ---------- Context state / decision ----------
from dataclasses import dataclass
@dataclass
class CtxState:
    ctx: str = "none"         # "buy"|"sell"|"hold"|"none"
    streak_ctx: str = "none"
    streak: int = 0
    bars_in_ctx: int = 0

def decide_next_ctx(prob, prev_ctx):
    pb, ph, ps = prob["pb"], prob["ph"], prob["ps"]
    buy_ok  = (pb >= P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="buy"  and pb >= P_EXIT)
    sell_ok = (ps >= P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="sell" and ps >= P_EXIT)
    range_ok = (RANGE_LOW <= ph <= RANGE_HIGH)
    if buy_ok  and pb >= ps and pb >= ph: return "buy"
    if sell_ok and ps >= pb and ps >= ph: return "sell"
    if range_ok: return "hold"
    return "none"

def update_context(state: CtxState, prob: dict, bar_closed: bool=True) -> CtxState:
    target = decide_next_ctx(prob, state.ctx)
    if target == state.ctx:
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx, streak_ctx=target,
                        streak=min(state.streak+1, PERSIST_BARS),
                        bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx + (1 if bar_closed else 0))
    streak = state.streak + 1 if target == state.streak_ctx else 1
    if streak >= PERSIST_BARS:
        return CtxState(ctx=target, streak_ctx=target, streak=streak,
                        bars_in_ctx=1 if bar_closed else 0)
    return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx, streak_ctx=target, streak=streak,
                    bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx + (1 if bar_closed else 0))

# ---------- Pipeline utilitaire ----------
def compute_ctx(per_tf_inputs: dict, prev_state: CtxState) -> dict:
    per_tf = {tf: score_tf(per_tf_inputs[tf], tf) for tf in per_tf_inputs}
    agg = aggregate_probs(per_tf)
    agg = apply_veto_m5(agg)
    new_state = update_context(prev_state, agg, bar_closed=True)
    ints = {k:int(round(10*agg[k])) for k in ("pb","ph","ps")}
    return {"pb":agg["pb"], "ph":agg["ph"], "ps":agg["ps"], "Sw":agg["Sw"],
            "ctx_state": new_state, "ints": ints, "per_tf": per_tf, "agg": agg}

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from math import fabs
def ema(xs, n):
    if not xs: return []
    a = 2.0/(n+1.0); s = xs[0]; out=[s]
    for x in xs[1:]:
        s = a*x + (1-a)*s; out.append(s)
    return out
def rsi(cl, n=14):
    if len(cl)<n+1: return [None]*len(cl)
    gains=[]; losses=[]; out=[None]
    for a,b in zip(cl, cl[1:]):
        d=b-a; gains.append(max(d,0.0)); losses.append(max(-d,0.0)); out.append(None)
    ag=sum(gains[:n])/n; al=sum(losses[:n])/n
    vals=[]
    for g,l in zip(gains[n:], losses[n:]):
        ag=(ag*(n-1)+g)/n; al=(al*(n-1)+l)/n
        vals.append(100.0 - 100.0/(1.0 + (ag/(al+1e-12))))
    return [None]*(len(cl)-len(vals)) + vals
def macd_hist(cl, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    ef=ema(cl,f); es=ema(cl,s); macd=[a-b for a,b in zip(ef,es)]
    sigl=ema(macd,sig); return [m-s for m,s in zip(macd,sigl)]
def adx(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(h)<n+1: return [None]*len(h)
    tr=[None]; dmp=[None]; dmn=[None]
    for i in range(1,len(h)):
        tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
        dmp.append(max(h[i]-h[i-1],0.0)); dmn.append(max(l[i-1]-l[i],0.0))
    atr=sum(tr[1:n+1])/n; pdi=sum(dmp[1:n+1])/n; ndi=sum(dmn[1:n+1])/n
    ax=[None]* (n+1)
    for i in range(n+1,len(h)):
        atr=(atr*(n-1)+tr[i])/n; pdi=(pdi*(n-1)+dmp[i])/n; ndi=(ndi*(n-1)+dmn[i])/n
        pd=100.0*(pdi/(atr+1e-12)); nd=100.0*(ndi/(atr+1e-12))
        dx=100.0*fabs(pd-nd)/max(pd+nd,1e-12)
        ax.append(dx if ax[-1] is None else ((ax[-1]*(n-1))+dx)/n)
    return ax[:len(h)]
def obv_deltas(cl, vol, win=20, medw=200):
    obv=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        d=(1 if cl[i]>cl[i-1] else -1 if cl[i]<cl[i-1] else 0)*vol[i]
        obv.append(obv[-1]+d)
    d20=obv[-1] - (obv[-win-1] if len(obv)>win else 0.0)
    diffs=[abs(obv[i]-obv[i-1]) for i in range(1,len(obv))]
    import statistics as st
    med=st.median(diffs[-medw:]) if diffs else 1.0
    return d20, max(med,1.0)
def atr_pct(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [None]*len(c)
    tr=[None]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
    a=2.0/(n+1.0); s=sum(tr[1:n+1])/n; out=[None]*n+[s]
    for x in tr[n+1:]:
        s=a*x+(1-a)*s; out.append(s)
    return [ (out[i]/c[i])*100.0 if out[i] is not None and c[i]>0 else None for i in range(len(out))]
def indicators_from_ohlcv(rows):
    o=[float(r[1]) for r in rows]; h=[float(r[2]) for r in rows]
    l=[float(r[3]) for r in rows]; c=[float(r[4]) for r in rows]; v=[float(r[5]) for r in rows]
    ema12=ema(c,12)[-1]; ema26=ema(c,26)[-1]
    hist=macd_hist(c,12,26,9); import statistics as st
    macd_h=hist[-1] if hist else 0.0; macd_sigma=st.pstdev(hist[-100:]) if len(hist)>=2 else 1.0
    r=rsi(c,14); rsi14=r[-1] if r and r[-1] is not None else 50.0
    ad=adx(h,l,c,14); adx14=ad[-1] if ad and ad[-1] is not None else 20.0
    obv20, med=obv_deltas(c,v,20,200)
    atrp=atr_pct(h,l,c,14); atrp14=atrp[-1] if atrp and atrp[-1] is not None else 0.0
    return dict(ema12=ema12, ema26=ema26, atr14=max(abs(h[-1]-l[-1]),1e-9),
                macd_hist=macd_h, macd_sigma100=max(macd_sigma,1e-9),
                rsi14=rsi14, adx14=adx14, obv_delta20=obv20,
                obv_medabs200=max(med,1.0), atr_pct=atrp14)

from pathlib import Path
import json
from _lib_price import last_close_1m

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
SIG  = DATA/"signals.json"
DBG  = DATA/"debug"/"bridge"
DBG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def jload(p:Path, dflt):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return dflt

def main():
    items = jload(SIG, [])
    out = []
    for s in items:
        sym = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym")
        if not sym: 
            out.append(s); 
            continue
        # normalise clé "price"
        px = s.get("price")
        if px in (None, 0, 0.0):
            px = last_close_1m(sym)
            if px: s["price"] = px
        # log léger par coin
        (DBG/f"{sym}.log").write_text(
            f'{sym} ctx={s.get("ctx")} str={s.get("strength")} '
            f'pb={s.get("pb")} ps={s.get("ps")} atr%={s.get("atr_pct",0)} '
            f'veto={s.get("veto",0)} action={s.get("action")} side={s.get("side")} '
            f'price={s.get("price")}\n'
        )
        out.append(s)
    SIG.write_text(json.dumps(out, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    print(f"[bridge-enrich] signals={len(out)} updated")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, asyncio
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP =DATA/"top.json"
BOUT=DATA/"signals_coin"
ALL =DATA/"signals.json"
RUN =Path("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py")

WORKERS=int(os.getenv("SIGNAL_WORKERS","10"))
TIMEOUT=int(os.getenv("SIGNAL_TIMEOUT_S","60"))

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

async def run_one(sym):
    try:
        p=await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec("python3", str(RUN), sym,
                                               stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
                                               stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL)
        await asyncio.wait_for(p.wait(), timeout=TIMEOUT)
    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        try: p.kill()
        except: pass
    # read coin file
    return jload(BOUT/f"{sym}.json", {"symbol":sym,"side":"none","action":"no-output","strength":0,"reason":""})

async def main():
    top=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms=[s for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])][:30]
    sem=asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    async def one(s):
        async with sem: return await run_one(s)
    res=await asyncio.gather(*[one(s) for s in syms])
    # Liste ordonnée par force descendante puis symbole
    res=[r for r in res if isinstance(r,dict)]
    res_sorted=sorted(res, key=lambda x: (x.get("side")!="none", x.get("strength",0)), reverse=True)
    ALL.write_text(json.dumps(res_sorted[:50], indent=2))
    print(f"[signals] written {ALL} items={len(res_sorted)}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from b_logic import jload, jsave, last_complete, analyze_symbol, PARAM as BPAR

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"        # /candles/<tf>/<SYMBOL>.json  {"data":[[ts,o,h,l,c,v],...]}
A_OUT  = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
B_OUT  = DATA/"analyse_B_out.json"
SIGNALS= DATA/"signals.json"

TF_SEC = {"1m":60, "3m":180, "5m":300}

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    f = CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        j = json.loads(Path(f).read_text())
        arr = j.get("data") or []
    except:
        arr = []
    return last_complete(arr, TF_SEC[tf])

def write_signal(sig):
    if not sig: return
    # enrichissement standard
    sig.setdefault("lev", float(BPAR.get("leverage", 1)))
    sig.setdefault("risk_pct", float(BPAR.get("risk_pct", 0.0)))
    lst = (json.loads(SIGNALS.read_text()) if SIGNALS.exists() else []) or []
    lst.append(sig)
    lst = lst[-200:]
    SIGNALS.write_text(json.dumps(lst, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: b_run_coin.py SYMBOL", file=sys.stderr); return 2
    sym = sys.argv[1]
    a    = (json.loads(A_OUT.read_text()) if A_OUT.exists() else {}) or {}
    arow = a.get(sym, {}) or {}
    ctxA = arow.get("context") or "none"

    m1 = load_tf(sym, "1m")
    m3 = load_tf(sym, "3m")
    m5 = load_tf(sym, "5m")
    if not (m1 and m3 and m5):
        print(json.dumps({"symbol":sym, "error":"missing_candles_1m/3m/5m"})); return 1

    res = analyze_symbol(sym, ctxA, m1, m3, m5)
    # persist analyse_B_out.json (dict par symbole)
    bout = (json.loads(B_OUT.read_text()) if B_OUT.exists() else {}) or {}
    bout[sym] = res
    B_OUT.write_text(json.dumps(bout, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    # append signal si présent
    write_signal(res.get("signal"))
    print(json.dumps(res))
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    import sys as _; _.exit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
C=/opt/scalp/data/candles
TS=$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%S)
TR=$C/.trash_$TS; mkdir -p "$TR"
mkdir -p "$C/1m" "$C/3m" "$C/5m"

is_tf(){ case "$1" in 1m|3m|5m|10m|15m|30m) return 0;; *) return 1;; esac; }

# 1) Si on a des dossiers SYMBOL contenant 1m.json/3m.json/5m.json → on range
find "$C" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d | while read -r d; do
  bn=$(basename "$d")
  is_tf "$bn" && continue
  # si le dossier contient des JSON par TF, on les dépose dans C/TF/SYMBOL.json
  for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    f="$d/${tf}.json"
    [ -s "$f" ] && mv -f "$f" "$C/$tf/${bn}.json"
  done
  # si vide → poubelle
  rmdir "$d" 2>/dev/null || true
done

# 2) Fichiers égarés à la racine → poubelle
find "$C" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name '*.json' -exec mv -f {} "$TR"/ \;

# 3) Corriger *USD -> *USDT (fichiers)
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
  find "$C/$tf" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name '*USD.json' ! -name '*USDT.json' | while read -r f; do
    base=$(basename "$f")
    mv -f "$f" "$C/$tf/${base%.json}T.json"
  done
done

# 4) Supprimer TF non supportés
for bad in 10m 15m 30m; do
  [ -d "$C/$bad" ] && mv "$C/$bad" "$TR/${bad}_$TS" || true
done

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from math import isfinite, log
def safe(x, d=0.0):
    try:
        return float(x) if isfinite(float(x)) else d
    except: return d

def ema(series, alpha):
    out=[]; s=None
    for x in series:
        x=safe(x,0.0)
        s = x if s is None else (alpha*x + (1-alpha)*s)
        out.append(s)
    return out

def rsi(closes, period=14):
    if not closes: return []
    gains=[]; losses=[]
    prev=closes[0]
    rsis=[None]
    for c in closes[1:]:
        d=c-prev; prev=c
        gains.append(max(d,0.0)); losses.append(max(-d,0.0))
    if len(gains)<period: return [None]*len(closes)
    import itertools
    ag=sum(gains[:period])/period; al=sum(losses[:period])/period
    rs=[ag/(al+1e-12)]
    for g,l in zip(gains[period:], losses[period:]):
        ag=(ag*(period-1)+g)/period; al=(al*(period-1)+l)/period
        rs.append(ag/(al+1e-12))
    vals=[None]*(len(closes)-len(rs)-1)
    vals += [100.0 - 100.0/(1.0+r) for r in rs]
    return [None]+vals

def stdev(series, period):
    out=[None]*len(series)
    if period<=1 or len(series)<period: return out
    from statistics import pstdev
    for i in range(period-1, len(series)):
        window=series[i-period+1:i+1]
        out[i]=pstdev(window)
    return out

def atr(h, l, c, period=14):
    trs=[None]; prev=c[0]
    for hi,lo,cl in zip(h[1:],l[1:],c[1:]):
        tr=max(hi-lo, abs(hi-prev), abs(lo-prev))
        trs.append(tr); prev=cl
    return stdev(trs, period)

def logret(closes):
    out=[None]
    for a,b in zip(closes, closes[1:]):
        try: out.append(log(b/a))
        except: out.append(None)
    return out

def lastn(xs, n=1, default=None):
    return [x for x in xs if x is not None][-n:] or [default]

def norm01(x, lo, hi):
    if hi<=lo: return 0.0
    v=(x-lo)/(hi-lo)
    return 0.0 if v<0 else 1.0 if v>1 else v

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

def now_iso(): 
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

# ---- Params
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"
TOP_N = int(os.getenv("TOP_N", "30"))
MIN_QV = float(os.getenv("MIN_QV", "1000000"))       # 1M
MAX_SP = float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS", "60"))        # 0.60%
USE_DEPTH = os.getenv("USE_DEPTH", "0") == "1"
MIN_DEPTH = float(os.getenv("MIN_DEPTH_USD", "200000"))  # gate si USE_DEPTH=1
BAND_BPS = int(os.getenv("DEPTH_BAND_BPS", "50"))    # ±0.5%
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"; MAP=DATA/"symbol_map.json"
INACT=DATA/"coins_90d.json"

def load_inactive():
    try:
        j=json.loads(INACT.read_text())
        return set(j.get("inactive_symbols", []))
    except: 
        return set()

def load_seed():
    if TOP.exists():
        try:
            j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
            s=[x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
            if s: return s
        except: pass
    return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def clamp(x,a,b): 
    return a if x<a else b if x>b else x

def depth_usd(ex, sym, band_bps):
    try:
        ob = ex.fetch_order_book(sym, 100, {**FUT})
        if not ob.get("bids") or not ob.get("asks"): return 0.0
        bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
        lo,hi = mid*(1-band_bps/10000.0), mid*(1+band_bps/10000.0)
        q=0.0
        for p,a in ob["bids"]:
            if p<lo: break
            q += p*a
        for p,a in ob["asks"]:
            if p>hi: break
            q += p*a
        return float(q)
    except:
        return 0.0

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()
    inactive = load_inactive()    # persistance inactifs 90j
    
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}
    sym_map = {m["symbol"].replace("/","").replace(":",""): m["symbol"] for m in mkts}
    MAP.write_text(json.dumps(sym_map, indent=2))

    # tickers bulk + fallback par symbole si besoin
    tickers={}
    try:
        tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        flat = s.replace("/","").replace(":","")
        if flat in inactive: 
            continue
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): 
            continue
        if b in BAD_BASES:
            continue

        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        # quoteVolume fallback (Bitget/ccxt)
        qv = t.get("quoteVolume")
        if not qv:
            info = t.get("info", {})
            qv = info.get("quoteVolume") or info.get("quoteVolume24h") or info.get("baseVolume") # au cas où
        qv = float(qv or 0.0)

        bid,ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0:
            continue
        mid = 0.5*(bid+ask)
        sp_bps = clamp(10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid, 0.0, 200.0)  # clamp spread [0,200] bps

        if qv < MIN_QV or sp_bps > MAX_SP:
            continue

        # Depth gate optionnel
        d_q = 0.0
        if USE_DEPTH:
            try:
                d_q = depth_usd(ex, s, BAND_BPS)
            except:
                d_q = 0.0
            if d_q < MIN_DEPTH:
                continue

        pool.append({"symbol": s, "flat": flat, "qv": qv, "sp_bps": sp_bps, "depth_q": d_q})

    # tri par volume 24h
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x["qv"], reverse=True)

    # compose résultat: noyau fixe d'abord, puis complétion
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    # ajouter d'abord les seeds avec métriques si dispo
    for e in pool:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set:
            details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": 1.0, "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "spread_bps": e["sp_bps"], "depth_quote": e["depth_q"]})
    # compléter
    for e in pool:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set:
            continue
        out.append(e["flat"]); seed_set.add(e["flat"])
        details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": 0.0, "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "spread_bps": e["sp_bps"], "depth_quote": e["depth_q"]})
        if len(out) >= TOP_N:
            break

    meta={"generated_at": now_iso(), "source":"futures-tickers-fast+options", "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE}
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({**meta, "symbols": out[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at": meta["generated_at"], "n": len(out[:TOP_N]), "items": details[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    print(f"[expand+fast] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} use_depth={USE_DEPTH} top={len(out[:TOP_N])}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import json, sys
from sanitize_symbol import sanitize

TOP = Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json")
BAK = Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json.bak")

def main():
    if not TOP.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] {TOP} introuvable", file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(1)

    raw = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    # on gère les 2 structures possibles: objet {"symbols":[...]} ou liste brute [...]
    if isinstance(raw, dict):
        symbols = raw.get("symbols", [])
        changed, out = normalize_list(symbols)
        raw["symbols"] = out
        # si présent, on tente aussi de nettoyer d'autres champs potentiels
        for k in ("seeds", "pool", "bad", "mapped"):
            if isinstance(raw.get(k), list):
                _, cleaned = normalize_list(raw[k])
                raw[k] = cleaned
        if changed: write(raw)
        print(f"[top-fix] total={len(out)}  changed={changed}")
    elif isinstance(raw, list):
        changed, out = normalize_list(raw)
        if changed: write(out)
        print(f"[top-fix] total={len(out)}  changed={changed}")
    else:
        print("[WARN] format inconnu pour top.json (ni dict ni list)")

def normalize_list(lst):
    seen = set()
    out  = []
    changed = False
    for sym in lst:
        s0 = str(sym)
        s1 = sanitize(s0)
        if s1 != s0:
            changed = True
        if s1 not in seen:
            seen.add(s1)
            out.append(s1)
        else:
            changed = True
    # tri stable par ordre alpha pour reproductibilité
    out = sorted(out)
    return changed, out

def write(obj):
    if TOP.exists():
        BAK.write_text(TOP.read_text())
    TOP.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from indicators_tf import indicators_from_ohlcv
from ctx_logic import compute_ctx, CtxState

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); CAND=DATA/"candles"
STATE_DIR=DATA/"analysis_a_state"; STATE_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True, parents=True)
REQ=("5m","15m","30m")

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"; j=json.loads(f.read_text()); rows=j.get("data")
    if not rows: raise ValueError(f"empty {f}")
    return rows[-600:]

def load_state(sym):
    f=STATE_DIR/f"{sym}.json"
    if not f.exists(): return CtxState()
    try:
        j=json.loads(f.read_text()); 
        return CtxState(**{k:j.get(k) for k in ("ctx","streak_ctx","streak","bars_in_ctx")})
    except: return CtxState()

def save_state(sym, st: CtxState):
    (STATE_DIR/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(st.__dict__, indent=2))

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("args: SYMBOL [OUT_JSON]", file=sys.stderr); return 2
    sym = sys.argv[1]
    outp = Path(sys.argv[2]) if len(sys.argv)>2 else (DATA/"analysis_a"/f"{sym}.json")
    for tf in REQ:
        f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
        if not f.exists(): 
            print(f"[analysis_a] missing {f}", file=sys.stderr); return 3
    per_tf_inputs={tf: indicators_from_ohlcv(load_tf(sym, tf)) for tf in REQ}
    st_prev=load_state(sym)
    out = compute_ctx(per_tf_inputs, st_prev)
    save_state(sym, out["ctx_state"])
    S01 = (out["pb"] - out["ps"] + 1.0)/2.0
    payload = {
        "symbol": sym,
        "S": round(S01,4),
        "pb": out["pb"], "pH": out["ph"], "ps": out["ps"],
        "pb_i": out["ints"]["pb"], "pH_i": out["ints"]["ph"], "ps_i": out["ints"]["ps"],
        "context": out["ctx_state"].ctx,
        "reason": f"Sw={out['Sw']:.4f} perTF={ {k:round(v['S'],3) for k,v in out['per_tf'].items()} }"
    }
    outp.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    outp.write_text(json.dumps(payload, indent=2))
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from typing import Dict, Any

# Seuils en "dixièmes" (alignés avec pb_i, pH_i, ps_i = int(10*proba))
PB_ENTER = 7   # >=0.70
PS_ENTER = 7
PB_EXIT  = 4   # <=0.40
PS_EXIT  = 4

# Garde ATR% 5m
ATR5_MIN = 0.10   # %
ATR5_MAX = 3.00   # %

COOLDOWN_BARS = 2  # 2 bougies 5m

@dataclass
class PosState:
    pos: str = "flat"        # flat|long|short
    cooldown: int = 0
    last_ctx: str = "none"

def _ok_atr5(atrp5: float) -> bool:
    try:
        a = float(atrp5)
    except:
        return False
    return (ATR5_MIN <= a <= ATR5_MAX)

def decide_signal(a_rec: Dict[str,Any], feats: Dict[str,Any], state: PosState):
    """
    a_rec: ligne issue de analyse_A (keys: S, pb_i, pH_i, ps_i, context, reason)
    feats: dict avec 'atrp5' (ATR% 5m)
    state: PosState persistant
    Return: dict(side, action, strength, reason, new_state)
    """
    ctx = (a_rec.get("context") or "none")
    pb_i = int(a_rec.get("pb_i", 0))
    ph_i = int(a_rec.get("pH_i", 0))
    ps_i = int(a_rec.get("ps_i", 0))
    atr_ok = _ok_atr5(feats.get("atrp5", 0.0))

    # Cooldown
    if state.cooldown > 0:
        ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=state.cooldown-1, last_ctx=ctx)
        return dict(side="none", action="cooldown", strength=0,
                    reason=f"cooldown={state.cooldown}", new_state=ns)

    # Entrées
    if state.pos == "flat" and atr_ok:
        if ctx == "buy"  and pb_i >= PB_ENTER:
            ns = PosState(pos="long", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="buy", action="enter_long", strength=pb_i,
                        reason=f"ctx=buy pb_i={pb_i} atr5={feats.get('atrp5'):.3f}%", new_state=ns)
        if ctx == "sell" and ps_i >= PS_ENTER:
            ns = PosState(pos="short", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="sell", action="enter_short", strength=ps_i,
                        reason=f"ctx=sell ps_i={ps_i} atr5={feats.get('atrp5'):.3f}%", new_state=ns)

    # Sorties
    if state.pos == "long":
        if (ctx != "buy") or (pb_i <= PB_EXIT) or (ps_i >= PS_ENTER):
            ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=COOLDOWN_BARS, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="sell", action="exit_long", strength=max(10-ps_i, 1),
                        reason=f"exit_long ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i} ps_i={ps_i}", new_state=ns)
        return dict(side="none", action="hold_long", strength=pb_i,
                    reason=f"hold_long ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i}", new_state=state)

    if state.pos == "short":
        if (ctx != "sell") or (ps_i <= PS_EXIT) or (pb_i >= PB_ENTER):
            ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=COOLDOWN_BARS, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="buy", action="exit_short", strength=max(10-pb_i, 1),
                        reason=f"exit_short ctx={ctx} ps_i={ps_i} pb_i={pb_i}", new_state=ns)
        return dict(side="none", action="hold_short", strength=ps_i,
                    reason=f"hold_short ctx={ctx} ps_i={ps_i}", new_state=state)

    # Flat par défaut
    return dict(side="none", action="idle", strength=0,
                reason=f"no-entry atr_ok={atr_ok} ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i} ps_i={ps_i}",
                new_state=PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import os, json, asyncio
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
RUN  = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/b_run_coin.py")

WORKERS = int(os.getenv("B_WORKERS", "12"))
TIMEOUT = int(os.getenv("B_TIMEOUT_S", "90"))

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

async def run_one(sym, sem):
    async with sem:
        try:
            p = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
                "python3", str(RUN), sym,
                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL
            )
            await asyncio.wait_for(p.wait(), timeout=TIMEOUT)
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            try: p.kill()
            except: pass

async def main():
    top=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms=[s for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])][:30]
    if not syms: 
        print("[b] no symbols"); return
    sem=asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    await asyncio.gather(*[run_one(s, sem) for s in syms])
    print(f"[b] done symbols={len(syms)}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys, time, subprocess, shutil
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
RANK = DATA/"top_ranked.json"
SIGS = DATA/"signals.json"
POS  = DATA/"positions.json"
AOUT = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LOG  = Path("/opt/scalp/logs/top_rebuild.log")
SERVICE="scalp-top-lite.service"
TIMER="scalp-top-lite.timer"

def jload(p, d=None):
    try:
        return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception:
        return d

def age_sec(iso):
    try:
        dt = datetime.fromisoformat(iso.replace("Z","+00:00"))
        return max(0, (datetime.now(timezone.utc)-dt).total_seconds())
    except Exception:
        return 9e9

def box(ok=None):  # None -> pending
    return "✅" if ok is True else ("❌" if ok is False else "⏳")

def is_active(unit):
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(["systemctl","is-active","--quiet",unit])
        return r.returncode==0
    except Exception:
        return False

def short(txt, n=80):
    s=str(txt or "")
    return s if len(s)<=n else s[:n-1]+"…"

def pick_best_worst(rank_items, k=2):
    if not rank_items: return [], []
    items = sorted(rank_items, key=lambda x: float(x.get("score",0.0)), reverse=True)
    best = items[:k]
    worst = items[-k:][::-1]
    return best, worst

def get_metrics_for(sym):
    flat = sym
    # from analyse_A_out.json -> { "BTCUSDT": {"pb":..,"pH":..,"ps":..,"context":..,"reason":..}, ...}
    a = jload(AOUT, {})
    m = a.get(flat) or {}
    # fallback from signals.json last matching
    if not m and SIGS.exists():
        sj = jload(SIGS, [])
        for it in reversed(sj if isinstance(sj,list) else sj.get("items",[])):
            if (it.get("symbol") or it.get("sym") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")==flat:
                m = {k:it.get(k) for k in ("pb","pH","ps","context","reason")}
                break
    # coercion
    def f(x): 
        try: return float(x)
        except: return 0.0
    pb, pH, ps = f(m.get("pb")), f(m.get("pH")), f(m.get("ps"))
    ctx = m.get("context") or m.get("ctx") or ""
    reason = m.get("reason") or m.get("why") or ""
    return pb, pH, ps, ctx, reason

def main():
    top = jload(TOP, {})
    rank = jload(RANK, {})
    symbols = top.get("symbols") or []
    items = rank.get("items") or []
    gen = top.get("generated_at")
    fresh_ok = gen is not None and age_sec(gen) <= 3*3600 and len(symbols)>=5
    svc_ok = is_active(SERVICE)
    tmr_ok = is_active(TIMER)

    # sections
    print("=== Services ===")
    print(f"{box(tmr_ok)} timer: {TIMER}")
    print(f"{box(svc_ok)} service: {SERVICE}\n")

    print("=== Top30 ===")
    src = top.get("source") or "?"
    print(f"{box(fresh_ok)} ts={gen or 'n/a'}  src={src}  N={len(symbols)}")
    # aperçu top 10
    for i,it in enumerate(items[:10],1):
        s = it.get("symbol","?")
        sc = it.get("score",0.0)
        d = int(float(it.get("depth_quote_band",0))/1000)
        print(f"{i:02d}. {s:>10}  S={sc:0.4f}  depth≈{d}k")
    print()

    # Analyses: BTC, ETH + 2 best/2 worst
    best, worst = pick_best_worst(items, 2)
    focus = []
    for sym in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if sym in [it.get("symbol") for it in items] or sym in symbols:
            focus.append({"symbol": sym, "score": next((it.get('score') for it in items if it.get('symbol')==sym), 1.0)})
    focus += best + worst
    # de-dup en gardant ordre
    seen=set(); f2=[]
    for it in focus:
        sym = it.get("symbol","")
        if sym and sym not in seen:
            seen.add(sym); f2.append(it)

    print("=== Analyses (BTC, ETH, 2 best, 2 worst) ===")
    if not f2:
        print(f"{box(False)} aucune donnée d'analyse")
    else:
        for it in f2:
            s = it.get("symbol")
            sc = float(it.get("score",0.0))
            pb,pH,ps,ctx,why = get_metrics_for(s)
            P = int(10*pb); H = int(10*pH); S = int(10*ps)
            print(f"{box(True)} {s:>10}  S={sc:0.4f}  pb={P} pH={H} ps={S}  ctx={short(ctx,40)}  reason={short(why,60)}")
    print()

    # Données nécessaires / inputs
    need_ok = TOP.exists() and RANK.exists()
    print("=== Inputs ===")
    print(f"{box(TOP.exists())} {TOP}")
    print(f"{box(RANK.exists())} {RANK}")
    print(f"{box(SIGS.exists())} {SIGS}")
    print(f"{box(POS.exists())} {POS}")
    print(f"{box(LOG.exists())} {LOG}")
    print()

    # Derniers 5 signaux
    print("=== 5 derniers signaux ===")
    sj = jload(SIGS, [])
    sigs = sj if isinstance(sj,list) else sj.get("items",[])
    # heuristique d'ordre par timestamp/ts
    def ts_of(x):
        for k in ("ts","timestamp","time","at"): 
            if k in x: 
                try: return float(x[k])
                except: pass
        return 0.0
    sigs = sorted(sigs, key=ts_of, reverse=True)[:5]
    if not sigs:
        print("⏳ aucun")
    else:
        for it in sigs:
            sym = (it.get("symbol") or it.get("sym") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")
            side = (it.get("side") or it.get("action") or "?").upper()
            px = it.get("price") or it.get("px") or 0
            print(f"• {sym:>10}  {side:>4}  @ {px}")
    print()

    # Positions / historique bref
    print("=== Positions / historique bref ===")
    pj = jload(POS, {})
    poss = pj.get("positions") or pj.get("open") or []
    if poss:
        for it in poss[:5]:
            sym = (it.get("symbol") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")
            side = it.get("side") or it.get("direction") or "?"
            sz = it.get("size") or it.get("qty") or 0
            upnl = it.get("unrealizedPnl") or it.get("uPnL") or 0
            print(f"• {sym:>10} {side:>4} sz={sz} uPnL={upnl}")
    else:
        print("⏳ aucune position détectée")
    print()

    # Résumé final
    all_ok = fresh_ok and svc_ok and need_ok
    print(f"=== Résultat global: {box(all_ok)} ===")
----- FILE END -----

MTime: 2025-09-27 05:43:31.777894950 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import json, time, sys, math, datetime as dt

D = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP = D/"top.json"                      # liste des symbols
CAND = D/"candles"

# TFs à inspecter (mins)
TFS = [1,5,15,30]

def read_top():
    p = TOP
    if not p.exists():
        print("ERR: top.json introuvable", file=sys.stderr); return []
    try:
        j = json.loads(p.read_text())
        syms = j.get("symbols") or j.get("items") or []
        # items peut être dicts {'symbol': 'BTCUSDT'}
        if syms and isinstance(syms[0], dict):
            syms = [x.get("symbol") for x in syms if x.get("symbol")]
        return syms
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"ERR top.json: {e}", file=sys.stderr); return []

def load_last(sym, tfm):
    """
    essaie plusieurs chemins:
    - /candles/SYM/TF/last.json
    - /candles/TF/SYM.json
    - /candles/SYM/TF.json
    retourne (ts_ms, close) ou (None, None)
    """
    tf = f"{tfm}m"
    candidates = [
        CAND/sym/tf/"last.json",
        CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json",
        CAND/sym/f"{tf}.json",
    ]
    for p in candidates:
        if p.exists():
            try:
                j = json.loads(p.read_text())
                # format attendu: liste de bougies [t,o,h,l,c,v]
                if isinstance(j, list) and j and isinstance(j[-1], list):
                    t, *_rest, c = j[-1][0], *j[-1][1:-1], j[-1][-2]
                    return int(t), float(c)
                # ou objet {"data": [...]} 
                if isinstance(j, dict) and "data" in j and j["data"]:
                    row = j["data"][-1]
                    t, c = int(row[0]), float(row[4])
                    return t, c
            except Exception:
                pass
    return None, None

def fmt_age(s):
    m, s = divmod(int(s), 60)
    h, m = divmod(m, 60)
    if h: return f"{h}h{m:02d}m"
    if m: return f"{m}m{s:02d}s"
    return f"{s}s"

def due_status(now, last_ts_ms, tfm):
    tf_sec = tfm*60
    # "due" quand la bougie (close) est attendue au prochain multiple de tf
    # et que l'âge dépasse ~90% du tf (proche clôture)
    if last_ts_ms is None: return "MISSING"
    last_close_sec = last_ts_ms//1000
    age = now - last_close_sec
    nxt = (last_close_sec//tf_sec + 1)*tf_sec
    secs_to_next = max(0, nxt - now)
    # statut
    if age < tf_sec*0.1:
        return f"fresh -{fmt_age(tf_sec-age)}"
    # align info “not due / due soon”
    tag = "due" if secs_to_next==0 else "not_due"
    return f"{tag} T-{secs_to_next}s"

def main():
    syms = read_top()
    if not syms:
        print("Aucun symbole dans top.json"); return
    now = int(time.time())
    print("== TF LOAD VISU ==")
    print("ts_now:", dt.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(now).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ"))
    print(f"symbols={len(syms)}   tfs={TFS}\n")
    header = f"{'coin':10} {'tf':>4} {'last(UTC)':>19} {'age':>8} {'status':>12} {'close':>12}"
    print(header)
    print("-"*len(header))
    miss=0
    for sym in syms:
        for tfm in TFS:
            ts_ms, close = load_last(sym, tfm)
            if ts_ms is None:
                miss+=1
                print(f"{sym:10} {tfm:>4} {'-':>19} {'-':>8} {'MISSING':>12} {'-':>12}")
                continue
            last = ts_ms//1000
            age = now - last
            status = due_status(now, ts_ms, tfm)
            iso = dt.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(last).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
            print(f"{sym:10} {tfm:>4} {iso:>19} {fmt_age(age):>8} {status:>12} {close:12.6f}")
    print("\nMISSING files:", miss)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
for s in sys.argv[1:]:
    p1=C/"1m"/f"{s}.json"; p3=C/"3m"/f"{s}.json"
    if not p1.exists(): continue
    a=json.loads(p1.read_text()); out=[]
    for i in range(0, len(a)//3*3, 3):
        g=a[i:i+3]
        ts=g[0][0]; o=g[0][1]; c=g[-1][4]
        h=max(x[2] for x in g); l=min(x[3] for x in g)
        v=sum(x[5] for x in g)
        out.append([ts,o,h,l,c,v])
    p3.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p3.write_text(json.dumps(out))
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
A=DATA/"analysis_a"
rows=[]
for f in sorted(A.glob("*.json")):
    j=json.loads(f.read_text())
    ctx=(j.get("context") or "none").lower()
    S=float(j.get("S") or 0)
    rows.append((ctx,S,f.stem))
tot=len(rows)
from collections import Counter
cnt=Counter(r[0] for r in rows)
print("A files:", tot, " | ", " ".join(f"{k}={cnt.get(k,0)}" for k in ("buy","sell","hold","none")))
rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)
print("\nTOP S:")
for ctx,S,sym in rows[:10]:
    print(f"{sym:10} S={S:.2f} ctx={ctx}")
print("\nNON-NONE:")
for ctx,S,sym in [r for r in rows if r[0]!="none"][:10]:
    print(f"{sym:10} S={S:.2f} ctx={ctx}")

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

BASE="/opt/scalp/data/candles"
# TF autorisés
TF=(1m 3m 5m 10m 15m 30m)

echo "[1/4] Vérif dossiers TF"
mkdir -p "$BASE"
for t in "${TF[@]}"; do
  mkdir -p "$BASE/$t"
done

echo "[2/4] Suppression de tous les JSON (y compris noms corrompus avec retours à la ligne)"
# -print0 gère les noms bizarres, xargs -0 supprime sans erreur
find "$BASE" -type f -name '*.json' -print0 | xargs -0r rm -f --

echo "[3/4] Suppression des dossiers au niveau racine qui ne sont pas des TF"
# liste blanche -> tout le reste est supprimé
shopt -s nullglob
for d in "$BASE"/*/; do
  name="$(basename "$d")"
  keep=0
  for t in "${TF[@]}"; do
    [[ "$name" == "$t" ]] && keep=1 && break
  done
  if [[ $keep -eq 0 ]]; then
    echo "  - rm -rf $d"
    rm -rf -- "$d"
  fi
done
shopt -u nullglob

echo "[4/4] Nettoyage des sous-dossiers vides restants"
find "$BASE" -type d -empty -mindepth 1 -delete

echo "OK. Structure cible à utiliser: $BASE/<TF>/<COIN>.json"
printf 'TF présents: '; ls -1 "$BASE" | paste -sd',' -

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, asyncio, sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
A_CMD = os.environ.get("A_CMD","python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py {sym}")
B_CMD = os.environ.get("B_CMD","python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py {sym}")
# compteur de bougies à fetch si ton fetcher en a besoin
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("CANDLES_LIMIT","600"))

# --- planification TF dues en fonction de l'horloge UTC ---
def due_tfs():
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    m = now.minute
    return {
        "1m":  True,                   # 1m toujours
        "3m":  (m % 3  == 0),          # si jamais utilisée
        "5m":  (m % 5  == 0),
        "15m": (m % 15 == 0),
        "30m": (m % 30 == 0),
    }

# --- fetch OHLCV pour un symbole et une TF ---
async def fetch_tf(sym:str, tf:str):
    # appelle ton outil de rafraîchissement; adapte si besoin
    # on n'exécute QUE si TF due
    from subprocess import CalledProcessError, run
    try:
        # remplace par ton fetcher interne si différent
        # exemple: python3 /opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh_top_async.py --sym BTCUSDT --tf 15m --limit 600
        cmd = ["python3","/opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh_one.py","--sym",sym,"--tf",tf,"--limit",str(LIMIT)]
        r = run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
        if r.returncode==0:
            print(f"[OK] {sym} {tf} {LIMIT}")
        else:
            sys.stderr.write(f"[ERR] {sym} {tf} {r.returncode} {r.stderr.strip()}\n")
    except FileNotFoundError:
        # si tu n'as pas de fetcher one-shot, ignorer proprement
        print(f"[SKIP-FETCH] no fetcher for {sym} {tf}")

# --- pipeline A puis B pour un symbole ---
async def run_sym(sym:str, tfdue:dict):
    # 1) fetch minimaux pour A (A ne dépend que de 5m/15m/30m)
    tasks=[]
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        if tfdue.get(tf, False):
            tasks.append(fetch_tf(sym, tf))
        else:
            print(f"[SKIP] {sym} {tf} not due")
    if tasks:
        await asyncio.gather(*tasks)

    # 2) Analyse A
    os.system(A_CMD.format(sym=sym))

    # 3) Si contexte déclenche B, le wrapper B_CMD décidera lui-même 1m/3m/5m pour l’entrée
    os.system(B_CMD.format(sym=sym))

async def main():
    tfdue = due_tfs()
    print(f"=== fetch_A_then_B @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ')}  "
          f"due: 5m={int(tfdue['5m'])} 15m={int(tfdue['15m'])} 30m={int(tfdue['30m'])} ===")
    top = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    symbols = top.get("symbols", [])
    # parallélisme
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(int(os.environ.get("MAX_PAR", "6")))
    async def guard(s):
        async with sem: await run_sym(s, tfdue)
    await asyncio.gather(*(guard(s) for s in symbols))
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}
PAPER="$DATA/paper"
BRDBG="$DATA/debug/bridge"
TS=$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)
CASH=${PAPER_BUDGET:-200.0}

mkdir -p "$PAPER" "$BRDBG" "$DATA/signals_coin"

# backups si présents
for f in "$DATA/signals.json" "$PAPER/positions.json" "$PAPER/balance.json"; do
  [[ -s "${f:-}" ]] && cp -a "$f" "$f.bak.$TS" || true
done

# reset des états
printf '[]\n' > "$DATA/signals.json"
printf '[]\n' > "$PAPER/positions.json"
printf '{ "cash": %.2f }\n' "$CASH" > "$PAPER/balance.json"
: > "$PAPER/cooldown.json" 2>/dev/null || true

# purge debug/anciennes sorties
rm -f "$BRDBG"/*.log 2>/dev/null || true
rm -f "$DATA/signals_coin"/*.json 2>/dev/null || true

# sanity rapide (sans jq requis)
echo "[reset] OK  -> cash=$(sed -n 's/.*"cash":[[:space:]]*\([0-9.]\+\).*/\1/p' "$PAPER/balance.json")"
echo "signals=$(wc -c <"$DATA/signals.json") bytes, positions=$(wc -c <"$PAPER/positions.json") bytes"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Analyse B durcie : pré-filtres 1m, triggers PB/BO/MR, anti-bruit, sizing, sécurité.
# Entrées:
#   - OHLCV 1m/3m/5m : /opt/scalp/data/candles/<tf>/<SYMBOL>.json
#   - Contexte A      : /opt/scalp/data/analyse_A_out.json
#   - Règles paires   : /opt/scalp/data/contracts_usdt.json  (min_notional, lot_step …) [optionnel]
# Sorties:
#   - /opt/scalp/data/analyse_B_out.json
#   - append -> /opt/scalp/data/signals.json

import json, math, time, statistics
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"
STATE  = DATA/"state"; STATE.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
SIGF   = DATA/"signals.json"
AOUT   = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
BOUT   = DATA/"analyse_B_out.json"
PAIRDB = DATA/"contracts_usdt.json"   # {symbol: {minNotional, lotStep, ...}}
CFGSTR = Path("/etc/scalp.strategy")

# ---------- Utils IO ----------
def jload(p, d=None):
    p=Path(p)
    if not p.exists(): return d
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except: return d

def jappend(p, item):
    arr = jload(p, [])
    arr.append(item)
    Path(p).write_text(json.dumps(arr, ensure_ascii=False))

def jsave(p, obj):
    p=Path(p); p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_complete(arr, tf_s):
    if not arr: return []
    now = __import__('time').time()*1000
    # si la dernière bougie n'est pas close on l'enlève
    if now - arr[-1][0] < tf_s*1000:
        return arr[:-1]
    return arr[:-1] if (now - arr[-1][0] < tf_s*1000) else arr

def close(a): return [x[4] for x in a]
def high(a):  return [x[2] for x in a]
def low(a):   return [x[3] for x in a]
def vol(a):   return [x[5] for x in a]
def tp(a):    return [(x[2]+x[3]+x[4])/3 for x in a]

# ---------- Indicators ----------
def ema(vals, n):
    k=2/(n+1); out=[]; e=None
    for v in vals:
        e = v if e is None else (v - e)*k + e
        out.append(e)
    return out

def rsi(vals, n=14):
    if len(vals)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(vals)
    gains=[0.0]; losses=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(vals)):
        d=vals[i]-vals[i-1]
        gains.append(max(d,0)); losses.append(max(-d,0))
    avg_gain=sum(gains[1:n+1])/n; avg_loss=sum(losses[1:n+1])/n
    rsis=[50.0]*(n)
    for i in range(n+1,len(vals)+1):
        avg_gain=(avg_gain*(n-1)+gains[i-1])/n
        avg_loss=(avg_loss*(n-1)+losses[i-1])/n
        rs= (avg_gain/avg_loss) if avg_loss>0 else 0
        r=100-(100/(1+rs)) if avg_loss>0 else 100
        rsis.append(r)
    return rsis

def true_range(h,l,c_prev): return max(h-l, abs(h-c_prev), abs(l-c_prev))
def atr(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    trs=[]
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: trs.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: trs.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    out=[]; a=None; k=2/(n+1)
    for tr in trs:
        a = tr if a is None else (tr-a)*k + a
        out.append(a)
    return out

def adx(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    if len(cs)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(cs)
    pdm=[0.0]; ndm=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cs)):
        up=hs[i]-hs[i-1]; dn=ls[i-1]-ls[i]
        pdm.append(up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0)
        ndm.append(dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0)
    tr = []
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: tr.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: tr.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    def rma(x,n):
        k=1/n; out=[]; a=None
        for v in x:
            a = v if a is None else a + k*(v-a)
            out.append(a)
        return out
    atrv=rma(tr,n); pdi=[0.0]*len(cs); ndi=[0.0]*len(cs)
    p=rma(pdm,n); n_=rma(ndm,n)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if atrv[i]>0:
            pdi[i]=100*p[i]/atrv[i]; ndi[i]=100*n_[i]/atrv[i]
    dx=[0.0]*len(cs)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        s=pdi[i]+ndi[i]; dx[i]= (100*abs(pdi[i]-ndi[i])/s) if s>0 else 0.0
    return rma(dx,n)

def macd_hist(vals, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    e1=ema(vals,f); e2=ema(vals,s)
    macd=[e1[i]-e2[i] for i in range(len(vals))]
    sigl=ema(macd,sig)
    return [macd[i]-sigl[i] for i in range(len(vals))]

def bb(vals, n=20, k=2.0):
    if len(vals)<n: return [None]*len(vals), [None]*len(vals), [None]*len(vals)
    ma=[]; dev=[]
    for i in range(len(vals)):
        if i<n-1:
            ma.append(None); dev.append(None)
        else:
            w=vals[i-n+1:i+1]
            m=sum(w)/n
            v=(sum((x-m)**2 for x in w)/n)**0.5
            ma.append(m); dev.append(v)
    upper=[(ma[i]+k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    lower=[(ma[i]-k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    return upper, lower, ma

def keltner(hs, ls, cs, n=20, k=1.5):
    ema_c=ema(cs,n)
    atrv=atr(hs,ls,cs,n)
    upper=[ema_c[i]+k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    lower=[ema_c[i]-k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    return upper, lower, ema_c

def obv(cl, vo):
    o=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        if cl[i]>cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]+vo[i])
        elif cl[i]<cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]-vo[i])
        else: o.append(o[-1])
    return o

def vwap(arr, n=20):
    tpv=tp(arr); v=vol(arr)
    out=[]; num=0.0; den=0.0
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        num += tpv[i]*v[i]; den += v[i]
        out.append(num/den if den>0 else tpv[i])
        if i>=n:
            num -= tpv[i-n]*v[i-n]; den -= v[i-n]
    return out

# ---------- Strategy params (override via /etc/scalp.strategy) ----------
PARAM = {
  "risk_pct": 0.003,           # 0.3%
  "leverage": 5,
  "min_notional": 5.0,
  "max_pair_expo_pct": 0.25,
  "lot_step": 0.0001,
  "cooldown_1m": 5,            # 5×1m
  "N_breakout": 20,
  "vol_mult_pullback": 1.3
}
if CFGSTR.exists():
    for ln in CFGSTR.read_text().splitlines():
        ln=ln.strip()
        if not ln or ln.startswith("#"): continue
        k,v = ln.split("=",1)
        try: PARAM[k]=float(v) if "." in v or v.isdigit() else v
        except: PARAM[k]=v

# ---------- Pair rules ----------
def get_pair_rules(sym):
    d = jload(PAIRDB, {})
    r = (d or {}).get(sym, {})
    return {
        "min_notional": float(r.get("minNotional", PARAM["min_notional"])),
        "lot_step":    float(r.get("lotStep",    PARAM["lot_step"]))
    }

# ---------- Préfiltres durcis ----------
def median_spread_1m(m1, k=5):
    """Médiane sur k dernières 1m du (H-L)/C ; supprime bruit bougie unique."""
    if not m1: return 1.0
    k = min(k, len(m1))
    cs = close(m1); hs=high(m1); ls=low(m1)
    arr=[]
    for i in range(len(cs)-k, len(cs)):
        if cs[i] <= 0: continue
        arr.append( (hs[i]-ls[i]) / cs[i] )
    return statistics.median(arr) if arr else 1.0

def prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5):
    # Vol 1m
    c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
    atr1=atr(h1,l1,c1,14)
    atrpct1 = (atr1[-1]/c1[-1])*100 if c1 and atr1[-1] else 0.0
    if atrpct1 < 0.10: return False, "atr1%<0.10"

    # Cooldown
    cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {}).get(sym, 0)
    if int(time.time()) < cd: return False, "cooldown"

    # Spread médian 3–5 bougies
    spr = median_spread_1m(m1, k=5)
    if spr > 0.010: return False, "spread>1%"

    return True, "ok"

# ---------- Evidences (0/1) ----------
def macd_accel(vals):
    h=macd_hist(vals)
    if len(h)<4: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (h[-1]>h[-2]>h[-3]) else 0.0

def squeeze_ok(hs,ls,cs):
    bu,bl,_ = bb(cs,20,2.0); ku,kl,_ = keltner(hs,ls,cs,20,1.5)
    if bu[-1] is None: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (bu[-1]-bl[-1]) < (ku[-1]-kl[-1]) else 0.0

def evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5):
    # N=20 en 3m => ~60m de range ; ADX(14) sur 5m
    c3=close(m3)
    if len(c3)<22: return 0.0
    N=int(PARAM["N_breakout"])
    hh=max(c3[-N-1:-1]); ll=min(c3[-N-1:-1])
    adx5 = adx(high(m5), low(m5), close(m5), 14)[-1] if m5 else 0.0
    accel = macd_accel(c3)
    sq = squeeze_ok(high(m3),low(m3),c3)
    if ctx=="buy"  and c3[-1]>hh and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    if ctx=="sell" and c3[-1]<ll and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    return 0.0

def evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3):
    c1=close(m1); v1=vol(m1); e20=ema(c1,20)
    up,lo,_ = bb(c1,20,2.0); vw= vwap(m1,20)
    rsi7=rsi(c1,7); vavg20=sum(v1[-20:])/max(1,len(v1[-20:]))
    if ctx=="buy":
        touch = ((lo[-1] is not None and c1[-1]<=lo[-1]) or c1[-1]<=e20[-1] or c1[-1]<=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]<=45
    elif ctx=="sell":
        touch = ((up[-1] is not None and c1[-1]>=up[-1]) or c1[-1]>=e20[-1] or c1[-1]>=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]>=55
    else:
        return 0.0
    volok = (v1[-1] >= PARAM["vol_mult_pullback"]*vavg20)
    return 1.0 if (touch and side and volok) else 0.0

def candle_reversal(c):
    if len(c)<3: return False
    b2,b1,c0 = c[-3],c[-2],c[-1]
    return (c0<b1 and b1>b2) or (c0>b1 and b1<b2)

def evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1):
    # Un seul sens par bougie: priorité au côté touché
    c1=close(m1); up,lo,_ = bb(c1,20,2.0); r7=rsi(c1,7)
    if up[-1] is None: return 0.0
    touched_up   = c1[-1]>=up[-1]
    touched_low  = c1[-1]<=lo[-1]
    if ctx!="hold": return 0.0
    if touched_up and not touched_low:
        return 1.0 if (r7[-1]>=60 and candle_reversal(c1)) else 0.0
    if touched_low and not touched_up:
        return 1.0 if (r7[-1]<=40 and candle_reversal(c1)) else 0.0
    # Si les deux ou aucun: pas d’ordre MR pour éviter double-sens
    return 0.0

# ---------- Entry scoring ----------
def entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx):
    if not (m1 and m3 and m5): return 0.0
    e1 = evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1)
    e3 = evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5)
    e5 = evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3)
    return 0.5*e5 + 0.3*e3 + 0.2*e1

# ---------- Sizing ----------
def round_step(q, step):
    if step<=0: return q
    return math.floor(q/step)*step

def size_order(sym, price, sl, balance, risk_pct, leverage, max_pair_expo_pct):
    rules = get_pair_rules(sym)
    min_notional = rules["min_notional"]
    lot_step     = rules["lot_step"]

    D = abs(price - sl)
    if D<=0: return 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0
    risk_usd = balance * risk_pct
    qty = risk_usd / D
    notional = qty * price

    if notional < min_notional:
        qty = min_notional / price
        notional = min_notional

    max_notional = balance * max_pair_expo_pct * leverage
    if notional > max_notional:
        qty = max_notional / price
        notional = max_notional

    qty = round_step(qty, lot_step)
    margin = notional / leverage
    return qty, notional, margin, risk_usd

# ---------- Mapping contexte A -> B ----------
def map_ctx_a_to_b(ctx_a):
    m = {"bullish":"buy", "bearish":"sell", "range":"hold"}
    return m.get(ctx_a, "none")

# ---------- Main per-symbol ----------
def analyze_symbol(sym, ctx_a, m1, m3, m5, balance=200.0):
    ok, why = prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5)
    if not ok: return {"symbol": sym, "ctx": "none", "why": why}

    ctx = map_ctx_a_to_b(ctx_a)

    score = entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx)

    # Veto 5m directionnel (EMA9-21)
    e9=ema(close(m5),9); e21=ema(close(m5),21)
    S5 = (e9[-1]-e21[-1])
    if ctx=="buy" and S5<0:  score = min(score, 0.59)
    if ctx=="sell" and S5>0: score = min(score, 0.59)

    # Persistance 2×1m
    pst=jload(STATE/"persist_B.json", {})
    st=pst.get(sym, {"score_ge":0})
    st["score_ge"] = st.get("score_ge",0)+1 if score>=0.60 else 0
    pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)

    signal=None
    if st["score_ge"]>=2:
        c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
        atr1 = atr(h1,l1,c1,14)[-1]
        entry = c1[-1]
        if ctx=="buy":
            sl = entry - 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry + 1.8*atr1
        elif ctx=="sell":
            sl = entry + 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry - 1.8*atr1
        else:
            # MR: pas d’ordre sans contexte clair -> garder neutre
            sl = entry; tp = entry

        qty, notion, margin, risk_usd = size_order(
            sym, entry, sl, balance,
            risk_pct=PARAM["risk_pct"],
            leverage=PARAM["leverage"],
            max_pair_expo_pct=PARAM["max_pair_expo_pct"]
        )

        if qty>0 and ctx in ("buy","sell"):
            signal = {
                "ts": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", time.gmtime()),
                "symbol": sym,
                "side": "buy" if ctx=="buy" else "sell",
                "entry": round(entry,6),
                "sl": round(sl,6),
                "tp": round(tp,6),
                "qty": qty,
                "notional": round(notion,2),
                "margin": round(margin,2),
                "risk_usd": round(risk_usd,2),
                "why": f"B:score>=0.60x2|ctxA={ctx_a}",
                "sl_type": "stop-market",        # exécution hard côté exchange
                "timeout_s": 25*60,              # 25×1m
                "trail_arm_at": round(1.0*atr1,6),
                "trail_step_atr": 1.0            # trailing 1×ATR après +1×ATR
            }
            # cooldown
            cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {})
            cd[sym] = int(time.time()) + int(PARAM["cooldown_1m"])*60
            jsave(STATE/"cooldown.json", cd)
            # reset persistence
            st["score_ge"]=0; pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)
            # append signal
            jappend(SIGF, signal)

    return {"symbol": sym, "ctxA": ctx_a, "ctx": ctx, "score": round(score,3), "signal": signal}

# ---------- Batch runner ----------
def load_tf(sym, tf):
    from pathlib import Path, PurePath as PP; import json
    DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
    tfsec={'1m':60,'3m':180,'5m':300,'15m':900,'30m':1800}.get(tf,60)
    f=C/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    if not f.exists(): return []
    a=json.loads(f.read_text())
    return last_complete(a, tfsec) 60)
    elif tf=="3m":  return last_complete(a, 180)
    elif tf=="5m":  return last_complete(a, 300)
    else: return a

def run_for_top(top_syms, balance=200.0):
    ctxA = jload(AOUT, {})
    out=[]
    for sym in top_syms:
        rec = ctxA.get(sym, {})
        ctxa = rec.get("context") or rec.get("ctx") or rec.get("trend") or "none"
        m1 = load_tf(sym,"1m"); m3 = load_tf(sym,"3m"); m5 = load_tf(sym,"5m")
        out.append(analyze_symbol(sym, ctxa, m1, m3, m5, balance=balance))
    jsave(BOUT, out)
    return out

if __name__ == "__main__":
    top = (jload(DATA/"top.json", {}) or {}).get("symbols", []) or []
    run_for_top(top[:30], balance=(jload(DATA/"paper_balance.json",{"balance":200.0})["balance"]))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
TOP=json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())["symbols"][:30]

def last_ts(p):
    try:
        a=json.loads(p.read_text()); return int(a[-1][0]) if a else 0
    except Exception: return 0

def age(ts): 
    return max(0,int(time.time()*1000-ts)//1000)

def fmt(a): 
    return f"{a//3600:02d}:{(a%3600)//60:02d}"

print(f"{'symbol':6s} {'5m':>5s} {'15m':>5s} {'30m':>5s}  (âge en mm:ss)")
for s in TOP:
    a5=age(last_ts(C/'5m'/f"{s}.json"))
    a15=age(last_ts(C/'15m'/f"{s}.json"))
    a30=age(last_ts(C/'30m'/f"{s}.json"))
    print(f"{s.replace('USDT',''):6s} {fmt(a5):>5s} {fmt(a15):>5s} {fmt(a30):>5s}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, math
from urllib.request import urlopen, Request
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.error import URLError, HTTPError

BASE="https://api.bitget.com"

def _http_json(path, params=None, tries=3, timeout=10):
    if params: path += ("?" + urlencode(params))
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            with urlopen(Request(BASE+path, headers={"User-Agent":"scalp/1"}), timeout=timeout) as r:
                raw=r.read().decode("utf-8")
                return json.loads(raw)
        except (URLError, HTTPError):
            if i+1>=tries: raise
            time.sleep(0.6*(2**i))

def ticker_last(symbol:str)->float|None:
    # v2
    j=_http_json("/api/v2/mix/market/ticker", {"symbol":symbol})
    data=j.get("data") or {}
    p=data.get("lastPr") or data.get("last") or data.get("close")
    try: return float(p)
    except: return None

def klines(symbol:str, granularity:int, limit:int=300):
    # try v2 first
    j=_http_json("/api/v2/mix/market/candles", {"symbol":symbol,"granularity":granularity,"limit":limit})
    data=j.get("data")
    if not data:
        j=_http_json("/api/mix/v1/market/candles", {"symbol":symbol,"granularity":granularity,"limit":limit})
        data=j.get("data")
    rows=[]
    # Bitget renvoie récents→anciens sous forme ["ts","open","high","low","close","volume"]
    for r in (data or []):
        try:
            ts=int(r[0])
            o,h,l,c=map(float,(r[1],r[2],r[3],r[4]))
            rows.append((ts,o,h,l,c))
        except: continue
    rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[0])  # ancien→récent
    return rows

# util
def tf_to_seconds(tf:str)->int:
    m={"1m":60,"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800,"1h":3600}
    return m.get(tf,60)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, ccxt, hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
F_OK=DATA/"coins_90d.json"
F_PEN=DATA/"coins_pending.json"
F_TOP=DATA/"top.json"
F_FIX=Path("/etc/scalp.fixed_top.json")

RUN=Path("/opt/scalp/run"); RUN.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
CACHE_DIR=RUN/"ohlcv_cache"; CACHE_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

LIMIT=int(os.getenv("TUNE_TOP_OHLCV_LIMIT","48"))      # nb bougies 1h stockées
WORKERS=int(os.getenv("TUNE_TOP_WORKERS","6"))         # parallélisme

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX=ex()

def load_list(p):
    try:
        j=json.loads(Path(p).read_text() or "{}")
        return j if isinstance(j,list) else (j.get("symbols") or [])
    except: return []

def load_fixed():
    try:
        j=json.loads(F_FIX.read_text()); lst=j.get("symbols",[])
        return [s for s in lst if isinstance(s,str)]
    except: return []

def universe():
    seen=set(); out=[]
    for s in load_fixed()+load_list(F_OK)+load_list(F_TOP)+load_list(F_PEN):
        if s and s not in seen:
            out.append(s); seen.add(s)
    return out

def ccxt_symbol(bitget_id:str)->str:
    return bitget_id.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT")

def cache_path(sym:str)->Path:
    h=hashlib.sha1(sym.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
    return CACHE_DIR/f"{h}.json"

def refresh_one(sym:str)->bool:
    try:
        ohlcv=EX.fetch_ohlcv(ccxt_symbol(sym), timeframe="1h", limit=LIMIT)
        cache_path(sym).write_text(json.dumps({"ts":time.time(),"data":ohlcv}))
        return True
    except Exception:
        return False

def main():
    U=universe()
    ok=0
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS) as tp:
        fut={tp.submit(refresh_one,s):s for s in U}
        for f in as_completed(fut):
            ok += 1 if f.result() else 0
    print(f"[ohlcv_refresh] universe={len(U)} updated={ok} limit={LIMIT} workers={WORKERS}")
    (RUN/"ohlcv_refresh.stamp").write_text(str(int(time.time())))
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
DEBUG = DATA/"debug"
RUN = Path("/opt/scalp/run")
LOCKDIR = RUN/"locks"
DEBUG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
LOCKDIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def load_top_symbols():
    top_path = DATA/"top.json"
    if not top_path.exists():
        return []
    try:
        j = json.loads(top_path.read_text())
        return (j.get("symbols") or [])[:30]
    except Exception:
        return []

def lock_path(sym): 
    return LOCKDIR/f"A_{sym}.lock"

def safe_run(sym:str)->tuple[str,bool,str]:
    p = lock_path(sym)
    try:
        fd = os.open(p, os.O_CREAT|os.O_EXCL|os.O_RDWR)
    except FileExistsError:
        return (sym, False, "locked")
    try:
        rc = os.system(f"/usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py {sym} >/dev/null 2>&1")
        ok = (os.WEXITSTATUS(rc)==0)
        return (sym, ok, "done")
    finally:
        try: os.close(fd); os.unlink(p)
        except: pass

def main():
    symbols = load_top_symbols()
    if not symbols:
        Path(DEBUG/"a_pool.json").write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),"ok":0,"err":0,"skipped":0,"note":"empty top.json"}, indent=2))
        print("[A-pool] empty top.json")
        return
    workers = max(1, min(os.cpu_count() or 2, 6))
    stats={"ok":0,"err":0,"skipped":0}
    with ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=workers) as px:
        fut = {px.submit(safe_run, s): s for s in symbols}
        for f in as_completed(fut):
            sym, ok, why = f.result()
            if why=="locked": stats["skipped"]+=1
            elif ok: stats["ok"]+=1
            else: stats["err"]+=1
    tmp = DEBUG/".a_pool.tmp"
    final = DEBUG/"a_pool.json"
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),**stats}, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(final)
    print(f"[A-pool] {stats}")

if __name__=="__main__": 
    main()

----- CONTENT -----
import time, math
TF_SEC = {"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800}

def last_closed_epoch(tf:str)->int:
    step = TF_SEC[tf]
    now  = int(time.time())
    return (now//step - 1)*step  # dernière bougie FERMÉE

def ttl_left(tf:str)->int:
    step = TF_SEC[tf]
    now  = int(time.time())
    next_close = (now//step + 0)*step  # fin de la bougie courante
    return max(0, next_close - now)

def since_for(tf:str, bars:int)->int:
    end = last_closed_epoch(tf)
    return (end - (bars-1)*TF_SEC[tf])

import json, time
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
TTL={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}
def last_ts(tf):
    latest=0
    for f in (C/tf).glob("*.json"):
        try:
            arr=json.loads(f.read_text())
            if isinstance(arr,list) and arr:
                ts=int(arr[-1][0])//1000
                if ts>latest: latest=ts
        except: pass
    return latest
def probe(tf):
    ts=last_ts(tf)
    age=int(time.time())-ts if ts else 1_000_000_000
    return {"tf":tf,"age_s":age,"ok":age<TTL[tf],"last_ts":ts}
out={"ts":int(time.time()),"fresh":[probe(tf) for tf in ("30m","15m","5m")]}
print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))

MTime: 2025-09-25 15:17:45.773233160 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"
TOP    = (DATA/"top.json").read_text()
SYMS   = json.loads(TOP).get("symbols", [])[:30]  # top strict

PERIOD = {"5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}

def worst(tf, syms):
    now = int(time.time())
    stale, bad = 0, []
    for s in syms:
        p = CAND/tf/f"{s}.json"
        if not p.exists():
            bad.append((s,"missing")); stale += 1; continue
        try:
            a = json.loads(p.read_text())
            ts = a[-1][0]//1000 if a else 0
        except Exception:
            bad.append((s,"corrupt")); stale += 1; continue
        lag = max(0, now - ts)
        if lag > PERIOD[tf] + 30:
            bad.append((s, lag)); stale += 1
    worst_lag = max([v for _,v in bad if isinstance(v,int)] or [0])
    return {"tf":tf, "worst_lag":worst_lag, "stale":stale, "bad":bad}

def main():
    out = {"ts": int(time.time()), "checks": []}
    ok = True
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        r = worst(tf, SYMS)
        out["checks"].append(r)
        if r["stale"]>0: ok = False
    print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
    sys.exit(0 if ok else 1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import asyncio, time, random
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Config: adapte selon la rateLimit de l’exchange (en ms)
RATE_LIMIT_MS = 200
MAX_INFLIGHT  = max(1, 1000//RATE_LIMIT_MS)
FETCH_WORKERS = min(8, MAX_INFLIGHT)

_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=FETCH_WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(MAX_INFLIGHT)

async def throttled_call(loop, func, *args, **kwargs):
    async with _sem:
        t0 = time.time()
        res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: func(*args, **kwargs))
        # respect rate-limit + jitter
        delay = max(0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - (time.time()-t0))
        if delay>0: await asyncio.sleep(delay + random.uniform(0,0.05))
        return res

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -a
[ -f /etc/scalp.env ] && source /etc/scalp.env
[ -z "${TELEGRAM_TOKEN:-}" ] && [ -n "${TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN:-}" ] && export TELEGRAM_TOKEN="$TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN"
[ -n "${CHAT_ID:-}" ] && export TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID="$CHAT_ID"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOPF=DATA/"top.json"
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
CAND=DATA/"candles"

TTL={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}
SAFETY=60   # on exige au moins 60s de validité restante pour ✅

def j(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def last_ts_tf(tf, symbols):
    mx=0; missing=[]
    for s in symbols:
        f=CAND/f"{tf}/{s}.json"
        try:
            arr=json.loads(f.read_text())
            if arr: mx=max(mx, arr[-1][0]//1000)
            else: missing.append(s)
        except Exception:
            missing.append(s)
    return mx, missing

def left_str(sec):
    sec=max(0,int(sec))
    return f"{sec//60:02d}m{sec%60:02d}s"

def main():
    top=j(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
    n=len(syms)

    now=int(time.time())
    # Data freshness per TF
    lefts={}
    oks={}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        ts,_=last_ts_tf(tf, syms)
        left = TTL[tf] - (now - ts)
        lefts[tf]=max(0,left)
        oks[tf] = lefts[tf] >= SAFETY

    # Analyse A freshness vs data
    a=j(AOUT, {"generated_at":"", "max_data_ts":0, "results":[]})
    try:
        ats=int(time.mktime(time.strptime(a["generated_at"], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")))
    except Exception:
        ats=0
    a_left = max(0, TTL["5m"] - (now - ats))
    # ok seulement si data 5/15/30 sont OK et analyse >= max_data_ts
    a_ok = all(oks.values()) and (ats >= a.get("max_data_ts",0))

    # lignes header
    print("# Dashboard")
    print(f"Top>90j {left_str(  (90*24*3600) ):>s} ✅ | Top30 {left_str(max(0,int(top.get('keep',30))*3600 - (now - 0)))} ✅  n={n:>2d} ✅")
    print(f"Data :  30m {left_str(lefts['30m'])} {'✅' if oks['30m'] else '❌'}  |  15m {left_str(lefts['15m'])} {'✅' if oks['15m'] else '❌'}  |  5m  {left_str(lefts['5m'])} {'✅' if oks['5m'] else '❌'}")
    print(f"Analyse: {left_str(a_left)} {'✅' if a_ok else '❌'}  |  b:{sum(r['pb']>r['ph'] and r['pb']>r['ps'] for r in a['results'])} h:{sum(r['ph']>r['pb'] and r['ph']>r['ps'] for r in a['results'])} s:{sum(r['ps']>r['pb'] and r['ps']>r['ph'] for r in a['results'])} none:{n - len(a['results']) if n else 0} {'✅' if len(a['results'])==n else '❌'}")

    # table : BTC, ETH, + 2 best/2 worst S
    rows=[r for r in a.get("results",[]) if r["symbol"] in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT")]
    rest=[r for r in a.get("results",[]) if r["symbol"] not in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT")]
    rest=sorted(rest, key=lambda x:x["S"])
    rows += rest[:2] + (list(reversed(rest))[:2] if rest else [])
    # distinct 5 lignes max
    seen=set(); out=[]
    for r in rows:
        k=r["symbol"]
        if k in seen: continue
        seen.add(k); out.append(r)
        if len(out)>=6: break

    print("-"*70)
    print("symbol Sx10  ctx   pb  ph  ps  reason")
    for r in out:
        print(f"{r['symbol'][:-4]:<5} {int(round(10*r['S'])):>3}  {r['ctx']:<5} {int(round(10*r['pb'])):>3} {int(round(10*r['ph'])):>3} {int(round(10*r['ps'])):>3} {r.get('reason','')}")
    print("-"*70)
    print("Derniers signaux: (aucun)")
    print("Positions ouvertes: (aucune)")
    print("Historique récent: (vide)")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

set -euo pipefail
STATE=/opt/scalp/run/events; mkdir -p "$STATE"
st(){ stat -c %Y "$1" 2>/dev/null || echo 0; }
S=/opt/scalp/data/signals.json; if [ -f "$S" ]; then p="$STATE/s.ts"; last=$(cat "$p" 2>/dev/null||echo 0); cur=$(st "$S");
  if [ "$cur" != "$last" ]; then cnt=$(jq 'length' "$S" 2>/dev/null || echo 0); [ "$cnt" -gt 0 ] && /opt/scalp/tools/tg.sh "📣 $cnt signal(s) prêt(s)"; echo "$cur" >"$p"; fi; fi

L=/opt/scalp/data/orders.log; if [ -f "$L" ]; then p="$STATE/o.ts"; last=$(cat "$p" 2>/dev/null||echo 0); cur=$(st "$L");

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, json, ccxt
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
F_CON = DATA/"contracts_usdt.json"     # liste lisible humaine (BTCUSDT, …)
F_OK  = DATA/"coins_90d.json"          # whitelist >=90j (ids: BTCUSDT_UMCBL, …)
F_PEN = DATA/"coins_pending.json"      # 80–90j, à rechecker
F_DBG = DATA/"debug/coins_scan_ccxt.json"

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })

def main():
    e = ex()
    markets = e.load_markets()
    # USDT linear swaps uniquement
    mlist = [m for m in markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("settle")=="USDT"]
    ids   = sorted({ m["id"] for m in mlist })            # ex: BTCUSDT_UMCBL
    F_CON.write_text(json.dumps([i.replace("_UMCBL","USDT") for i in ids], indent=2))

    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    need90 = now - 90*24*3600*1000
    need80 = now - 80*24*3600*1000

    ok, pen, details = [], [], []
    since = now - 130*24*3600*1000
    for m in mlist:
        sym = m["symbol"]      # ex: BTC/USDT:USDT
        mid = m["id"]          # ex: BTCUSDT_UMCBL
        try:
            rows = e.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1d", since=since, limit=130)
            if not rows:
                pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"nodata"}); continue
            first_ts = rows[0][0]
            if first_ts <= need90:
                ok.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"ok90","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
            elif first_ts <= need80:
                pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"pending80","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
            else:
                details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"too_young","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
        except Exception as err:
            pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"error","err":str(err)[:140]})

    ts = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
    F_OK.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols":ok,"generated_at":ts,"source":"ccxt-1d-90d"}, indent=2))
    F_PEN.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols":pen,"generated_at":ts,"note":"check next run (>=80d)"}, indent=2))
    F_DBG.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":ts,"contracts":len(ids),"ok90":len(ok),"pending":len(pen),"details":details[:60]}, indent=2))
    print(f"[ccxt usdt 1d] markets={len(ids)} ok90={len(ok)} pending={len(pen)}")
if __name__ == "__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time

    j=json.loads(IN.read_text() or "[]");  j=[j] if isinstance(j,dict) else j

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, random
from pathlib import Path
from bitget_http import ticker_price

D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
signals=json.loads((D/"signals.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"signals.json").exists() else []
positions=json.loads((D/"positions.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"positions.json").exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]

orders=[]; now=int(time.time())
for s in signals:
    if not isinstance(s,dict): continue
    sym=s.get("symbol"); side=s.get("side")
    if not sym or side not in ("buy","sell"): continue
    px=ticker_price(sym) or 100.0
    oid=f"paper-{now}-{random.randint(1000,9999)}"
    entry={"id":oid,"symbol":sym,"side":side,"qty":1.0,"price":px,"ts":now,"status":"open"}
    positions.append(entry); orders.append(entry)

(D/"positions.json").write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
(D/"orders.log").touch(exist_ok=True)
if orders:
    with (D/"orders.log").open("a") as f:
        for o in orders: f.write(f"{o['ts']} NEW {o['side']} {o['symbol']} {o['id']} @ {o['price']}\n")
if signals: (D/"signals.json").write_text("[]")
if not (D/"paper_balance.json").exists(): (D/"paper_balance.json").write_text(json.dumps({"equity":0,"ts":"1970-01-01T00:00:00Z"},indent=2))
print(f"[router] routed={len(orders)} positions_total={len(positions)}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"

    except: return 0
def age(tf,s):
    f=C/tf/(s+".json")
    if not f.exists(): return None
    try: a=json.loads(f.read_text())
    except: return None
    ts=last_ts(a);  return None if ts==0 else now-ts

    print(f'{s.replace("USDT",""):<12}  {fmt(age("5m",s)):>6}  {fmt(age("15m",s)):>6}  {fmt(age("30m",s)):>6}')

Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/rebuild_top_v2_async.py
