#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, time, asyncio, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# ====== Config ======
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PARAMS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/top_params.json")
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("TOP_WORKERS", "10"))
RATE_LIMIT_MS = int(os.getenv("TOP_RATE_LIMIT_MS", "200"))
MAX_INFLIGHT = max(1, 1000 // RATE_LIMIT_MS)
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}  # Bitget futures USDT

# ====== Helpers ======
def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
def load_params(): return json.loads(PARAMS.read_text())

def rank_norm(d):
    if not d: return {}
    it = sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])
    n = max(1, len(it)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(it)}

def ema(vals, p):
    if not vals: return 0.0
    a=2/(p+1); e=float(vals[0])
    for v in vals[1:]: e=a*float(v)+(1-a)*e
    return float(e)

def winsorize(vals, p=0.01):
    if not vals: return vals
    s=sorted(vals); n=len(s)
    lo=s[max(0,int(n*p)-1)]; hi=s[min(n-1,int(n*(1-p)))]
    return [min(max(v,lo),hi) for v in vals]

def spread_bps_from_ticker(t):
    bid, ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
    if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: return 1e9
    mid = 0.5*(bid+ask); return 10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid

def depth_quote_in_band(ob, band_bps=50):
    if not ob or not ob.get("bids") or not ob.get("asks"): return 0.0
    bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
    lo=mid*(1-band_bps/10000.0); hi=mid*(1+band_bps/10000.0)
    q=0.0
    for p,a in ob["bids"]:
        if p<lo: break
        q+=p*a
    for p,a in ob["asks"]:
        if p>hi: break
        q+=p*a
    return float(q)

def spread_bps_median_proxy(o1h24):
    vals=[]
    for k in (o1h24 or []):
        _,_,h,l,_,_=k
        if h and l:
            mid=0.5*(h+l)
            if mid>0: vals.append(10000.0*(h-l)/mid)
    return float(stats.median(vals)) if vals else 1e9

# ====== Throttle async ======
_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(MAX_INFLIGHT)
async def throttled(loop, func, *args, **kw):
    async with _sem:
        t0=time.time()
        try:
            res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: func(*args, **kw))
        except Exception:
            res = None
        dt=time.time()-t0
        sl=max(0.0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - dt)
        if sl: await asyncio.sleep(sl)
        return res

# ====== Per-symbol job (Futures only) ======
async def fetch_bundle(loop, ex, sym, band_bps, funding_since_ms):
    # 1D pour activité + âge
    o1d = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1d", 400, FUT)
    if not isinstance(o1d, list) or not o1d:
        return {"skip": True}  # pas d'info fiable
    last_ts = o1d[-1][0]; first_ts = o1d[0][0]

    # 1H pour turnover EMA, vola, spread proxy
    o1h = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1h", 24*7+1, FUT)
    turnover_vals=[]; rets=[]
    o1h24 = o1h[-24:] if isinstance(o1h,list) else []
    spr_med = spread_bps_median_proxy(o1h24)
    if isinstance(o1h, list) and len(o1h)>10:
        prev=o1h[0][4]
        for _,_,_,_,c,v in o1h[1:]:
            turnover_vals.append(float(v)*float(c))
            if prev>0 and c>0: rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
            prev=c
    turn_ema = float(ema(turnover_vals, 24))
    vola7d = float(stats.pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0

    # Order book depth
    ob = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_order_book, sym, 100, FUT)
    depth_q = depth_quote_in_band(ob, band_bps)

    # Funding 7j
    fund_abs = 0.0
    if hasattr(ex, "fetchFundingRateHistory"):
        hist = await throttled(loop, ex.fetchFundingRateHistory, sym, funding_since_ms, None, {**FUT})
        vals=[]
        if isinstance(hist, list):
            for it in hist:
                fr = it.get("fundingRate") or it.get("fundingRateDaily") or 0.0
                try: vals.append(abs(float(fr)))
                except: pass
        if vals: fund_abs = float(sum(vals)/len(vals))

    return {
        "skip": False,
        "last_ts": last_ts, "first_ts": first_ts,
        "turnover_ema7d": turn_ema, "vola7d": vola7d,
        "spread_bps_med": spr_med, "depth_quote": depth_q,
        "funding_abs_mean": fund_abs
    }

# ====== Main ======
def main():
    import ccxt
    p = load_params()
    EX, QUOTE, N = p["exchange"], p["quote"], p["top_n"]
    flt, dep, W = p["filters"], p["depth"], p["scoring"]

    NOW = datetime.now(timezone.utc); NOW_ISO = now_iso()
    cutoff_90d_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=90)).timestamp()*1000)
    listing_cut_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=int(flt.get("min_listing_days",180)))).timestamp()*1000)
    funding_since_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=7)).timestamp()*1000)
    band_bps = int(dep.get("band_bps",50))
    min_depth_q = float(dep.get("min_quote_depth",0.0))
    min_qv = float(flt["min_quote_vol_24h"])
    max_sp = float(flt["max_spread_bps"])

    ex0 = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex0.load_markets()

    # Univers: SWAP linéaire USDT
    mkts = [m for m in ex0.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols = [m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases = {m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # Tickers avec params (certains exchanges ignorent params sur fetch_tickers → fallback par symbole)
    tickers = {}
    try:
        tickers = ex0.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s] = ex0.fetch_ticker(s, {**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s] = {}

    # Pré-filtre rapide
    bad_kw = tuple(flt["exclude_leveraged_keywords"])
    bad_bases = set(flt["exclude_bases"])
    pre=[]; vol24={}
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in bad_kw): continue
        if b in bad_bases: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        qv=float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        sp=spread_bps_from_ticker(t)
        if qv < min_qv or sp > max_sp: continue
        pre.append(s); vol24[s]=qv

    # Pool de clients
    def ex_factory():
        e = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
        try: e.load_markets()
        except Exception: pass
        return e
    clients = [ex_factory() for _ in range(max(1, min(WORKERS, len(pre))))]

    async def run_all():
        loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
        tasks=[]
        for i,s in enumerate(pre):
            ex = clients[i % len(clients)]
            tasks.append(fetch_bundle(loop, ex, s, band_bps, funding_since_ms))
        res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        return {s:r for s,r in zip(pre,res)}

    results = asyncio.run(run_all())

    # Gates et métriques
    inactive_90d=[]; too_young=[]; depth_fail=[]; metrics={}
    for s,r in results.items():
        if isinstance(r,Exception) or r is None or r.get("skip"):  # pas de data fiable → ignore
            continue
        if r["last_ts"] < cutoff_90d_ms:
            inactive_90d.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        if r["first_ts"] and r["first_ts"] > listing_cut_ms:
            too_young.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        if r["depth_quote"] < min_depth_q:
            depth_fail.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        metrics[s]=r

    # coins_90d.json
    DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (DATA/"coins_90d.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "cutoff_days": 90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive_90d)
    }, indent=2))

    if not metrics:
        # pas de top possible
        (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
            "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "futures-only+advanced-async-v2",
            "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "symbols": []
        }, indent=2))
        (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
            "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "n": 0,
            "gates": {"inactive_90d": len(inactive_90d), "too_young": len(too_young), "depth_fail": len(depth_fail)},
            "items": []
        }, indent=2))
        print(f"[top-v2-futures] pre={len(pre)} active=0 top=0 inactive90d={len(inactive_90d)} tooyoung={len(too_young)} depthfail={len(depth_fail)}")
        return

    # Winsor + log-scale
    vvals=[vol24.get(s,0.0) for s in metrics]
    tvals=[metrics[s]["turnover_ema7d"] for s in metrics]
    vvals=winsorize(vvals,0.01) if len(vvals)>10 else vvals
    tvals=winsorize(tvals,0.01) if len(tvals)>10 else tvals
    vmap={s: math.log1p(v) for s,v in zip(metrics.keys(), vvals)}
    tmap={s: math.log1p(v) for s,v in zip(metrics.keys(), tvals)}
    volmap={s: metrics[s]["vola7d"] for s in metrics}
    dmap  ={s: metrics[s]["depth_quote"] for s in metrics}
    spmap ={s: metrics[s]["spread_bps_med"] for s in metrics}
    fmap  ={s: metrics[s]["funding_abs_mean"] for s in metrics}

    Rv,Rt,Rvol,Rd,Rs,Rf = map(rank_norm,(vmap,tmap,volmap,dmap,spmap,fmap))
    W = p["scoring"]

    score={}
    for s in metrics:
        score[s] = (
            W["w_volume24h"]       * Rv.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_turnover7d_ema"]  * Rt.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_volatility7d"]    * Rvol.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_depth"]           * Rd.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_spread_med"]      * Rs.get(s,0.0) +
            W.get("w_funding",-0.05)*Rf.get(s,0.0)
        )

    ranked = sorted(score.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)
    top_syms = [s.replace("/","") for s,_ in ranked[:p["top_n"]]]

    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "futures-only+advanced-async-v2",
        "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "symbols": top_syms
    }, indent=2))

    out=[]
    for s,sc in ranked[:p["top_n"]]:
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        m=metrics[s]
        out.append({
            "symbol": s.replace("/",""),
            "score": round(float(sc),6),
            "volume24h_quote": float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0),
            "turnover7d_ema": float(m["turnover_ema7d"]),
            "volatility7d": float(m["vola7d"]),
            "depth_quote_band": float(m["depth_quote"]),
            "spread_bps_median": float(m["spread_bps_med"]),
            "funding_abs_mean": float(m["funding_abs_mean"])
        })

    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "n": len(top_syms),
        "gates": {"inactive_90d": len(inactive_90d), "too_young": len(too_young), "depth_fail": len(depth_fail)},
        "items": out
    }, indent=2))

    print(f"[top-v2-futures] pre={len(pre)} active={len(metrics)} top={len(top_syms)} "
          f"inactive90d={len(inactive_90d)} tooyoung={len(too_young)} depthfail={len(depth_fail)} "
          f"workers={WORKERS} inflight={MAX_INFLIGHT}")
if __name__ == "__main__": main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ts(){ date -Is; }

DATA=/opt/scalp/data

# TTL (validité)
TTL_COINS90=$((2*24*3600))   # 2 jours
TTL_TOP=$((2*3600))          # 2 h
TTL_AOUT=$((5*60))           # 5 min

fresh(){ # fresh file ttl
  f=$1; ttl=$2
  [ -s "$f" ] || return 1
  ts=$(jq -r '.generated_at // empty' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
  [ -n "$ts" ] || return 1
  now=$(date +%s)
  ft=$(date -d "$ts" +%s 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  age=$(( now - ft ))
  [ $age -lt $ttl ]
}

echo "[INIT] $(ts) start"

# Solde initial si absent
[ -s $DATA/paper_balance.json ] || echo '{"equity":200,"ts":"'"$(ts)"'"}' > $DATA/paper_balance.json
[ -s $DATA/signals.json ] || echo '[]' > $DATA/signals.json
[ -s $DATA/history.json ] || echo '[]' > $DATA/history.json
[ -s $DATA/positions.json ] || echo '{"positions":[]}' > $DATA/positions.json

# 1) Univers
if ! fresh $DATA/coins_90d.json $TTL_COINS90; then
  echo "[INIT] coins_90d refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_contracts_usdt_ccxt.py || true
fi

# 2) Top
if ! fresh $DATA/top.json $TTL_TOP; then
  echo "[INIT] top.json refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_top.py || true
fi

# 3) Analyse A (si expiré)
if ! fresh $DATA/analyse_A_out.json $TTL_AOUT; then
  echo "[INIT] Analyse A refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py || true
  bash /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_guard.sh || true
fi

# 4) Analyse B (toujours 1m → ctx dépendant)
echo "[INIT] Analyse B run"
python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_1m3m_subset.py || true
bash /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_guard.sh || true

echo "[INIT] $(ts) done"
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TOP=/opt/scalp/data/top.json
[ -s "$TOP" ] || { echo "[data-guard] no top.json"; exit 0; }
# calc retard maxi via python (pire des top30)
python3 - <<'PY'
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
def last(s,tf):
    p=C/tf/(s+".json")
    if not p.exists(): return 0
    try:
        a=json.loads(p.read_text()); return int(a[-1][0])//1000 if a else 0
    except: return 0
top=json.loads(Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json").read_text()); syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
now=int(time.time()); bad=[]
for tf,period in [("5m",300),("15m",900),("30m",1800)]:
    left=min([period-(now-last(s,tf)) if last(s,tf)>0 else 0 for s in syms] or [0])
    if left<=0: bad.append(tf)
if bad:
    print("[data-guard] refresh TF:", ",".join(bad)); sys.stdout.flush()
    import subprocess as sp
    for tf in bad: sp.call(["python3","/opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py", tf])
else:
    print("[data-guard] OK")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
pos_f=D/"positions.json"; bal_f=D/"paper_balance.json"
positions=json.loads(pos_f.read_text() or "[]") if pos_f.exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]
now=int(time.time()); closed=0
for p in positions:
    if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="open" and now-int(p.get("ts",now))>20:
        p["status"]="closed"; p["close_ts"]=now; p["pnl"]=1 if int(str(p.get("id",""))[-1])%2 else -1; closed+=1
pos_f.write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
equity=sum(p.get("pnl",0) for p in positions if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="closed")
bal={"equity":equity,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}
bal_f.write_text(json.dumps(bal,indent=2))
print(f"[monitor] closed={closed} equity={equity}")

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/filter_top.py
Size: 2131
MTime: 2025-09-25 18:21:16.038024120 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import argparse, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
NOW  = int(time.time())

TF_REQ = [("5m",300), ("15m",900), ("30m",1800)]
STALE = 2*3600  # on considère "frais" si dernière bougie < 2h

def load_universe(p):
    p = Path(p)
    if not p.exists(): return []
    try: j = json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return []
    syms = j.get("symbols") or j.get("Symbols") or []
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str)]

def score_symbol(sym:str)->tuple:
    """score = nb de TF présents et frais, puis inverse de staleness."""
    ok = 0
    worst_left = -10**9
    for tf,period in TF_REQ:
        f = CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
        if not f.exists(): continue
        try:
            a = json.loads(f.read_text())
            ts = int(a[-1][0])//1000 if a else 0
        except Exception:
            ts = 0
        left = max(0, (ts + period) - NOW)  # validité restante
        age = period - left
        if age <= STALE: ok += 1
        worst_left = max(worst_left, left)
    return (ok, worst_left)  # tri décroissant

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--universe", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--keep", type=int, default=30)
    ap.add_argument("--fixed", default="BTCUSDT,ETHUSDT,XRPUSDT,SOLUSDT,BNBUSDT")
    ap.add_argument("--out", required=True)
    args = ap.parse_args()

    uni = load_universe(args.universe)
    fixed = [s.strip() for s in (args.fixed or "").split(",") if s.strip()]
    fixed = [s for s in fixed if s in uni]

    rest = [s for s in uni if s not in fixed]
    scored = sorted(rest, key=score_symbol, reverse=True)

    pick = list(dict.fromkeys(fixed + scored))[:args.keep]

    out = {
        "symbols": pick,
        "generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
        "source": "coins_90d->local_candles",
        "keep": args.keep,
        "fixed": fixed,
    }
    Path(args.out).write_text(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
    print(f"[top] n={len(pick)} fixed={len(fixed)} -> {args.out}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, time, shutil
from pathlib import Path
OK=True; msgs=[]
def need(p,t="f"):
    global OK
    P=Path(p); ex=(P.is_file() if t=="f" else P.is_dir())
    if not ex: OK=False; msgs.append(f"missing:{t}:{p}")
def touch(p): Path(p).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True); Path(p).touch()
for f in ("/etc/scalp.env","/etc/scalp.app","/etc/scalp.tuning"): need(f,"f")
for d in ("/opt/scalp/tools","/opt/scalp/logs","/opt/scalp/data","/opt/scalp/data/debug","/opt/scalp/run"): need(d,"d")
need("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_minutely.sh","f")
for f in ("contracts_usdt.json","coins_90d.json","top.json"): touch(f"/opt/scalp/data/{f}")
st=shutil.disk_usage("/opt/scalp"); OK = OK and st.free >= 500*1024*1024 or False
out={"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ",time.gmtime()),"ok":OK,"issues":msgs}
Path("/opt/scalp/data/debug/preflight.json").write_text(json.dumps(out,indent=2))
print(json.dumps(out)); sys.exit(0 if OK else 2)
PY

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
Q="/opt/scalp/run/symbol_queue.txt"; MAX="${QUEUE_MAX_PER_TICK:-10}"
[ -f "$Q" ] || exit 0
mapfile -t ALL < <(grep -E '^[A-Z0-9]+' "$Q" 2>/dev/null || true); [ ${#ALL[@]} -eq 0 ] && { rm -f "$Q"; exit 0; }
KEEP=(); cnt=0
for S in "${ALL[@]}"; do
  if [ "$cnt" -lt "$MAX" ]; then /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_for_symbol_hint.sh "$S" || true; cnt=$((cnt+1)); else KEEP+=("$S"); fi
done
( [ ${#KEEP[@]} -gt 0 ] && printf "%s\n" "${KEEP[@]}" > "$Q" ) || rm -f "$Q"
echo "[drain] processed=$cnt remaining=${#KEEP[@]}"
SHH

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
T=float(os.environ.get("TUNE_S_THRESHOLD","0.6"))
A=json.loads((D/"analyse_A_out.json").read_text() or "[]")
A=[A] if isinstance(A,dict) else A
signals=[]
now=int(time.time())
for r in A:
    if not isinstance(r,dict): continue
    ctx=str(r.get("context","none")).lower(); S=float(r.get("S",0) or 0)
    if ctx in ("buy","sell") and S>=T:
        signals.append({"symbol":r.get("symbol"),"side":ctx,"score":S,"ts":now,"source":"B"})
(D/"signals.json").write_text(json.dumps(signals,indent=2))
print(f"[B] signals={len(signals)} T={T}")

cat >/opt/scalp/tools/signal_router.py <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, random
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
signals=json.loads((D/"signals.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"signals.json").exists() else []
positions=json.loads((D/"positions.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"positions.json").exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]
orders=[]; now=int(time.time())
for s in signals:
    if not isinstance(s,dict): continue
    sym=s.get("symbol"); side=s.get("side")
    if not sym or side not in ("buy","sell"): continue
    oid=f"paper-{now}-{random.randint(1000,9999)}"
    entry={"id":oid,"symbol":sym,"side":side,"qty":1.0,"price":100.0,"ts":now,"status":"open"}
    positions.append(entry); orders.append(entry)
(D/"positions.json").write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
(D/"orders.log").touch(exist_ok=True)
if orders:
    with (D/"orders.log").open("a") as f:
        for o in orders: f.write(f"{o['ts']} NEW {o['side']} {o['symbol']} {o['id']}\n")
if signals: (D/"signals.json").write_text("[]")
if not (D/"paper_balance.json").exists(): (D/"paper_balance.json").write_text(json.dumps({"equity":0,"ts":"1970-01-01T00:00:00Z"},indent=2))
print(f"[router] routed={len(orders)} positions_total={len(positions)}")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
pos_f=D/"positions.json"; bal_f=D/"paper_balance.json"
positions=json.loads(pos_f.read_text() or "[]") if pos_f.exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]
now=int(time.time()); closed=0
for p in positions:
    if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="open" and now-int(p.get("ts",now))>20:
        p["status"]="closed"; p["close_ts"]=now; p["pnl"]=1 if int(str(p.get("id",""))[-1])%2 else -1; closed+=1
pos_f.write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
equity=sum(p.get("pnl",0) for p in positions if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="closed")
bal={"equity":equity,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}
bal_f.write_text(json.dumps(bal,indent=2))
print(f"[monitor] closed={closed} equity={equity}")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
RUN=Path("/opt/scalp/run"); RUN.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
M=RUN/"metrics.prom"; D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DD=D/"debug"
def J(p,default=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return default
pf=J(DD/"preflight.json",{}); ae=J(DD/"a_export_check.json",{}); bs=J(DD/"b_status.json",{})
top=J(D/"top.json",{}); coins=J(D/"coins_90d.json",{}); sig=J(D/"signals.json",[])
now=int(time.time()); L=[]
def g(n,v,l=None):
    if v is None: return
    if isinstance(v,bool): v=1 if v else 0
    lbl="" if not l else "{"+",".join([f'{k}=\"{str(x)}\"' for k,x in l.items()])+"}"
    L.append(f"{n}{lbl} {v}")
g("scalp_ok", pf.get("ok",0), {"comp":"preflight"})
g("scalp_ok", ae.get("ok",0), {"comp":"analyse_a_export"})
g("scalp_ok", bs.get("ok",0), {"comp":"analyse_b"})
g("scalp_counts", len((top or {}).get("symbols",[])), {"name":"top"})
g("scalp_counts", len((coins or {}).get("symbols",[])), {"name":"coins90"})
g("scalp_counts", len(sig if isinstance(sig,list) else []), {"name":"signals"})
g("scalp_timestamp", now, {"name":"export"})
M.write_text("\n".join(L)+"\n"); print(f"[metrics] wrote {M}")
PY

  echo "$(TS) preflight:not-ok -> skip tick" >>"$LOG"; /opt/scalp/tools/alert_eval.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/metrics_export.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/events_notify.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; echo "$(TS) tick:end" >>"$LOG"; exit 0; fi

  TF_ORDER="${SYNC_TF_ORDER:-1m,5m,15m,30m}" FORCE_CATCHUP=1 TARGET_ROWS="${A_TARGET_ROWS:-600}" /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/sync_candles_safe.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true

fi
if [ "$(date +%M)" = "00" ] && [ $((10#$(date +%H) % ${QUALITY_EVERY_HOURS:-2})) -eq 0 ]; then echo "$(TS) quality:start" >>"$LOG"; /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/run_quality_only.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; echo "$(TS) quality:end" >>"$LOG"; fi
PERIOD_H="${CONTRACTS_PERIOD_H:-48}"; ST="$RUN/contracts.stamp"; now=$(date +%s); last=0; [ -f "$ST" ] && last=$(cat "$ST"||echo 0)
if [ $(( now - last )) -ge $(( PERIOD_H*3600 )) ]; then echo "$(TS) contracts:start" >>"$LOG"; [ -f /opt/scalp/tools/refresh_contracts.py ] && /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/refresh_contracts.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; [ -f /opt/scalp/tools/rebuild_coins_90d_light.py ] && /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/rebuild_coins_90d_light.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; date +%s > "$ST"; echo "$(TS) contracts:end" >>"$LOG"; fi
[ -x /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b.sh ] && /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true

echo "$(TS) tick:end" >>"$LOG"; exit 0

#!/usr/bin/env python3
def ema(vals,n):
    if not vals: return []
    k=2/(n+1); out=[vals[0]]
    for x in vals[1:]: out.append(out[-1]+k*(x-out[-1]))
    return out
def minmax_pos(vals,win):
    out=[]
    for i in range(len(vals)):
        a=max(0,i-win+1); w=vals[a:i+1]
        lo=min(w); hi=max(w); rng=(hi-lo) or 1e-9
        out.append((vals[i]-lo)/rng)
    return out
def slope(vals,step=5):
    out=[0]*len(vals)
    for i in range(step,len(vals)):
        prev=vals[i-step] or 1e-9
        out[i]=(vals[i]-prev)/abs(prev)
    return out
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/a_sanity.py
Size: 1420
MTime: 2025-09-25 12:14:08.091800209 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
BASE=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=BASE/"candles"
TOP=json.loads((BASE/"top.json").read_text()) if (BASE/"top.json").exists() else {"symbols":[]}
now=int(time.time())

def load(sym, tf):
    p=C/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return None, f"missing:{tf}"
    try:
        j=json.loads(p.read_text()); k=j.get("data",[])
        if not k: return None, f"empty:{tf}"
        # drop bougie incomplète
        tf_s={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}[tf]
        if now - int(k[-1][0]//1000) < int(0.9*tf_s): k=k[:-1]
        if len(k)<500: return None, f"bars<{500}:{tf}"
        age= now - int(k[-1][0]//1000)
        if age>tf_s*2: return None, f"stale:{tf} age={age}s"
        return k, "ok"
    except Exception as e:
        return None, f"readerr:{tf}:{e}"

issues=[]
ok=0
syms=list(TOP.get("symbols",[]))
for sym in syms:
    row={"symbol":sym}
    bad=[]
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        k,st=load(sym, tf)
        row[f"{tf}_status"]=st
        if st!="ok": bad.append(st)
    if bad: issues.append({**row,"fail":bad})
    else: ok+=1

out={"ts":now,"checked":len(syms),"ok":ok,"fail":len(issues),"issues":issues[:20]}
print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
# dump complet pour inspection
DEBUG=BASE/"debug"; DEBUG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(DEBUG/"a_sanity.json").write_text(json.dumps({**out,"issues_full":issues}, indent=2))
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
source /etc/scalp.app 2>/dev/null || true
CANDLES_DIR="${CANDLES_DIR:-/opt/scalp/data/candles}"; AGE="${FRESH_AGE_SEC:-180}"
[ -d "$CANDLES_DIR" ] || exit 0
tmp=$(mktemp)
find "$CANDLES_DIR" -type f -mmin -$(( AGE/60 )) \( -name '*.parquet' -o -name '*.json' -o -name '*.csv' \) >"$tmp" || true
symbols=$(awk -F/ 'NF>=2{for(i=1;i<=NF;i++){if($(i)=="candles"&&i+1<=NF){print $(i+1)}}}' "$tmp" | tr '[:lower:]' '[:upper:]' | sort -u)
rm -f "$tmp"; [ -n "$symbols" ] || exit 0
/opt/scalp/tools/enqueue_symbols.py $symbols

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
/opt/scalp/tools/env_compat.sh >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
LOG="/opt/scalp/logs/paper_loop.log"; PY="${PYTHON_BIN:-/usr/bin/python3}"

MTime: 2025-09-26 06:02:18.399849066 +0000

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, math, statistics as st
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"
OUTF = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
HIST_DIR = DATA/"history/A"
HIST_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

TF_STEPS = {"30m":1800, "15m":900, "5m":300}
TF_W = {"30m":0.5, "15m":0.3, "5m":0.2}
TAU = {"30m":0.35, "15m":0.30, "5m":0.25}
ATR_GATE = {"30m":0.0025, "15m":0.0018, "5m":0.0012}  # en ratio

P_ENTER, P_EXIT = 0.60, 0.45

def jload(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def ema(arr, n):
    k = 2/(n+1)
    out=[]
    s=None
    for x in arr:
        s = x if s is None else (x*k + s*(1-k))
        out.append(s)
    return out

def atr(h,l,c,n=14):
    tr=[]
    prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        if i==0: tr.append(h[i]-l[i])
        else: tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-prev), abs(l[i]-prev)))
        prev=c[i]
    return ema(tr,n)

def macd_hist(c, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    e1=ema(c,f); e2=ema(c,s)
    macd=[e1[i]-e2[i] for i in range(len(c))]
    es=ema(macd, sig)
    return [macd[i]-es[i] for i in range(len(c))]

def rsi(c, n=14):
    gains=[]; losses=[]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        d=c[i]-c[i-1]
        gains.append(max(d,0)); losses.append(max(-d,0))
    def rma(x, n):
        if not x: return []
        a=[sum(x[:n])/n]+[0]*(len(x)-n)
        for i in range(n,len(x)):
            a[i-n+1] = (a[i-n]*(n-1)+x[i])/n
        return [0]* (len(x)-len(a)) + a
    rg=rma(gains,n); rl=rma(losses,n)
    out=[50]*len(c)
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        avg_g=rg[i-1]; avg_l=rl[i-1]
        if avg_l==0 and avg_g==0: out[i]=50
        elif avg_l==0: out[i]=100
        else:
            rs=avg_g/avg_l
            out[i]=100-(100/(1+rs))
    return out

def obv_slope(c, v, n=20):
    obv=[0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        if c[i]>c[i-1]: obv.append(obv[-1]+v[i])
        elif c[i]<c[i-1]: obv.append(obv[-1]-v[i])
        else: obv.append(obv[-1])
    out=[0]*len(c)
    for i in range(len(c)):
        out[i] = 0 if i<n else obv[i]-obv[i-n]
    return out

def tanh(x,cap=3.0):
    x=max(-cap,min(cap,x))
    return math.tanh(x)

def subscores_for_tf(ts,c,h,l,v,tf):
    if len(c)<60: return 0.0, {}
    atr14=atr(h,l,c,14)
    at = atr14[-1]
    atp = 0.0 if c[-1]==0 else at/c[-1]

    e12=ema(c,12); e26=ema(c,26)
    s_ema = tanh((e12[-1]-e26[-1])/(1.5*at + 1e-12))

    hist = macd_hist(c)
    scale = st.median([abs(x) for x in hist[-100:]]) or 1.0
    s_macd = tanh(hist[-1]/scale)

    rsi14 = rsi(c,14)
    s_rsi = max(-1.0, min(1.0,(rsi14[-1]-50)/50))

    # ADX light (proxy via variation ATR/price)
    s_adx = max(-1.0, min(1.0, (atp-0.002)/0.01))

    obvs=obv_slope(c,v,20)
    med = st.median([abs(x) for x in obvs[-200:]]) or 1.0
    s_obv = tanh(obvs[-1]/med)

    w = {"ema":0.35,"macd":0.25,"rsi":0.20,"adx":0.10,"obv":0.10}
    gate = ATR_GATE[tf]
    if atp < gate:
        w["ema"]*=0.5; w["macd"]*=0.5
    S = (w["ema"]*s_ema + w["macd"]*s_macd + w["rsi"]*s_rsi + w["adx"]*s_adx + w["obv"]*s_obv) / sum(w.values())
    return S, {"S":S,"atp":atp}

def softmax_probs(S, tau):
    epos = math.exp(S/tau)
    eneg = math.exp(-S/tau)
    Z = epos + 1 + eneg
    return {"pb":epos/Z, "ph":1/Z, "ps":eneg/Z}

def aggregate_probs(per_tf):
    wsum=sum(TF_W.values())
    pb = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ph = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ps = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    Sw = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    tot=pb+ph+ps
    if tot<=0: pb=ph=ps=1/3
    else: pb,ph,ps = pb/tot, ph/tot, ps/tot
    out={"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]
            out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]
            out[f"S_{tf}"]= per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out

def apply_veto_m5(agg):
    pb,ps = agg["pb"], agg["ps"]
    pb30, pb15 = agg.get("pb_30m",0), agg.get("pb_15m",0)
    ps30, ps15 = agg.get("ps_30m",0), agg.get("ps_15m",0)
    S5 = agg.get("S_5m",0.0)
    bull_ok = (pb>=P_ENTER) and (pb30>=0.55) and (pb15>=0.55) and (S5>=0)
    bear_ok = (ps>=P_ENTER) and (ps30>=0.55) and (ps15>=0.55) and (S5<=0)
    if not bull_ok and pb>=P_ENTER: agg["pb"] = max(agg["pb"], P_EXIT-1e-6)
    if not bear_ok and ps>=P_ENTER: agg["ps"] = max(agg["ps"], P_EXIT-1e-6)
    agg["veto5"] = (not bull_ok and pb>=P_ENTER) or (not bear_ok and ps>=P_ENTER)
    return agg

def decide_ctx(pb,ph,ps, prev=None):
    # hystérésis
    if prev=="bull":
        if pb>=P_EXIT: return "bull"
        if ps>=P_ENTER: return "bear"
        return "none" if 0.40<=ph<=0.60 else "none"
    if prev=="bear":
        if ps>=P_EXIT: return "bear"
        if pb>=P_ENTER: return "bull"
        return "none" if 0.40<=ph<=0.60 else "none"
    # neutre
    if pb>=P_ENTER: return "bull"
    if ps>=P_ENTER: return "bear"
    if 0.40<=ph<=0.60: return "range"
    return "none"

def load_ohlcv(symbol, tf):
    p = CAND/f"{tf}/{symbol}.json"
    a = jload(p, [])
    if not a: return None
    ts   = [i[0]//1000 for i in a]
    o,h,l,c,v = zip(*[(i[0]//1000,i[2],i[3],i[4],i[5]) for i in a])  # use high, low, close, volume
    return list(ts), list(c), list(h), list(l), list(v)

def main():
    top=jload(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
    if not syms:
        Path(OUTF).write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at":"", "results":[]}))
        print("[A] empty top"); return 0

    results=[]
    freshness_ok=True
    max_data_ts=0

    for s in syms:
        per_tf={}
        for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
            got = load_ohlcv(s, tf)
            if not got: freshness_ok=False; continue
            ts,c,h,l,v = got
            max_data_ts = max(max_data_ts, ts[-1])
            S, extra = subscores_for_tf(ts,c,h,l,v,tf)
            probs = softmax_probs(S, TAU[tf]); probs["S"]=S
            per_tf[tf]=probs

        if not per_tf: continue
        agg = aggregate_probs(per_tf)
        agg = apply_veto_m5(agg)
        ctx = decide_ctx(agg["pb"], agg["ph"], agg["ps"])
        reason=[]
        if agg.get("veto5"): reason.append("veto_5m")
        if ctx=="none": reason.append("unclear")
        result={
            "symbol": s,
            "pb": agg["pb"], "ph": agg["ph"], "ps": agg["ps"],
            "S": agg["Sw"], "ctx": ctx, "reason": ("/".join(reason) if reason else "ok")
        }
        results.append(result)

        # --- Historique JSONL par coin
        rec = {
            "ts": int(time.time()),
            "pb": agg["pb"], "ph": agg["ph"], "ps": agg["ps"],
            "S": agg["Sw"], "ctx": ctx, "reason": result["reason"]
        }
        (HIST_DIR/f"{s.replace('USDT','')}.jsonl").open("a").write(json.dumps(rec, separators=(",",":"))+"\n")

    out = {"generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
           "max_data_ts": max_data_ts,
           "results": results}
    Path(OUTF).write_text(json.dumps(out))
    print(f"[A] n={len(results)} out={OUTF}")
    # diagnostics min set
    b=h=s=none=0
    for r in results:
        m=max(r["pb"],r["ph"],r["ps"])
        if r["pb"]==m: b+=1
        elif r["ps"]==m: s+=1
        elif r["ph"]==m: h+=1
        else: none+=1
    print(b); print(h); print(s)
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, math, sys
from pathlib import Path
from statistics import pstdev
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta

NOW = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
NOW_ISO = NOW.isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PARAMS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/top_params.json")

def load_params():
    p = json.loads(PARAMS.read_text())
    p["exchange"] = p.get("exchange","bitget")
    p["quote"] = p.get("quote","USDT")
    p["top_n"] = int(p.get("top_n",30))
    return p

def iso(ts): 
    return datetime.fromtimestamp(ts/1000, tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def last_1d_ts(ex, sym):
    try:
        o = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1d", limit=2)
        return o[-1][0] if o else 0
    except Exception:
        return 0

def stats_7d(ex, sym):
    try:
        o = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1h", limit=24*7+1)
    except Exception:
        return (0.0, 0.0)
    if len(o) < 10:
        return (0.0, 0.0)
    trn = 0.0
    rets = []
    prev = o[0][4]
    for _,_,_,_,c,v in o[1:]:
        trn += float(v)*float(c)
        if prev>0 and c>0:
            rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
        prev = c
    vol = float(pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0
    return (trn, vol)

def spread_bps(t):
    bid, ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
    if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: return 1e9
    mid = 0.5*(bid+ask)
    return 10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid

def norm_rank(d):
    items = sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])
    n = max(1, len(items)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(items)}

def main():
    import ccxt
    params = load_params()
    EX, QUOTE, N = params["exchange"], params["quote"], params["top_n"]
    flt, w = params["filters"], params["scoring"]

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    symbols = [s for s in ex.symbols if s.endswith(f"/{QUOTE}")]

    # 1) coins_90d.json
    cutoff_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=90)).timestamp()*1000)
    inactive = []
    for s in symbols:
        if last_1d_ts(ex, s) < cutoff_ms:
            inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
    (DATA/"coins_90d.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source":"ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE, "cutoff_days":90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive)
    }, indent=2))

    # 2) filtres rapides
    tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols)
    def base(sym): return sym.split("/")[0]
    bad_kw = tuple(flt["exclude_leveraged_keywords"])
    bad_bases = set(flt["exclude_bases"])
    min_qv = float(flt["min_quote_vol_24h"])
    max_sp = float(flt["max_spread_bps"])

    pool = []
    for s in symbols:
        s_flat = s.replace("/","")
        if s_flat in inactive: 
            continue
        b = base(s)
        if any(k in b for k in bad_kw): 
            continue
        if b in bad_bases: 
            continue
        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        qv = float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        sp = spread_bps(t)
        if qv < min_qv or sp > max_sp: 
            continue
        pool.append(s)

    # 3) mesures
    vol24, turn7, vola7, spd = {}, {}, {}, {}
    for s in pool:
        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        vol24[s] = float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        spd[s] = spread_bps(t)
        trn, vol = stats_7d(ex, s)
        turn7[s], vola7[s] = trn, vol

    # 4) scoring principal
    ranked = []
    if pool:
        r1, r2, r3, r4 = norm_rank(vol24), norm_rank(turn7), norm_rank(vola7), norm_rank(spd)
        score = {s: (
            w["w_volume24h"]   * r1.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_turnover7d"]  * r2.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_volatility7d"]* r3.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_spread"]      * r4.get(s,0.0)
        ) for s in pool}
        ranked = sorted(score.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    # 4b) fallback si pool vide: top par volume 24h sur tout l'univers actif
    if not ranked:
        vol_all = {s: float(tickers.get(s,{}).get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
                   for s in symbols if s.replace("/","") not in inactive}
        ranked = sorted(vol_all.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    top_syms = [sym.replace("/","") for sym,_ in ranked[:N]]

    # 5) sorties
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "coins_90d+advanced",
        "exchange": EX,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "symbols": top_syms
    }, indent=2))

    # détail pour affichage
    ranked_out = []
    for sym, sc in ranked[:N]:
        t = tickers.get(sym, {})
        ranked_out.append({
            "symbol": sym.replace("/",""),
            "score": round(float(sc), 6),
            "volume24h_quote": float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0),
            "turnover7d": float(turn7.get(sym, 0.0)),
            "volatility7d": float(vola7.get(sym, 0.0)),
            "spread_bps": float(spd.get(sym, 1e9))
        })
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "n": len(top_syms),
        "items": ranked_out
    }, indent=2))

    print(f"[top] pool={len(symbols)} pre={len(pool)} inactive90d={len(inactive)} top={len(top_syms)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CBASE=DATA/"candles"; (CBASE/"1m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LIMIT=520

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX=ex()

def b2ccxt(sym): return sym.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT")

def drop_incomplete(rows):
    if not rows: return rows
    if int(time.time()*1000) - rows[-1][0] < int(0.9*60*1000): return rows[:-1]
    return rows

def load_active_symbols():
    try:
        arr=json.loads((AOUT).read_text() or "[]")
        return [r["symbol"] for r in arr if r.get("context","none")!="none"]
    except: return []

def save_1m(sym, rows):
    out={"generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
         "tf":"1m","symbol":sym,"limit":LIMIT,"data":rows}
    (CBASE/"1m"/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(out))

def main():
    syms=load_active_symbols()
    ok=0; errs=[]
    for s in syms:
        try:
            rows=EX.fetch_ohlcv(b2ccxt(s), timeframe="1m", limit=LIMIT)
            rows=drop_incomplete(rows)
            if len(rows)<100: raise RuntimeError("too few bars")
            save_1m(s, rows); ok+=1
        except Exception as e:
            errs.append({"symbol":s,"err":str(e)[:140]})
    (DATA/"debug/candles_refresh_subset_1m.json").write_text(json.dumps(
        {"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),"updated":ok,"errors":errs}, indent=2))
    print(f"[subset_1m] updated={ok} errors={len(errs)}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta

# Config
EXCHANGE = "bitget"
QUOTE = "USDT"
TOP_N = 30
NOW_ISO = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
OUT_90D = DATA/"coins_90d.json"
OUT_TOP = DATA/"top.json"

def ts_ms_to_iso(tsms:int)->str:
    return datetime.fromtimestamp(tsms/1000, tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def main():
    try:
        import ccxt
    except Exception as e:
        print("ccxt requis:", e, file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EXCHANGE)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    symbols = [s for s in ex.symbols if s.endswith(f"/{QUOTE}")]

    # Détecter inactivité >90j avec OHLCV 1d
    cutoff = datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(days=90)
    cutoff_ms = int(cutoff.timestamp()*1000)

    inactive = []
    last_seen = {}
    for s in symbols:
        try:
            ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(s, timeframe="1d", limit=2)
            if not ohlcv:
                inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
                continue
            last_ts = ohlcv[-1][0]
            last_seen[s] = last_ts
            if last_ts < cutoff_ms:
                inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
        except Exception:
            # En cas d'erreur API, ne classe pas en TOP par prudence
            inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))

    # Mesurer liquidité 24h via tickers
    tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols)
    def vol_quote(sym):
        t = tickers.get(sym, {})
        v = t.get("quoteVolume")
        # Fallback si absent
        return float(v) if v is not None else 0.0

    # Construire TOP hors inactifs >90j
    actives = [s for s in symbols if s.replace("/","") not in inactive]
    actives.sort(key=lambda s: vol_quote(s), reverse=True)
    top_syms = [s.replace("/","") for s in actives[:TOP_N]]

    # Écrire coins_90d.json
    coins_90d = {
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange": EXCHANGE,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "cutoff_days": 90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive),
        "notes": "Pairs dont la dernière bougie 1d est plus vieille que 90 jours, exclues du top30."
    }
    OUT_90D.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp = OUT_90D.with_suffix(".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(coins_90d, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(OUT_90D)

    # Écrire top.json
    top = {
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "coins_90d",
        "exchange": EXCHANGE,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "symbols": top_syms
    }
    tmp = OUT_TOP.with_suffix(".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(top, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(OUT_TOP)

    # Sortie console utile
    print(f"[rebuild_top] top={len(top_syms)} inactive_90d={len(inactive)}")
    if last_seen:
        worst = min(last_seen.values())
        print(f"[rebuild_top] oldest_last_ts={ts_ms_to_iso(worst)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, json
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.request import Request, urlopen
from urllib.error import URLError, HTTPError
BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
def _get(path, params=None, tries=4, timeout=12):
    q=f"{BASE}{path}"+(f"?{urlencode(params)}" if params else "")
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            req=Request(q, headers={"Accept":"application/json"})
            with urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as r:
                return json.loads(r.read().decode("utf-8"))
        except (URLError,HTTPError):
            if i+1>=tries: raise
            time.sleep(0.6*(2**i))
def normalize_symbol(sym):
    s=sym.replace("-","_").upper()
    return (s.replace("_UMCBL",""), "usdt-futures")
def history_candles(sym, granularity="1m", limit=200, end_ms=None):
    s, prod=normalize_symbol(sym)
    p={"symbol":s,"granularity":granularity,"limit":int(limit),"productType":prod}
    if end_ms: p["endTime"]=int(end_ms)
    j=_get("/api/v2/mix/market/history-candles", p)
    raw=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else j
    out=[]
    for k in raw:
        try:
            ts=int(k[0]); o,h,l,c=map(float,k[1:5]); v=float(k[5])
            out.append({"ts":ts,"o":o,"h":h,"l":l,"c":c,"v":v})
        except: pass
    out.sort(key=lambda x:x["ts"])
    return out
def ticker_price(sym):
    s, prod=normalize_symbol(sym)
    j=_get("/api/v2/mix/market/ticker", {"productType":prod,"symbol":s})
    d=(j or {}).get("data",{})
    p=d.get("last") or d.get("lastPr") or d.get("close") or d.get("markPrice")
    return float(p) if p is not None else None

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); CAND=DATA/"candles"
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"; TOP=DATA/"top.json"
LIMIT=600
TF_LIST=["1m","3m"]               # pour Analyse B

def ex():
    import ccxt
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })

def norm_symbol(mkts, base):
    if base in mkts: return base
    if base.endswith("_UMCBL"):
        q=base.split("_")[0].replace("USDT","/USDT:USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
    if base.endswith("USDT"):
        q=base.replace("USDT","/USDT:USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
        q=base.replace("USDT","/USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
    for k in mkts:
        if k.replace(":USDT","").replace("/","").upper()==base.replace("_UMCBL","").upper():
            return k
    return None

def drop_incomplete(rows, tf):
    tf_s={"1m":60,"3m":180}[tf]; now=int(time.time()); last=int(rows[-1][0]//1000)
    if now-last < int(0.9*tf_s): rows=rows[:-1]
    return rows

def save_json(path, rows):
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    path.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),"data":rows}))

def subset_symbols():
    syms=[]
    try:
        a=json.loads(AOUT.read_text())
        syms=[r.get("symbol") for r in a if r.get("context") in ("buy","sell","hold")]
    except: pass
    if not syms:
        try:
            t=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); syms=t.get("symbols",[])[:30]
        except: pass
    return list(dict.fromkeys(syms))  # unique et ordre conservé

def main():
    e=ex(); mkts=e.load_markets()
    syms=subset_symbols()
    ok=wrote=0
    for base in syms:
        sid=norm_symbol(mkts, base)
        if not sid: continue
        for tf in TF_LIST:
            try:
                rows=e.fetch_ohlcv(sid, timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT)
                rows=drop_incomplete(rows, tf)
                if len(rows)<200: continue
                save_json(CAND/tf/f"{base}.json", rows)
                wrote+=1
            except: pass
        ok+=1
    print(f"[candles_refresh_1m3m_subset] in={len(syms)} ok={ok} wrote={wrote}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, os
from pathlib import Path
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.request import Request, urlopen
from bitget_http import history_candles

BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
F_CON=D/"contracts_usdt.json"
F_OK =D/"coins_90d.json"
F_PENDING=D/"coins_pending.json"
F_DBG=D/"debug/coins_scan_1d.json"

SEED=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","XRPUSDT","SOLUSDT","BNBUSDT","ADAUSDT","DOGEUSDT","LTCUSDT","LINKUSDT","DOTUSDT"]

def http_get(path, params=None, tries=4, timeout=12):
    q=f"{BASE}{path}"+(f"?{urlencode(params)}" if params else "")
    hdr={"Accept":"application/json","User-Agent":"scalp-bot/1.0"}
    last=None
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            with urlopen(Request(q, headers=hdr), timeout=timeout) as r:
                import json as _j; return _j.loads(r.read().decode("utf-8"))
        except Exception as e:
            last=e; time.sleep(0.5*(2**i))
    raise last

def list_usdt_contracts():
    try:
        j=http_get("/api/v2/mix/market/contracts", {"productType":"umcbl"})
        data=(j or {}).get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else (j or [])
        s=sorted({str(d.get("symbol","")).upper() for d in data if str(d.get("symbol","")).upper().endswith("USDT")})
        return s or SEED
    except Exception:
        return SEED

def atomic_write(path: Path, obj):
    tmp=path.with_suffix(".tmp"); tmp.write_text(json.dumps(obj,indent=2)+"\n"); os.replace(tmp, path)

def main():
    now_ms=int(time.time()*1000)
    need90=now_ms-90*24*3600*1000
    need80=now_ms-80*24*3600*1000

    syms=list_usdt_contracts()
    atomic_write(F_CON, syms)

    ok=[]; pending=[]; meta=[]
    for s in syms:
        try:
            k=history_candles(s,"1d",limit=120)  # 1 appel par coin
            if not k:
                # pas de données -> garder en pending pour recheck
                pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"nodata"})
                continue
            first_ts=k[0]["ts"]
            if first_ts<=need90:
                ok.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"ok90","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
            elif first_ts<=need80:
                pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"pending80","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
            else:
                meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"too_young","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
        except Exception as e:
            pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"error","err":str(e)})

    ts=time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
    atomic_write(F_OK, {"symbols":ok,"generated_at":ts,"source":"bitget-1d-90d"})
    atomic_write(F_PENDING, {"symbols":pending,"generated_at":ts,"note":"check next run (>=80d)"})
    atomic_write(F_DBG, {"ts":ts,"total":len(syms),"ok90":len(ok),"pending80_or_err":len(pending),"details":meta})
    print(f"[usdt 1d] total={len(syms)} ok90={len(ok)} pending={len(pending)}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/ctx_logic.py

MTime: 2025-09-25 21:36:50.948060693 +0000

import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
W=dict(EMA=0.35,MACD=0.25,RSI=0.20,ADX=0.10,OBV=0.10)
TAU={"30m":0.35,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.25}
TF_W={"30m":0.50,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.20}
ATR_GATE={"30m":0.25,"15m":0.18,"5m":0.12}
P_ENTER=0.60
P_EXIT=0.45
RANGE_LOW,RANGE_HIGH=0.40,0.60
PERSIST_BARS=2
def clip(x,lo,hi):return hi if x>hi else lo if x<lo else x
def tanh(x):return math.tanh(x)
def softmax_triple(S,tau):
    e1=math.exp(S/tau); e2=math.exp(-S/tau); d=e1+1.0+e2
    return e1/d,1.0/d,e2/d
def score_tf(inp,tf):
    atr=max(inp.get("atr14",0.0),1e-12)
    s_ema=tanh((inp.get("ema12",0.0)-inp.get("ema26",0.0))/(1.5*atr))
    sigma=max(inp.get("macd_sigma100",1e-12),1e-12)
    s_macd=tanh(inp.get("macd_hist",0.0)/sigma)
    s_rsi=clip((inp.get("rsi14",50.0)-50.0)/50.0,-1.0,1.0)
    s_adx=clip((inp.get("adx14",20.0)-20.0)/20.0,-1.0,1.0)
    med=max(inp.get("obv_medabs200",1e-12),1e-12)
    s_obv=tanh(inp.get("obv_delta20",0.0)/med)
    reasons=[]
    atr_pct=float(inp.get("atr_pct",0.0))
    if atr_pct<ATR_GATE[tf]:
        s_ema*=0.5; s_macd*=0.5; reasons.append(f"gate_atr_{tf}")
    num=(W["EMA"]*s_ema+W["MACD"]*s_macd+W["RSI"]*s_rsi+W["ADX"]*s_adx+W["OBV"]*s_obv)
    S=clip(num/sum(W.values()),-1.0,1.0)
    pb,ph,ps=softmax_triple(S,TAU[tf])
    return {"S":S,"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"reasons":reasons}
def aggregate_probs(per_tf):
    wsum=sum(TF_W.values())
    pb=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ph=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ps=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    Sw=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    tot=pb+ph+ps
    pb,ph,ps=(1/3,1/3,1/3) if tot<=0 else (pb/tot,ph/tot,ps/tot)
    out={"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]; out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]; out[f"S_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out
def apply_veto_m5(agg,reasons):
    pb,ps=agg["pb"],agg["ps"]
    pb30,pb15=agg.get("pb_30m",0.0),agg.get("pb_15m",0.0)
    ps30,ps15=agg.get("ps_30m",0.0),agg.get("ps_15m",0.0)
    S5=agg.get("S_5m",0.0)
    bull_ok=(pb>=P_ENTER) and (pb30>=0.55) and (pb15>=0.55) and (S5>=0.0)
    bear_ok=(ps>=P_ENTER) and (ps30>=0.55) and (ps15>=0.55) and (S5<=0.0)
    if pb>=P_ENTER and not bull_ok: reasons.append("veto5_buy"); agg["pb"]=max(agg["pb"],P_EXIT-1e-6)
    if ps>=P_ENTER and not bear_ok: reasons.append("veto5_sell"); agg["ps"]=max(agg["ps"],P_EXIT-1e-6)
    tot=agg["pb"]+agg["ph"]+agg["ps"]
    if tot>0: agg["pb"],agg["ph"],agg["ps"]=agg["pb"]/tot,agg["ph"]/tot,agg["ps"]/tot
    return agg
@dataclass
class CtxState:
    ctx:str="none"; streak_ctx:str="none"; streak:int=0; bars_in_ctx:int=0
def decide_next_ctx(prob,prev_ctx,reasons):
    pb,ph,ps=prob["pb"],prob["ph"],prob["ps"]
    buy_ok=(pb>=P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="buy" and pb>=P_EXIT)
    sell_ok=(ps>=P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="sell" and ps>=P_EXIT)
    range_ok=(RANGE_LOW<=ph<=RANGE_HIGH)
    if buy_ok and pb>=ps and pb>=ph: reasons.append("enter_buy" if pb>=P_ENTER else "hold_buy"); return "buy"
    if sell_ok and ps>=pb and ps>=ph: reasons.append("enter_sell" if ps>=P_ENTER else "hold_sell"); return "sell"
    if range_ok: reasons.append("range_band"); return "hold"
    reasons.append("under_thresholds"); return "none"
def update_context(state,prob,reasons,bar_closed=True):
    target=decide_next_ctx(prob,state.ctx,reasons)
    if target==state.ctx:
        if state.streak>=PERSIST_BARS: reasons.append("persistence_ok")
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx,streak_ctx=target,streak=min(state.streak+1,PERSIST_BARS),bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx+(1 if bar_closed else 0))
    streak=state.streak+1 if target==state.streak_ctx else 1
    if streak>=PERSIST_BARS:
        reasons.append("persistence_ok")
        return CtxState(ctx=target,streak_ctx=target,streak=streak,bars_in_ctx=1 if bar_closed else 0)
    else:
        reasons.append("persistence_wait")
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx,streak_ctx=target,streak=streak,bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx+(1 if bar_closed else 0))
def compute_ctx(per_tf_inputs,prev_state):
    per_tf={tf:score_tf(per_tf_inputs[tf],tf) for tf in per_tf_inputs}
    agg=aggregate_probs(per_tf)
    reasons=[]
    for tf in per_tf: reasons+=per_tf[tf].get("reasons",[])
    agg=apply_veto_m5(agg,reasons)
    new_state=update_context(prev_state,agg,reasons,bar_closed=True)
    ints={k:int(round(10*agg[k])) for k in ("pb","ph","ps")}
    return {"pb":agg["pb"],"ph":agg["ph"],"ps":agg["ps"],"Sw":agg["Sw"],"ctx_state":new_state,"ints":ints,"per_tf":per_tf,"agg":agg,"reasons":reasons[:8]}
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/dashboard_live.sh
Size: 527
MTime: 2025-09-25 12:53:36.191336189 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=/opt/scalp/data

    python3 /opt/scalp/tools/show_dashboard.py || true
    prev="$cur"

  sleep 2

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, sys
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"

TF_CFG = {"5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}
SAFETY_LAG = 5        # secondes post close avant d'accepter la bougie
MAX_PER_SYMBOL = 400  # profondeur locale max par TF

def now_s(): return int(time.time())
def read_json(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def bitget():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "enableRateLimit": True,
        "options": {"defaultType": "swap"},
    })

def tf_to_ccxt(tf): return tf   # ccxt accepte '5m','15m','30m'

def fp(symbol, tf): 
    return CAND/f"{tf}/{symbol}.json"

def load_local(symbol, tf):
    p = fp(symbol, tf)
    if not p.exists(): return []
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return []

def save_local(symbol, tf, arr):
    p = fp(symbol, tf)
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr, separators=(",",":")))

def last_ts(arr): 
    return 0 if not arr else int(arr[-1][0])//1000

def aligned_floor(ts, step):  # floor(ts to step)
    return (ts//step)*step

def fetch_append(ex, symbol, tf, limit_keep):
    step = TF_CFG[tf]
    local = load_local(symbol, tf)
    last = last_ts(local)

    # on ne demande une nouvelle bougie QUE si la bougie vient d’être close + SAFETY_LAG
    t = now_s()
    last_close = aligned_floor(t, step)
    if t < last_close + SAFETY_LAG:
        # dernière bougie pas encore «finalisée» : on ne touche à rien
        return local, False

    # since : on repart un peu avant la dernière pour éviter trous
    since = (last - 3*step) * 1000 if last else (t - limit_keep*step)*1000
    try:
        ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(symbol, tf_to_ccxt(tf), since=since, limit=limit_keep+10)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[fetch] {symbol} {tf} error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        return local, False

    # dédoublonnage (ts croissants, millis)
    merged = {int(a[0]):a for a in local}
    for a in ohlcv:
        merged[int(a[0])] = a
    out = [merged[k] for k in sorted(merged.keys())]
    # bornage mémoire (MAX_PER_SYMBOL)
    out = out[-MAX_PER_SYMBOL:]

    # validité : ne garder que bougies <= last_close (donc closes)
    out = [a for a in out if int(a[0])//1000 <= last_close]

    changed = (len(out) != len(local)) or (last_ts(out) != last)
    if changed:
        save_local(symbol, tf, out)
    return out, changed

def main():
    top = read_json(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms = top.get("symbols", [])
    if not syms:
        print("top.json vide, skip"); return 0

    ex = bitget()
    ok=skip=err=0
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        for s in syms:
            try:
                _, changed = fetch_append(ex, s, tf, MAX_PER_SYMBOL)
                ok += 1 if changed else 0
                skip += 0 if changed else 1
            except Exception as e:
                err += 1
                print(f"[{s} {tf}] EXC {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    print(json.dumps({"ok":ok,"skip":skip,"err":err,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}))
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
from b_logic import jload, jsave, last_complete, analyze_symbol, DATA, CAND

TOP = jload(DATA/"top.json", {"symbols":[]}).get("symbols", [])[:30]
A = jload(DATA/"analyse_A_out.json", {"results":[]})
if isinstance(A, list): A={"results":A}
ctxA = { r.get("symbol",""): (r.get("ctx") or "none") for r in A.get("results",[]) }

out=[]; signals=[]
for sym in TOP:
    m1 = last_complete(jload(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json", []), 60)
    m3 = last_complete(jload(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json", []), 180)
    m5 = last_complete(jload(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json", []), 300)
    if len(m1)<50 or len(m3)<50 or len(m5)<50:
        out.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":"none","score":0.0,"why":"insufficient"})
        continue
    res = analyze_symbol(sym, ctxA.get(sym,"none"), m1, m3, m5, balance=jload(DATA/"balance.json", {"balance":200}).get("balance",200))
    out.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":res.get("ctx","none"),"score":res.get("score",0.0)})
    if res.get("signal"):
        signals.append(res["signal"])

# write analyse_B_out.json
jsave(DATA/"analyse_B_out.json", {"generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()), "results": out})

# append signals
if signals:
    sigf = DATA/"signals.json"
    arr = jload(sigf, [])
    if not isinstance(arr,list): arr=[]
    arr.extend(signals)
    jsave(sigf, arr)

print(json.dumps({"n":len(out), "signals":len(signals)}))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, hmac, hashlib, base64, requests

BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"

def sign(message: str, secret: str) -> str:
    return base64.b64encode(
        hmac.new(secret.encode(), message.encode(), hashlib.sha256).digest()
    ).decode()

def auth_headers(path: str, method="GET", body="") -> dict:
    api_key     = os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY")
    api_secret  = os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET")
    passphrase  = os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE")
    ts          = str(int(time.time() * 1000))
    prehash     = ts + method.upper() + path + body
    sig         = sign(prehash, api_secret)
    return {
        "ACCESS-KEY": api_key,
        "ACCESS-SIGN": sig,
        "ACCESS-TIMESTAMP": ts,
        "ACCESS-PASSPHRASE": passphrase,
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def main():
    # --- public check (no auth needed) ---
    r = requests.get(BASE + "/api/v2/mix/market/contracts", params={"productType":"usdt-futures"})
    print("[PUBLIC]", r.status_code, r.text[:200])

    # --- private check (auth required) ---
    path = "/api/v2/user/fee/query"
    url  = BASE + path
    r = requests.get(url, headers=auth_headers(path))
    print("[PRIVATE]", r.status_code, r.text[:200])

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import requests

BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"

def get_ohlcv(symbol="BTCUSDT_UMCBL", granularity="1day", limit=5):
    """
    Récupère les bougies OHLCV pour un symbole donné
    granularity: "1min", "5min", "15min", "1hour", "4hour", "1day", "1week"
    limit: nombre de bougies à récupérer
    """
    path = "/api/v2/mix/market/candles"
    params = {
        "symbol": symbol,
        "granularity": granularity,
        "limit": limit
    }
    try:
        r = requests.get(BASE + path, params=params, timeout=10)
        r.raise_for_status()
        return r.status_code, r.json()
    except Exception as e:
        return 500, {"error": str(e)}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    code, data = get_ohlcv()
    print("[OHLCV]", code)
    print(data)

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

PY=$(command -v python3)

/usr/bin/env ${PY} - <<'PY'
import os, time, ccxt, math
ex=ccxt.bitget({
  "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
  "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
  "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
  "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
  "enableRateLimit": True,
})
# temps serveur Bitget en ms
srv_ms = ex.milliseconds()
loc_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
offset = srv_ms - loc_ms  # positif si serveur "en avance"
# calcul du prochain top de minute côté serveur
next_min = ((srv_ms//60000)+1)*60000
sleep_ms = (next_min - srv_ms) + 800  # +0.8s de marge
if sleep_ms>0:
    time.sleep(sleep_ms/1000.0)
print(f"[sync] offset_ms={offset} slept_ms={sleep_ms}")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG="/opt/scalp/logs/priority_runner.log"; mkdir -p /opt/scalp/logs
now_s=$(date +%s)

jget_ts() {
  # lit .generated_at sinon mtime
  local f="$1" ; local ttl="$2"
  if [ ! -s "$f" ]; then echo "0"; return; fi
  if command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local ts
    ts=$(jq -r '.generated_at // empty' "$f" 2>/dev/null || true)
    if [ -n "$ts" ]; then date -d "$ts" +%s 2>/dev/null || echo "0"; return; fi
  fi
  stat -c %Y "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "0"
}

fresh() {
  # fresh <file> <ttl_seconds>
  local f="$1" ttl="$2"
  local ft; ft=$(jget_ts "$f" "$ttl")
  [ "$ft" -gt 0 ] && [ $(( now_s - ft )) -lt "$ttl" ]
}

echo "$(date -Is) tick:start" >>"$LOG"

# TTL
TTL_COINS90=$((48*3600))
TTL_TOP=$((2*3600))
TTL_A=$((5*60))

F_COINS="/opt/scalp/data/coins_90d.json"
F_TOP="/opt/scalp/data/top.json"
F_A="/opt/scalp/data/analyse_A_out.json"

# 1) Univers USDT >=90j (48h)
if ! fresh "$F_COINS" "$TTL_COINS90"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh coins_90d" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_contracts_usdt_ccxt.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 2) Top (2h)
if ! fresh "$F_TOP" "$TTL_TOP"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh OHLCV only (top.json protected)" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_top.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 3) Analyse A (5min) -> ne rafraîchit TF que si A expiré
if ! fresh "$F_A" "$TTL_A"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh A (TF 30/15/5 + A)" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_guard.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 4) Analyse B chaque minute, sync 1m (coins ctx != none) puis B
/opt/scalp/tools/run_b_synced.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_guard.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true

echo "$(date -Is) tick:end" >>"$LOG"

Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/run_analysis_a_coin.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, argparse, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CBASE=DATA/"candles"
OUT =DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
STATE=Path("/opt/scalp/run/a_state.json")

# Tuning
W_EMA,W_MACD,W_RSI,W_ADX,W_OBV = 0.35,0.25,0.20,0.10,0.10
TAU = {"30m":0.35,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.25}
ALPHA={"30m":0.5,"15m":0.3,"5m":0.2}
ATR_GATE={"30m":0.0025,"15m":0.0018,"5m":0.0012}

def ema(x,n):
    if not x: return []
    k=2/(n+1); o=[x[0]]
    for v in x[1:]: o.append(o[-1]+k*(v-o[-1]))
    return o
def stdev(x):
    if len(x)<2: return 0.0
    mu=sum(x)/len(x)
    return (sum((v-mu)**2 for v in x)/len(x))**0.5
def atr(h,l,c,n=14):
    trs=[]; prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        trs.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-prev), abs(l[i]-prev))); prev=c[i]
    return ema(trs,n)
def macd_hist(c, fast=12, slow=26, sig=9):
    m=[a-b for a,b in zip(ema(c,fast), ema(c,slow))]
    s=ema(m,sig); n=min(len(m),len(s))
    return [m[-n+i]-s[-n+i] for i in range(n)]
def rsi(c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(c)
    g=[0.0]; d=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        ch=c[i]-c[i-1]; g.append(max(ch,0.0)); d.append(max(-ch,0.0))
    ag=ema(g,n); ad=ema(d,n)
    out=[]
    for x,y in zip(ag,ad):
        rs=x/(y+1e-12); out.append(100-100/(1+rs))
    return out
def adx(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(c)
    pd=[0.0]; md=[0.0]; TR=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        up=h[i]-h[i-1]; dn=l[i-1]-l[i]
        pd.append(up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0)
        md.append(dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0)
        TR.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
    pdi=[100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(pd,n), ema(TR,n))]
    mdi=[100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(md,n), ema(TR,n))]
    DX=[100*abs(a-b)/(a+b+1e-12) for a,b in zip(pdi,mdi)]
    return ema(DX,n)
def obv(c,v):
    o=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        o.append(o[-1] + (v[i] if c[i]>c[i-1] else (-v[i] if c[i]<c[i-1] else 0.0)))
    return o

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    p=CBASE/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    j=json.loads(p.read_text())
    k=j["data"]
    if len(k)<500: raise RuntimeError(f"{sym} {tf} <500 bars")
    # colonnes
    o=[r[1] for r in k]; h=[r[2] for r in k]; l=[r[3] for r in k]; c=[r[4] for r in k]; v=[r[5] for r in k]
    return o,h,l,c,v,k[-1][0]

def subscores_tf(o,h,l,c,v, tf):
    # EMA spread / ATR gate
    atr14 = atr(h,l,c,14)[-1]
    base = max(1.5*atr14,1e-9)
    s_ema = math.tanh( (ema(c,12)[-1] - ema(c,26)[-1]) / base )

    # MACD hist / sigma100
    hist = macd_hist(c)
    sigma = stdev(hist[-100:]) if len(hist)>=100 else stdev(hist)
    s_macd = math.tanh( (hist[-1])/(sigma+1e-12) )

    # RSI
    s_rsi = max(-1.0,min(1.0,(rsi(c,14)[-1]-50.0)/50.0))

    # ADX
    s_adx = max(-1.0,min(1.0,(adx(h,l,c,14)[-1]-20.0)/20.0))

    # OBV slope(20)/median(|OBV|_200)
    ob = obv(c,v)
    slope = ob[-1]-ob[-21] if len(ob)>=21 else 0.0
    denom = stats.median([abs(x) for x in (ob[-200:] if len(ob)>=200 else ob)]) or 1.0
    s_obv = math.tanh(slope/denom)

    # ATR% gate
    gate = (atr14 / c[-1]) < ATR_GATE[tf]
    w_ema = W_EMA*0.5 if gate else W_EMA
    w_macd= W_MACD*0.5 if gate else W_MACD
    num = w_ema*s_ema + w_macd*s_macd + W_RSI*s_rsi + W_ADX*s_adx + W_OBV*s_obv
    den = (w_ema + w_macd + W_RSI + W_ADX + W_OBV)
    S = num/den if den>0 else 0.0

    # Softmax tri-state
    t=TAU[tf]
    epos=math.exp(S/t); eneg=math.exp(-S/t); den3=epos+1+eneg
    pb=epos/den3; ph=1/den3; ps=eneg/den3

    return {"S":S,"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"atrpct":atr14/c[-1]}

def persist(symbol, candidate, bar_ts):
    try: st=json.loads(STATE.read_text() or "{}")
    except: st={}
    rec=st.get(symbol, {"last":"none","streak":0,"ts":0})
    if candidate!="none":
        if rec["last"]==candidate and rec.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            rec["streak"]=min(2, rec.get("streak",0)+1)
        else:
            rec["streak"]=1
        rec["last"]=candidate; rec["ts"]=bar_ts
    else:
        if rec.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            rec={"last":"none","streak":0,"ts":bar_ts}
    st[symbol]=rec
    STATE.write_text(json.dumps(st))
    return candidate if rec["streak"]>=2 else "none"

def decide_context(pb,ph,ps,res):
    bull = pb>=0.60 and (res["30m"]["pb"]>=0.55) and (res["15m"]["pb"]>=0.55)
    bear = ps>=0.60 and (res["30m"]["ps"]>=0.55) and (res["15m"]["ps"]>=0.55)
    veto_buy = res["5m"]["S"]<0
    veto_sell= res["5m"]["S"]>0
    if bull and not veto_buy: return "buy"
    if bear and not veto_sell: return "sell"
    if 0.40 <= res["30m"]["ph"] <= 0.60: return "hold"
    return "none"

def upsert_out(rec):
    try: arr=json.loads(OUT.read_text() or "[]")
    except: arr=[]
    m={r["symbol"]:i for i,r in enumerate(arr) if isinstance(r,dict) and "symbol" in r}
    if rec["symbol"] in m:
        arr[m[rec["symbol"]]]=rec
    else:
        arr.append(rec)
    OUT.write_text(json.dumps(arr, indent=2))

def main():
    ap=argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--symbol", required=True)
    a=ap.parse_args()
    sym=a.symbol

    # load TFs
    o30,h30,l30,c30,v30,ts30 = load_tf(sym,"30m")
    o15,h15,l15,c15,v15,ts15 = load_tf(sym,"15m")
    o5 ,h5 ,l5 ,c5 ,v5 ,ts5  = load_tf(sym,"5m")

    r30=subscores_tf(o30,h30,l30,c30,v30,"30m")
    r15=subscores_tf(o15,h15,l15,c15,v15,"15m")
    r5 =subscores_tf(o5 ,h5 ,l5 ,c5 ,v5 ,"5m")

    # agrégation
    S = ALPHA["30m"]*r30["S"] + ALPHA["15m"]*r15["S"] + ALPHA["5m"]*r5["S"]
    pb= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["pb"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["pb"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["pb"]
    ph= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["ph"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["ph"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["ph"]
    ps= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["ps"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["ps"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["ps"]
    s=pb+ph+ps; 
    if s>0: pb,ph,ps = pb/s, ph/s, ps/s

    ctx_cand=decide_context(pb,ph,ps, {"30m":r30,"15m":r15,"5m":r5})
    ctx = persist(sym, ctx_cand, ts5)

    rec={"symbol":sym,"S":round(S,6),"pb":round(pb,6),"ph":round(ph,6),"ps":round(ps,6),
         "context":ctx,"ts":int(ts5//1000)}
    upsert_out(rec)
    print(f"[A-coin] {sym} ctx={ctx} S={rec['S']}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

# Params
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"; N=int(os.getenv("TOP_N","30"))
BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}
MIN_QV=float(os.getenv("MIN_QV","1000000"))  # 1M
MAX_SP=float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS","50"))   # 0.5%
FUT={"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"

# noyau fixe lu de top.json existant, sinon BTC/ETH/SOL/XRP/BNB
def load_seed():
    if TOP.exists():
        try:
            j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
            return [x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
        except: pass
    return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    # Univers futures USDT
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # Tickers bulk (fallback par symbole si besoin)
    tickers={}
    try: tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    # Préfiltre rapide
    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): continue
        if b in BAD_BASES: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        qv=float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        bid,ask=t.get("bid"),t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: continue
        mid=0.5*(bid+ask); sp_bps=10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid
        if qv<MIN_QV or sp_bps>MAX_SP: continue
        pool.append((s,qv,sp_bps))

    # Tri volume desc et complétion
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    for s,qv,sp in pool:
        flat=s.replace("/","")
        if flat in seed_set: 
            details.append({"symbol":flat,"score":1.0,"volume24h_quote":qv,"spread_bps":sp})
            continue
        out.append(flat); seed_set.add(flat)
        details.append({"symbol":flat,"score":0.0,"volume24h_quote":qv,"spread_bps":sp})
        if len(out)>=N: break

    # Écritures
    meta={"generated_at":now_iso(),"source":"futures-tickers-fast","exchange":EX,"quote":QUOTE}
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({**meta,"symbols":out[:N]}, indent=2))
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": meta["generated_at"],
        "n": len(out[:N]),
        "items": details[:N]
    }, indent=2))
    print(f"[expand] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} top={len(out[:N])}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()
